# math.NA [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [PriorIDENT: Prior-Informed PDE Identification from Noisy Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05946)
*Cheng Tang,Hao Liu,Dong Wang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种先验信息弱形式稀疏回归框架，通过物理先验约束和弱形式处理，从噪声时空数据中稳健识别偏微分方程（PDEs）。该方法在多种典型系统中优于无先验基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从噪声时空数据中识别控制偏微分方程面临两大挑战：微分操作导致的噪声放大，以及过完备库（overcomplete libraries）带来的模糊性。现有方法需要同时解决这两个问题。

Method: 提出先验信息弱形式稀疏回归框架（prior-informed weak-form sparse-regression framework），包含三个紧凑物理先验：哈密顿先验（Hamiltonian，斜梯度和能量守恒）、守恒律先验（conservation-law，通量形式且共享交叉方向系数）和能量最小化先验（energy-minimization，变分耗散）。结合子空间追踪流程（subspace-pursuit pipeline），通过修剪和残差缩减模型选择获得简约可解释模型。

Result: 在多种典型系统（包括哈密顿振荡器和三体问题、粘性Burgers方程和二维浅水方程、扩散和Allen-Cahn动力学）中，该方法实现了更高的真阳性率、稳定的系数恢复，以及在显著噪声下保持结构保持动力学。在强形式和弱形式设置中均持续优于无先验基线。

Conclusion: 紧凑结构先验与弱形式相结合，为从噪声数据中进行物理忠实的偏微分方程识别提供了稳健且统一的途径。该方法在噪声环境下表现出优越的性能和物理一致性。

Abstract: Identifying governing partial differential equations (PDEs) from noisy spatiotemporal data remains challenging due to differentiation-induced noise amplification and ambiguity from overcomplete libraries. We propose a prior-informed weak-form sparse-regression framework that resolves both issues by refining the dictionary before regression and shifting derivatives onto smooth test functions. Our design encodes three compact physics priors-Hamiltonian (skew-gradient and energy-conserving), conservation-law (flux-form with shared cross-directional coefficients), and energy-minimization (variational, dissipative)-so that all candidate features are physically admissible by construction. These prior-consistent libraries are coupled with a subspace-pursuit pipeline enhanced by trimming and residual-reduction model selection to yield parsimonious, interpretable models. Across canonical systems-including Hamiltonian oscillators and the three-body problem, viscous Burgers and two-dimensional shallow-water equations, and diffusion and Allen--Cahn dynamics-our method achieves higher true-positive rates, stable coefficient recovery, and structure-preserving dynamics under substantial noise, consistently outperforming no-prior baselines in both strong- and weak-form settings. The results demonstrate that compact structural priors, when combined with weak formulations, provide a robust and unified route to physically faithful PDE identification from noisy data.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Quantum Diffusion Models: Score Reversal Is Not Free in Gaussian Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06488)
*Ammar Fayad*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 基于扩散的生成建模通过添加分数漂移来反转噪声半群。对于连续变量高斯马尔可夫动力学，完全正性在生成器层面耦合了漂移和扩散。量子限制衰减器（quantum-limited attenuator）的固定扩散Wigner分数反向漂移在特定条件下违反CP，任何高斯CP修复都必须注入额外扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在分析基于扩散的生成建模（diffusion-based generative modeling）中反向噪声半群（reversing a noising semigroup）的完全正性（complete positivity, CP）约束。特别关注连续变量高斯马尔可夫动力学（continuous-variable Gaussian Markov dynamics）中漂移和扩散的耦合关系。

Method: 研究采用量子限制衰减器（quantum-limited attenuator）作为分析模型，包含热参数ν和压缩参数r。通过分析固定扩散Wigner分数（Bayes）反向漂移（fixed-diffusion Wigner-score reverse drift）的CP条件，探讨高斯CP修复（Gaussian CP repair）的必要性。

Result: 研究发现，当cosh(2r)>ν时，固定扩散Wigner分数反向漂移违反完全正性（violates CP）。任何高斯完全正性修复都必须注入额外扩散（inject extra diffusion），导致保真度（fidelity）下界由几何常数c_geom和最坏情况互信息I_dec^wc决定。

Conclusion: 在量子扩散生成建模中，完全正性约束强制要求额外扩散注入，这建立了生成模型保真度与信息论量之间的基本关系。该结果揭示了量子系统中反向噪声过程的物理约束条件。

Abstract: Diffusion-based generative modeling suggests reversing a noising semigroup by adding a score drift. For continuous-variable Gaussian Markov dynamics, complete positivity couples drift and diffusion at the generator level. For a quantum-limited attenuator with thermal parameter $ν$ and squeezing $r$, the fixed-diffusion Wigner-score (Bayes) reverse drift violates CP iff $\cosh(2r)>ν$. Any Gaussian CP repair must inject extra diffusion, implying $-2\ln F\ge c_{\text{geom}}(ν_{\min})I_{\mathrm{dec}}^{\mathrm{wc}}$.

</details>


### [3] [Classical Simulability from Operator Entanglement Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05656)
*Neil Dowling*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了局域算符纠缠（LOE）与矩阵乘积算符（MPO）可模拟性之间的严格联系，证明LOE的标度行为决定了量子多体系统是否可用经典张量网络有效模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域算符纠缠（local-operator entanglement, LOE）量化了海森堡算符的非局域结构，可作为多体混沌（many-body chaos）的诊断工具。研究旨在建立LOE与矩阵乘积算符（matrix-product operator, MPO）可模拟性之间的严格理论联系。

Method: 通过严格的数学界限证明，分析LOE的α-Rényi熵的渐近标度行为。对于α≥1的情况，证明体积律标度（volume law scaling）导致MPO无法有效近似；对于α<1的情况，证明对数标度（logarithmic scaling）保证MPO可模拟性。同时提供数值证据和随机矩阵模型支持。

Result: 当α≥1的LOE呈现体积律标度时，算符无法用MPO有效近似；而当α<1的LOE呈现对数标度时，算符可用MPO模拟。这一结果适用于无限温度自关联函数、时序无序关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlators）以及计算基态系综的平均期望值。

Conclusion: 研究为"低算符纠缠意味着张量网络可有效表示"的启发式期望提供了严格理论基础，扩展了矩阵乘积态理论的基础结果，并在量子混沌与经典可模拟性之间建立了形式联系。

Abstract: Local-operator entanglement (LOE) quantifies the nonlocal structure of Heisenberg operators and serves as a diagnostic of many-body chaos. We provide rigorous bounds showing when an operator can be well-approximated by a matrix-product operator (MPO), given asymptotic scaling of its LOE $α$-Rényi entropies. Specifically, we prove that a volume law scaling for $α\geq 1$ implies that the operator cannot be approximated efficiently as an MPO while faithfully reproducing all expectation values. On the other hand, if we restrict to correlations over a relevant sub-class of (ensembles of) states, then logarithmic scaling of the $α< 1$ Rényi LOE entropies implies MPO simulability. This result covers a range of relevant quantities, including infinite temperature autocorrelation functions, out-of-time-ordered correlators, and average-case expectation values over ensembles of computational basis states. Beyond this regime, we provide numerical evidence together with a random matrix model to argue that, also for out-of-equilibrium expectation values, logarithmic scaling for $α< 1$ Rényi LOE typically guarantees simulability. Our results put on firm footing the heuristic expectation that a low operator entanglement implies efficient tensor network representability, extending celebrated foundational results from the theory of matrix-product states and providing a formal link between quantum chaos and classical simulability.

</details>


### [4] [Significant modifications of Lamb shift at small centripetal accelerations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05945)
*Yan Peng,Jiawei Hu,Hongwei Yu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 研究向心加速原子与电磁真空涨落耦合时的兰姆位移（Lamb shift）。发现即使加速度极小，旋转运动也会导致各向异性的能级移动，其特性取决于原子极化方向与旋转轴的相对取向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究向心加速（centripetally accelerated）原子与电磁真空涨落（electromagnetic vacuum fluctuations）耦合时的兰姆位移，探索非惯性运动对量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）效应的修正。

Method: 聚焦于极小的轨道半径（orbital radius）情况，使切向速度保持非相对论性（nonrelativistic）而向心加速度极小，分析原子极化方向（polarization direction）与旋转轴（rotation axis）不同相对取向时的兰姆位移。

Result: 兰姆位移呈现显著的各向异性（anisotropic）：沿旋转轴极化的原子，非惯性修正仅出现在半径的二阶项，能级间距可能略微减小或增大；垂直旋转轴极化的原子，非惯性修正出现在半径的领头阶，总是增大能级间距。当角速度（angular velocity）远大于跃迁频率（transition frequency）时，旋转诱导的修正可与惯性兰姆位移量级相当。

Conclusion: 即使在极小的向心加速度下，圆周运动（circular motion）也能显著改变兰姆位移，且修正具有强烈的各向异性，对原子极化方向高度敏感。这表明非惯性效应在量子电动力学现象中可能扮演重要角色。

Abstract: We investigate the Lamb shift of centripetally accelerated atoms coupled to electromagnetic vacuum fluctuations. Focusing on a very small orbital radius (so that the tangential speed remains nonrelativistic and the proper centripetal acceleration can be extremely small), we show that the resulting level shift is intrinsically anisotropic and depends sensitively on the atomic polarization direction. For atoms polarizable along the rotation axis, the leading noninertial contribution enters only at second order in the orbital radius and can slightly decrease or increase the energy-level spacing, depending on the angular-velocity regime. In contrast, for atoms polarizable perpendicular to the rotation axis, the noninertial contribution appears already at the leading order in the radius and always increases the energy-level spacing. Remarkably, when the angular velocity greatly exceeds the transition frequency, the rotation-induced correction can become comparable in magnitude to the inertial Lamb shift, indicating that circular motion can significantly modify the Lamb shift even in the regime of very small centripetal accelerations.

</details>


### [5] [Ramsey correlation spectroscopy with phase cycling using a single quantum sensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05650)
*Inbar Zohar,Santiago Oviedo-Casado,Andrej Denisenko,Rainer Stöhr,Amit Finkler*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: RESOLUTE协议通过将拉姆齐测量与关联光谱学相结合，克服了量子传感器在低频信号检测中的局限性，将有效相干时间从0.38μs延长至5.1μs，实现了在1/T₁至1/T₂ᵖ范围内先前无法访问的频谱区域检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度磁光谱学（magnetic spectroscopy）为材料性质和动力学提供了独特见解，但低频信号检测面临挑战。由于有限相干时间（T₂*），振荡频率低于1/T₂*的信号在积累足够相位前就已衰减，限制了氮空位（nitrogen-vacancy, NV）中心等量子传感器的低频探测能力。

Method: 提出RESOLUTE协议，结合拉姆齐测量（Ramsey measurements）与关联光谱学（correlation spectroscopy）。该协议在两个传感周期之间的关联周期（T_corr < T₁）内，将累积相位存储为布居数不平衡，从而产生大于T₂*的有效相干时间T₂ᵖ。通过整合绝热脉冲（adiabatic pulses）和相位循环（phase cycling），实现了稳健的自旋控制和有效的直流信号提取。

Result: 实验证明有效相干时间从T₂* = 0.38μs延长至T₂ᵖ = 5.1μs，超越了哈恩回波（Hahn Echo）测量。该技术成功在低至49G（约50kHz）的磁场下检测到¹³C核自旋拉莫尔进动（Larmor precession）。使用费舍尔信息（Fisher information）的理论分析进一步表征了RESOLUTE在频率估计能力方面的优势。

Conclusion: RESOLUTE协议通过将频率匹配条件转移到关联时间，实现了在1/T₁至1/T₂ᵖ频谱区域的检测突破。这些进展增强了对弱偶极相互作用的灵敏度，对单分子成像（single-molecule imaging）和量子传感应用至关重要。

Abstract: Magnetic spectroscopy at the nanoscale provides unique insights into material properties and dynamics, with quantum sensors like nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers being ideally suited for these scales. However, detecting low-frequency signals remains a challenge due to finite coherence times ($T_2^*$), as signals oscillating slower than $1/T_2^*$ decay before sufficient phase accumulation occurs. We present RESOLUTE (Ramsey corrElation SpectroscOpy puLse seqUence wiTh phasE cycling), a protocol that overcomes these limitations by combining Ramsey measurements with correlation spectroscopy. By storing accumulated phase as a population imbalance during a correlation period ($T_\mathrm{corr} < T_1$) between two sensing periods, RESOLUTE generates an effective coherence time $T_2^p > T_2^*$. This shifts the frequency-matching condition to the correlation time, enabling detection in the previously inaccessible spectral region between $1/T_1$ and $1/T_2^p$. We experimentally demonstrate an extension of the effective coherence time from $T_2^* = 0.38\,μs$ to $T_2^p = 5.1\,μs$, surpassing Hahn Echo measurements. The technique successfully detects $^{13}$C nuclear spin Larmor precession at fields as low as 49$\,$G ($\sim$50$\,$kHz). We further provide theoretical insight using Fisher information to characterize RESOLUTE's frequency estimation capabilities compared to existing protocols. Finally, by integrating adiabatic pulses and phase cycling, we demonstrate robust spin control and effective DC signal extraction. These advancements provide enhanced sensitivity to weak dipolar interactions, essential for single-molecule imaging and quantum sensing applications.

</details>


### [6] [Thermodynamics of Quantum Coupled Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06336)
*Shuvadip Ghosh,Arnab Ghosh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该综述从热力学角度分析纳米尺度系统中的量子耦合输运过程，以熵产生率为核心框架，探讨了量子点系统中的基本输运、耦合输运现象，以及逆电流等非平衡热力学效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在从热力学视角审视纳米尺度系统中的量子耦合输运过程。虽然热力学定律在经典和量子领域具有普适性，但研究特别关注开放量子系统框架下的微观机制，尤其是与电子库耦合的量子点系统。

Method: 分析基于熵产生率框架，通过共轭力-流对表达非平衡过程。研究首先考察基本单输运过程，然后扩展到耦合输运，使用最小化的双端单量子点设置分析耦合的能量和粒子输运，并扩展到三端耦合量子点几何结构。

Result: 研究表明传统热电现象（包括塞贝克效应、佩尔捷效应以及热电热机和制冷机）作为热力学交叉效应自然涌现。在耦合量子点系统中，发现了逆电流现象，即电流在相互平行的热力学力作用下反向流动而不违反第二定律，这需要打破能量和粒子输运之间的对称性。

Conclusion: 熵产生率框架为理解纳米尺度系统中的量子耦合输运提供了统一的热力学视角。三端耦合量子点几何结构为研究耦合输运提供了多功能平台，而逆电流现象展示了耦合输运中超越标准交叉效应的丰富热力学行为。

Abstract: This review presents a thermodynamic perspective on quantum coupled transport processes in nanoscale systems. Our analysis is formulated within the framework of entropy production rate, the central quantity governing non-equilibrium processes and expressed through conjugate force-flux pairs. Although thermodynamic laws are universal across classical and quantum domains, the discussion is developed within a microscopic open quantum system framework, focusing on quantum dots (QDs) coupled to electronic reservoirs. We first examine elementary single transport processes and highlight their strong thermodynamic constraints in the near-equilibrium regime. This motivates the study of coupled transport, where multiple force-flux pairs coexist and interact, leading to richer thermodynamic behaviour. Using entropy production as the guiding principle, we analyse coupled energy and particle transport in a minimal two-terminal single-QD setup and show how conventional thermoelectric phenomena, including Seebeck and Peltier effects as well as thermoelectric heat engines and refrigerators, naturally emerge as thermodynamic cross-effects. We then extend the framework to a three-terminal coupled quantum dot (CQD) geometry, which provides a versatile platform for studying coupled transport and reduces, under suitable constraints, to the well-known Sánchez-Büttiker configuration. Beyond standard cross-effects, we discuss the phenomenon of inverse currents in coupled transport (ICC), where a current flows against mutually parallel thermodynamic forces without violating the second law. We show that ICC requires breaking the symmetry between energy and particle transport and identify the conditions for its realization in coupled quantum-dot systems with attractive interdot interactions.

</details>


### [7] [Methods for characterization of atomic-scale field emission point-electron-source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06499)
*Shuai Tang,Mingkai Gou,Yingzhou Hu,Jie Tang,Yan Shen,Yu Zhang,Lu-chang Qin,Ningsheng Xu,Richard G. Forbes,Shaozhi Deng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于场离子显微镜-场电子显微镜（FIM-FEM）的实验方法，用于测量场发射（FE）电子源的视在发射面积，解决了现有理论分析方法在原子尺度冷阴极表征中的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 场发射电子源需要接近原子尺度以实现高空间分辨率和稳定发射，但目前缺乏统一的实验方法来提取视在发射面积（apparent emission area），而该参数对预测束流特性至关重要。现有基于Fowler-Nordheim（FN）理论的简化分析方法存在物理局限性。

Method: 论文报道了一种基于场离子显微镜和场电子显微镜（FIM-FEM）的实验方法，用于确定场发射电子源的视在发射面积。该方法不依赖于传统的基于绘图的数据分析方法，特别适用于原子尺度冷阴极的表征。

Result: FIM-FEM方法与基于Murphy-Good（MG）理论分析得到的发射面积差异因子为7.4，而与简化FN理论分析的差异约为25，证实了MG理论在场发射数据分析中的优越性。该方法可推导出源能量展宽、降低亮度和发射效率等关键指标。

Conclusion: 该研究为表征场发射电子源，特别是原子尺度冷阴极，提供了一种新的实验方法，并提供了可下载程序辅助分析。现有基于绘图的数据分析方法不适用于这类先进电子源的表征需求。

Abstract: Field emission (FE) electron sources are made close to atomic-scale to reach the highest spatial resolution as well as stable emission for electron microscopy, electron beam inspection and lithography. At present, no single agreed method exists of using FE current-voltage data to extract the apparent emission area, which is needed for predicting some beam properties. The 1956 theory of Murphy and Good (MG) is better physics than the 1920s theory of Fowler and Nordheim (FN) and colleagues, but many researchers use simplified FN theory to analyse experimental data. The present paper reports an experimental method of finding apparent emission area, based on using field ion and field electron microscopes (FIM-FEM). The discrepancy of emission area between the FIM-FEM method and MG-based analysis is a factor of 7.4, while that with simplified FN-based analysis is about 25, confirming MG theory is better for FE data analysis. The result allows deduction of key indicators, including source energy spread, reduced brightness and emission efficiency. A downloadable program is made available to help analysis. Our work provides a new experimental method of characterizing FE electron sources, especially the atomic-scale cold cathode, for which existing plot-based data-analysis methods are not suitable.

</details>


### [8] [Optimal recovery for quantum error correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06520)
*Sun Woo P. Kim*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了确定量子纠错码最优错误阈值（optimal error threshold）的新方法，通过引入互迹距离（mutual trace distance）这一信息论量，无需显式优化即可精确确定最优阈值，并证明了Petz和Schumacher-Westmoreland恢复方案的最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子纠错码阈值计算通常基于特定解码器（如最大似然解码器），但这仅提供了阈值下界。真正的"最优阈值"应通过优化所有可能的量子信道恢复方案来确定，而现有方法未能提供精确确定最优阈值的诊断工具。

Method: 引入互迹距离（mutual trace distance）作为信息论量，该量提供了确定最优阈值$p_\mathrm{th}^\mathrm{opt}$的必要且充分诊断工具，无需显式优化。研究分析了包括Petz和Schumacher-Westmoreland（SW）恢复方案在内的各种量子信道恢复方案。

Result: 证明了Petz和Schumacher-Westmoreland恢复方案是最优的，即它们的阈值等于$p_\mathrm{th}^\mathrm{opt}$。互迹距离能够精确确定最优阈值，而传统方法（如相干信息）仅提供阈值下界。进一步探索了最优与非最优恢复方案的结构及其相图。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了确定量子纠错码最优错误阈值的理论框架，通过互迹距离提供了精确诊断工具，并证明了特定恢复方案的最优性，为理解量子纠错恢复方案的结构和相变行为奠定了基础。

Abstract: The calculation of the error threshold of quantum error correcting codes typically proceeds as follows. First, syndromes are measured. Then, a decoder infers the error chain and the corresponding correction is applied. The threshold is then defined as the largest correctable error rate, with the maximum-likelihood decoder corresponding to the ``optimal'' threshold. However, a broader set of operations could be used to recover quantum information. The true optimal threshold should be optimised over all possible recovery schemes, which can be described by quantum channels. Here, we study such optimal recovery channels and their thresholds $p_\mathrm{th}^\mathrm{opt}$. We introduce an information-theoretic quantity, mutual trace distance, which provides a necessary and sufficient diagnostic for sharply determining $p_\mathrm{th}^\mathrm{opt}$ without explicit optimisation. In contrast, previous works give a lower bound on $p_\mathrm{th}^\mathrm{opt}$ by specifying particular recovery schemes, e.g. Schumacher-Westmoreland (SW) which provides coherent information as a diagnostic to lower bound $p^\mathrm{opt}_\mathrm{th}$. We prove that the Petz and SW recovery schemes are optimal, i.e. their threshold is $p_\mathrm{th}^\mathrm{opt}$. With their optimality established, we explore the structure of optimal and non-optimal recovery schemes and their phase diagrams.

</details>


### [9] [Towards Studying Superconductivity in the Fermi-Hubbard Model on Rydberg Atoms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06529)
*Kübra Yeter-Aydeniz,Nora M. Bauer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用里德堡原子处理器（Rydberg atom processor）和基于采样的量子对角化（sample-based quantum diagonalization, SQD）方法计算费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）基态能量的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决费米-哈伯德模型在大U参数下的基态能量计算问题，并探讨一维费米-哈伯德模型中准超导性（quasi-superconductivity）的相关机制。

Method: 方法基于费米-哈伯德模型与海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）之间的微扰关系，利用里德堡原子处理器制备海森堡模型并进行采样，然后使用这些样本对大U参数的费米-哈伯德模型进行对角化。研究还包含了各向异性（anisotropy）和次近邻相互作用（next-nearest-neighbor interactions）。

Result: 在Aquila量子处理器上的数值和实验结果表明，所研究区域的海森堡模型采样足以使56个量子比特的系统基态收敛，且里德堡原子采样相比随机采样具有明显优势。研究还提供了在IBM Quantum硬件上实现的56量子比特哈伯德模型的基准测试。

Conclusion: 该方法能够有效计算费米-哈伯德模型的基态能量和化学势，并为研究涌现超导性（emergent superconductivity）提供了能隙分析（gap analysis）工具。

Abstract: We present a method for calculating the ground state energy of the Fermi-Hubbard model leveraging Rydberg atom processors and sample-based quantum diagonalization (SQD). By exploiting the perturbative relationship between the Fermi-Hubbard and Heisenberg models, the procedure samples from the Heisenberg model as prepared on the Rydberg atom processor, and uses the samples to diagonalize the Fermi-Hubbard model for large U. We include anisotropy and next-nearest-neighbor interactions and discuss the relevant regime for quasi-superconductivity in the 1-dimensional Fermi- Hubbard model. Numerical and experimental results on the Aquila quantum processor are presented for ground state energy calculations as well as the chemical potential. We find that the Heisenberg model sampling in the studied regime is sufficient to converge near to the ground state for up to 56 qubits, and we see a clear advantage of Rydberg atom sampling as opposed to random sampling even with 10x more samples for diagonalization. We also present a gate-based implementation of the gate-based SQD algorithm on IBM Quantum hardware for 56-qubit Hubbard model as a benchmark. Finally, we provide a gap analysis for studying emergent superconductivity using this method.

</details>

### [10] [Identification of an Unreported Structure Type in GdNiSn4 and Its Implications for Materials Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05613)
*Xin Zhang,Scott B. Lee,Sudipta Chatterjee,Hanqi Pi,Yi Yang,Fatmagül Katmer,Emily G. Ward,Daniel E. Widdowson,Charles C. Tam,Sarah Schwarz,Connor J. Pollak,Jaime M. Moya,Grigorii Skorupskii,Vitaliy A. Kurlin,Stephen D. Wilson,B. Andrei Bernevig,Leslie M. Schoop*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在晶体无机材料领域，新的结构类型很少被发现，大多数实验实现的结构基元都是几十年前建立的。尽管人工智能辅助的材料发现工作正在进行，但这些方法尚未产生令人信服的新结构类型，而主要是现有化合物的取代变体。

Method: 研究采用传统实验方法发现了化合物GdNiSn4的新结构类型，并测试了当前最先进的人工智能材料生成模型预测该材料正确结构的能力。通过仔细分析新结构，将其视为两种已知结构类型的堆叠，并探索了其稳定性的电子和空间因素。

Result: 研究发现GdNiSn4采用了一种新的结构类型，而当前最先进的人工智能材料生成模型无法预测这种材料及其正确结构。该结构可被视为两种已知结构类型的堆叠，研究还发现了GdNiSn4具有复杂的磁性质，突显了其在未来非常规磁性研究中的潜在价值。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了传统实验方法在发现新材料结构中的持续重要性，同时指出了当前人工智能材料生成模型的局限性。研究提出了改进未来AI引导材料发现的策略，并展示了GdNiSn4在磁性研究中的潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Crystal structures define how matter is organized at the atomic level. In the realm of crystalline inorganic materials, new structure types are rarely found, and most experimentally-realized structural motifs were established decades ago. Considerable efforts are underway to discover new crystalline inorganic compounds, often aided by artificial intelligence (AI). However, thus far, these methods have not yielded convincing new structure types, but rather substitutional variations of existing compounds. Here we introduce a new structure type adopted by the compound GdNiSn4, discovered the old-fashioned way. We test whether current state-of-the-art AI-based material generation models can predict this material in its correct structure and find that they fail to do so. We carefully analyze the new structure and argue that it can be viewed as a stack of two known structure types. We explore electronic and steric factors underlying its stability and propose strategies to improve future AI-guided materials discovery. Furthermore, we report complex magnetic properties in GdNiSn4, highlighting its potential interest for future studies of unconventional magnetism.

### [11] [Active Learning for Tractable and Reproducible Pulsed Laser Deposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05699)
*Jackson S. Bentley,Christopher Rouleau,Ilia N. Ivanov,T. Zac Ward,Jiaqiang Yan,Anghea Dolisca,Rob G. Moore,Gyula Eres,Richard F. Haglund,Sumner B. Harris,Matthew Brahlek*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究展示了基于高斯过程贝叶斯优化的主动学习框架如何改善脉冲激光沉积（PLD）生长LaVO₃薄膜的质量控制、可重复性和物理理解，通过多属性优化实现了相纯薄膜的制备并揭示了生长机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管生长条件与材料性质之间存在已知关系，但由于PLD的高度非平衡性质以及生长过程中积累的缺陷和竞争相，持续制备高质量复杂氧化物（如LaVO₃）薄膜仍然困难。

Method: 采用基于高斯过程贝叶斯优化（Gaussian process Bayesian optimization）的主动学习框架，结合测量的体相和表面晶格性质以及杂质相信息，高效映射LaVO₃的PLD多维生长空间。

Result: 通过调整这些性质的相对权重，模型识别出优化区域，在该区域中相纯（phase-pure）的LaVO₃薄膜表现出二维表面、接近理想的晶格参数和最小的亚带隙光学吸收。训练后的模型揭示了不同缺陷形成机制之间的明显竞争。

Conclusion: 研究表明，属性引导的机器学习（property-guided machine learning）可以加速材料优化，同时为理解PLD中的基本生长机制提供新途径，从而促进复杂氧化物中量子现象的理解和利用。

Abstract: This paper shows how data-driven machine learning approaches can improve growth control, reproducibility, and physical insight in the pulsed laser deposition (PLD) growth of correlated oxides. Despite well-known relationships between growth conditions and material properties, consistently producing high-quality films of complex materials like LaVO$_3$ remains difficult due to the highly non-equilibrium nature of PLD and the defects and competing phases that accumulate during growth. Here, we use an active learning framework based on Gaussian process Bayesian optimization that incorporates measured bulk and surface lattice properties along with impurity phase information to efficiently map the multidimensional growth space of LaVO$_3$ by PLD. By tuning the relative weighting of these properties, the model identifies an optimized region where phase-pure films of LaVO$_3$ exhibit two-dimensional surfaces, near-ideal lattice parameters, and minimal sub-band gap optical absorption. The trained model reveals clear competition among different defect formation mechanisms that are connected to unseen parameters like supersaturation and surface mobility, thus giving insight into the highly non-equilibrium process of PLD growth. Together, this demonstrates that property-guided machine learning can accelerate materials optimization while providing a new way to address fundamental growth mechanisms in PLD that enable understanding and utilization of quantum phenomena found in complex oxides.

### [12] [The Evolution of Magnetism in a Thin Film Pyrochlore Ferromagnetic Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05717)
*Margaret A. Anderson,Megan E. Goh,Yang Zhang,Kyeong-Yoon Baek,Michael Schulze,Mario Brutzam,Christoph Liebald,Chris Lygouras,Dan Ferenc Segedin,Aaron M. Day,Zubia Hasan,Donald A. Walko,Hua Zhou,Peter Bencok,Alpha T. N'Diaye,Charles M. Brooks,Ismail El Baggari,John T. Heron,S. M. Koopayeh,Daniel Rytz,Christo Guguschev,Julia A. Mundy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究首次合成了烧绿石结构Y₂V₂O₇薄膜，发现其保持绝缘铁磁性且居里温度可达体材料值，薄膜厚度减小导致居里温度下降符合有限尺寸效应，应变变化引起磁各向异性从面内转向面外，为可调控拓扑磁振子器件奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 烧绿石钒酸盐（pyrochlore vanadates）如Lu₂V₂O₇和Y₂V₂O₇是下一代无耗散器件的理想候选材料，因其作为铁磁绝缘体（Tc ~ 70 K）被认为具有磁振子霍尔效应（magnon Hall effect）并可能承载拓扑磁振子（topological magnons）。这些完全无耗散的磁振子边缘态可用于实现自旋电子或磁振子器件中的低功耗信息传输。

Method: 在结构同型的Y₂Ti₂O₇衬底上首次合成了烧绿石Y₂V₂O₇薄膜，并系统研究了其磁性性质在超薄极限下的演化规律。

Result: 所有薄膜均为绝缘铁磁体，居里温度最高可达体材料值（Tc ~ 68 K），且随厚度减小而降低，符合有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）。薄膜还表现出磁各向异性从面内易轴转向面外易轴的变化，这与部分应变弛豫的发展以及外加磁场中非零磁滞回线的出现相一致。

Conclusion: 应变对磁各向异性的影响得到证实，这为可调控的磁振子拓扑（tunable magnon topology）器件开发铺平了道路，是实现低功耗信息传输器件的重要进展。

Abstract: The pyrochlore vanadates are compelling candidates for next-generation dissipationless devices. Lu2V2O7 and Y2V2O7 are ferromagnetic insulators (Tc ~ 70 K) that are believed to exhibit the magnon Hall effect and are expected to host topological magnons. Their completely dissipationless magnon edge states could be harnessed to realize low-power information transport in spintronic or magnonic devices. As a crucial step in the realization of devices, we synthesize the first thin films of pyrochlore Y2V2O7 on isostructural Y2Ti2O7 substrates and explore the evolution of their magnetic properties down to the ultrathin limit. All films are insulating ferromagnets with transition temperatures of up to the bulk value (Tc ~ 68 K) that decrease with thickness according to finite-size effects. Our films also exhibit a change in anisotropy from in-plane to out-of-plane easy axis coincident with the development of partial strain relaxation and nonzero magnetic hysteresis in an applied field. This evolution demonstrates the impact of strain on magnetic anisotropy and paves the way to tunable magnon topology.

</details>


### [13] [Twist-Controlled Modulation of Quantum Emitters in a Van der Waals Bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05856)
*Angus Gale,Seungjun Lee,Seungmin Park,Evan Williams,Helen Zhi Jie Zeng,James Liddle-Wesolowski,Young Duck Kim,Milos Toth,Tony Low,Igor Aharonovich*

TL;DR: 该研究展示了通过机械扭转（mechanical twisting）范德华（van der Waals）材料六方氮化硼（hBN）同质双层结构，可在室温下调控单个量子发射体（quantum emitter），实现超过30纳米（约100毫电子伏特）的可调谐性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料的堆叠和扭转（stacking and twisting）引起了凝聚态物理和纳米光子学领域的广泛关注，主要源于层间耦合（interlayer coupling）产生的新颖光物理现象。研究旨在探索扭转自由度（twist degree of freedom）对量子发射体的调控能力。

Method: 采用六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）范德华同质双层结构，通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）模拟量子发射体发射特性随扭转角（twist angle）的变化。实验上通过机械扭转顶层hBN层实现原位调控（in-situ tuning）。

Result: 密度泛函理论结果显示嵌入的发射体强烈受扭转角和顶层hBN堆叠方式影响。实验成功实现了对嵌入量子发射体的原位调控，获得了超过30纳米（约100毫电子伏特）的可调谐性（tunability）。

Conclusion: 机械扭转可用于调控范德华材料中嵌入的量子发射体，这标志着向可编程片上量子电路（programmable on-chip quantum circuitry）迈出了关键一步。

Abstract: Stacking and twisting two dimensional materials has garnered enormous attention across the condensed matter and the nanophotonic communities. The surge of interest stems from the emergence of novel photophysical phenomena that arise due to the interlayer coupling of the individual layers. Here, we demonstrate that the twist degree of freedom can modulate a single quantum emitter at room temperature. We employ a van der Waals homobilayer of hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) and model the emission properties of quantum emitters as a function of the twist angle. Density functional theory results show that the embedded emitters are strongly influenced by the twist angle and the stacking of the top hBN layer. We consequently engineer these systems experimentally, and demonstrate in-situ tuning of embedded quantum emitters by mechanically twisting the top hBN layer, achieving tunability of over 30 nm (~ 100 meV). Our work demonstrates that mechanical twisting can be harnessed to modulate the embedded quantum emitters in a vdW material, marking a crucial step towards a programmable on-chip quantum circuitry.

### [14] [Electrically tunable circular photocurrent via local-field induced symmetry breaking at a metal-MoTe2 interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05866)
*Butian Zhang,Kexin Wang,Jun-Tao Ma,Yiya Guo,Chengyu Yan,Xin Yi,Luojun Du,Youwei Zhang,Hua-Hua Fu,Shun Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过在金-MoTe₂异质结界面处实现显著的圆偏振光电流，揭示了利用内置电场调控过渡金属二硫化物中圆偏振光电流的机制，为电压可调谐的圆偏振光电探测器和谷电子器件提供了有效策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属二硫化物（transition metal dichalcogenides, TMDCs）是研究对称性调控圆偏振光响应的理想平台。中心对称的2H相TMDCs的高晶体对称性本质上禁止了圆光电流效应（circular photogalvanic effect），需要外部电场或应变来降低对称性以激活该效应。肖特基结（Schottky junctions）提供了普遍存在的内置电场，但TMDCs中圆光电流的产生和控制机制尚不明确。

Method: 研究制备了局域化的金-MoTe₂异质结构，并在垂直入射条件下测量了界面处的圆光电流。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析了金界面诱导的MoTe₂价带自旋劈裂（spin splitting）和谷依赖的自旋序（valley-dependent spin ordering）。

Result: 实验观察到界面处显著的圆光电流，该电流归因于由内置电场强度和方向控制的圆光电流效应，可通过外部偏压进行连续调制。第一性原理计算表明金界面诱导了MoTe₂价带的自旋劈裂，建立了谷依赖的自旋序。多层2H-MoTe₂在垂直入射下观测到的圆光电流表明局域面内电场破坏了C3旋转对称性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种有效策略，通过利用内置电场调控TMDCs中的圆光电流效应，为开发电压可调谐的圆偏振光电探测器（circularly polarized photodetectors）和谷电子器件（valleytronic devices）提供了基础。

Abstract: Transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) constitute a promising platform for symmetry-engineered responses to circularly polarized light. The high crystal symmetry of centrosymmetric 2H-phase TMDCs inherently forbids the circular photogalvanic effect, thereby necessitating external stimuli such as electric fields or strain to lower the symmetry for its activation. While Schottky junctions provide a ubiquitous built-in field for potentially inducing circular photocurrents, the mechanism for the generation and control of circular photocurrents in TMDCs is not understood. In this study, we fabricated a localized gold-MoTe2 heterostructure and demonstrate a pronounced circular photocurrent at the interface under normal incidence. The photocurrent is attributed to circular photogalvanic effect governed by the strength and direction of the built-in electric field, enabling continuous modulation via an external bias. First-principles calculations show that the gold interface induces a spin splitting in the valence bands of MoTe2, establishing a valley-dependent spin ordering. The observed circular photocurrent from multilayer 2H-MoTe2 under normal incidence indicates the breaking of C3 rotational symmetry by the local in-plane field. These results establish an effective strategy for developing voltage-tunable circularly polarized photodetectors and valleytronic devices.

</details>


### [15] [Theory of central peak and acoustic anomaly in cubic BaTiO3 close to ferroelectric transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05914)
*Akira Onuki*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究基于金兹堡-朗道理论（Ginzburg-Landau theory）分析了立方结构顺电相中钛酸钡（BaTiO₃）型铁电体的静态和动态特性，重点探讨了电致伸缩耦合（electrostrictive coupling）如何导致中心峰（central peak）和声学异常（acoustic anomaly）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多铁电体的散射实验中长期观察到中心峰现象，但其起源尚未得到充分理解。本研究旨在通过电致伸缩耦合效应解释这些中心峰的产生机制，并分析其对弹性模量和声学特性的影响。

Method: 采用金兹堡-朗道理论框架，以极化强度（polarization）为序参数，研究立方结构顺电相中铁电体的静态和动态行为。特别关注极化与弹性位移之间的电致伸缩耦合效应，分析位移时间关联函数的傅里叶-拉普拉斯变换。

Result: 电致伸缩耦合在小波数下导致位移时间关联函数中出现中心峰，该峰在接近相变时出现并增强且宽度变窄。从位移动态关联的声学部分获得了频率依赖的弹性模量C₁₁*(ω)、C₁₂*(ω)和C₄₄*(ω)，其奇异部分源于电致伸缩耦合。中心峰和弹性模量中的频率以标度形式ωτ_D出现，其中τ_D为介电常数中的德拜弛豫时间。

Conclusion: 电致伸缩耦合是铁电体中心峰现象和声学异常的关键物理机制，为长期观察到的实验现象提供了理论解释。该研究建立了中心峰、弹性模量奇异性和声速衰减之间的统一理论框架。

Abstract: We present a Ginzburg-Landau theory on statics and dynamics of BaTiO$_3$-type ferroelectrics in
  the paraelectric phase with the cubic structure, where the order parameter is the polarization $\bi p$. Unique effects are caused by the electrostrictive (ES) coupling between
  ${\bi p}$ and the elastic displacement $\bi u$. We show that the ES coupling gives rise to a central peak in the Fourier-Laplace transform of the displacement time-correlation function at small wave numbers. It emerges and grows with a narrow width as the transition is approached. Such central peaks have long been observed in a number of scattering experiments in various ferroelectrics, but their origin has not been well understood. From the acoustic part of the displacement dynamic correlation we obtain the frequency-dependent elastic moduli $C_{11}^*(ω)$, $C_{12}^*(ω)$, and $C_{44}^*(ω)$, whose singular parts arise from the ES coupling, We then calculate the singular sound velocity and
  attenuation. In the central peak and the elastic moduli, the frequency $ω$ appears in the scaled form $ωτ_D$, where $τ_D$ is the Debye relaxation time in the frequency-dependent dielectric constant.
  {Keywords}: ferroelectric transition, central peak, acoustic anomaly, electrostrictive coupling

</details>


### [16] [Riemannian geometric classification and emergent phenomena of magnetic textures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05955)
*Koki Shinada,Naoto Nagaosa*

TL;DR: 本文从微分几何视角提出磁结构新分类法，引入两种新型标量自旋手性（geodesic SSC和torsional SSC），并证明geodesic SSC可诱导非互易响应作为量子几何效应。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统磁结构分类基于矢量自旋手性（VSC）和标量自旋手性（SSC），但该分类不完整，特别是非共面结构无法仅用SSC充分表征，如锥形磁体所示。需要更精确的几何分类框架。

Method: 采用微分几何方法分析实空间中自旋轨迹的曲线和曲面，引入两种新型标量自旋手性：测地标量自旋手性（geodesic scalar spin chirality）和扭转标量自旋手性（torsional scalar spin chirality）。构建包含非绝热效应和磁结构高阶空间梯度的半经典理论。

Result: 基于新型手性识别出三类不同的非共面磁结构。测地SSC诱导出新兴能带不对称性，导致非互易响应作为量子几何效应。该机制是纯轨道效应，无需自旋轨道耦合，与SSC驱动的拓扑霍尔效应传统图像平行。

Conclusion: 发展的几何视角为磁结构分类、量子几何、涌现电动力学及更广泛的涌现现象提供了广泛新见解。新型手性分类框架完善了传统分类体系，揭示了新的量子几何效应机制。

Abstract: We propose a new classification of magnetic textures from the viewpoint of differential geometry. Magnetic textures are conventionally classified into collinear, coplanar, and noncoplanar magnets. These classes are typically characterized by the vector spin chirality (VSC) and the scalar spin chirality (SSC), which indicate noncollinearity and noncoplanarity, respectively. However, this conventional classification is incomplete: in particular, noncoplanar textures cannot be fully characterized by the SSC alone, as exemplified by conical magnets. To refine this classification, we analyze the curves and surfaces traced by spins in real space using differential geometry and introduce two novel scalar spin chiralities that properly characterize noncoplanarity: the geodesic scalar spin chirality and the torsional scalar spin chirality. These quantities are directly connected to differential geometry: the former reflects the geodesic curvature while the latter is related to the torsion. Based on these chiralities, we identify three distinct classes of noncoplanar magnetic textures. Furthermore, analogous to the roles of the VSC and the conventional SSC in emergent electrodynamics, the geodesic SSC gives rise to novel emergent phenomena. By constructing a semiclassical theory including nonadiabatic effects and higher-order spatial gradients of magnetic textures, we demonstrate that the geodesic SSC induces an emergent band asymmetry, leading to nonreciprocal responses as a quantum geometric effect. This mechanism is a purely orbital effect, requiring no spin-orbit coupling, and the resulting discussion runs in parallel with the conventional picture of the topological Hall effect driven by the SSC. The geometric viewpoint developed here will provide broad new insights into classification, quantum geometry, emergent electrodynamics, and a wider variety of emergent phenomena.

Here, we present Spectra-Scope, an open-source AutoML framework for automatic characterization of material properties from spectroscopy data using interpretable machine learning (ML) models. The software is implemented in Python and a no-code web application. It comprises tools for data preprocessing, nonlinear feature extraction, machine learning model training, and feature downselection. Users can easily train different types of simple, interpretable ML models on a set of feature transformations quickly and with modest computational resources. In this work, we outline the methods of Spectra-Scope and its effectiveness across diverse datasets, with applications to materials and agricultural spectroscopy data.   <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: β-Ga₂O₃作为有前景的宽带隙半导体，其离子诱导缺陷形成和各向异性弹性的影响尚未被充分理解。研究旨在探索各向异性系统中应变-应力动力学，建立宏观实验与原子尺度模拟的直接比较方法。

Result: XRD观察到面外方向应变以各向异性方式累积：沿[010]方向为压缩应变，垂直于(100)和(001)方向为拉伸应变。MD模拟提出的各向异性应力/应变累积模型与实验结果高度一致。在较高损伤水平下，实验和MD均揭示出取向无关的β到γ相变，多晶型间存在固定的晶体学关系。

Conclusion: 该工作通过探索各向异性系统中的应变-应力动力学，建立了直接比较宏观尺度衍射实验与原子尺度模拟的方法，为利用各向异性响应调控离子注入/辐照系统的性能开辟了新途径。

Abstract: While $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ is considered a promising wide bandgap semiconductor, the impact of ion-induced defect formation and anisotropic elasticity remains poorly understood. Here, we combine a simulation and experiment X-ray diffraction (XRD) study of the strain-stress dynamics induced by ion implantation into $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ single-crystals with different surface orientations. The strain accumulation in the out-of-plane direction is observed by XRD to occur in an anisotropic manner, with compressive strain along the [010] direction and tensile strain along the directions perpendicular to (100) and (001). An anisotropic stress/strain accumulation model is proposed and probed via Molecular Dynamics (MD), showing an excellent agreement with the experiments. For higher damage levels, pole figures obtained both experimentally and by MD via a novel reciprocal-space projection method reveal an orientation-independent $β$-to-$γ$ phase transition, with a fixed crystallographic relationship between the polymorphs. By exploring the strain-stress dynamics in anisotropic systems, this work establishes a method to directly compare macroscale diffraction experiments and atomistic simulations and opens a new path to engineer the properties of such systems utilizing their anisotropic response to ion implantation/irradiation.

</details>


### [25] [Giant orbital magnetoresistance in the antiferromagnet CoO driven by dynamic orbital angular momentum interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06425)
*Christin Schmitt,Sachin Krishnia,Edgar Galindez-Ruales,Luca Micus,Takashi Kikkawa,Hiroki Arisawa,Marjana Lezaic,Duc Tran,Timo Kuschel,Jairo Sinova,Eiji Saitoh,Gerhard Jakob,Olena Gomonay,Yuriy Mokrousov,Mathias Kläui*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过使用轨道角动量主导的材料CoO，在CoO/Cu*结构中实现了超过50倍的轨道霍尔磁阻增强，展示了轨道电流与静态轨道角动量的直接相互作用，为轨道电子学器件提供了前所未有的能量效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道电流效应比自旋电流大数个数量级的预测引起了广泛关注，但轨道电流的潜力尚未完全发挥，因为传统上需要将轨道电流转换为自旋电流才能与自旋角动量主导的静态磁化相互作用。

Method: 通过使用轨道角动量主导的反铁磁绝缘体CoO，构建CoO/Cu*异质结构，研究轨道电流与静态轨道角动量的直接相互作用机制，并与传统的CoO/Pt结构进行对比。

Result: 在CoO/Cu*结构中观察到超过50倍的轨道霍尔磁阻（orbital Hall magnetoresistance）增强，这是由表面氧化Cu*产生的动态轨道角动量（即轨道电流）与CoO中构成磁矩的静态轨道角动量之间的独特相互作用驱动的。与CoO/Pt相比，CoO/Cu*界面处的轨道电流散射机制导致轨道磁阻符号反转。

Conclusion: 通过使用CoO等轨道角动量主导的材料，可以直接利用巨大的轨道电流优势，这在传统自旋主导的磁体中无法实现。这为轨道电子学（orbitronics）器件提供了前所未有的能量效率，结合了反铁磁体的终极稳定性和太赫兹（THz）动力学特性。

Abstract: Recent predictions of orders of magnitude larger orbital current effects compared to spin currents have attracted significant interest. However, the full potential of giant orbital currents remains to be fully harnessed, since so far, the orbital currents need to be converted into spin currents before they can interact with the static magnetization that is dominated by spin angular momentum in conventional magnets. By using a magnet dominated by orbital angular momentum, we demonstrate a more than fifty-fold enhancement in orbital Hall magnetoresistance in CoO/Cu*, compared to conventional CoO/Pt. This is found to be driven by a unique interaction between dynamic orbital angular momentum from surface oxidized Cu* (i.e., the orbital current) and the static orbital angular momentum which constitutes the magnetic moments in the antiferromagnetic insulator CoO. A distinctive scattering mechanism for orbital currents at the CoO interface leads to a sign reversal in orbital magnetoresistance in CoO/Cu* compared to CoO/Pt. Our results show how by using orbital angular momentum-dominated materials such as CoO, we can harness the benefits of giant orbital currents that have not been possible using conventional spin-dominated magnets, for orbitronics-based devices, offering unprecedented energy efficiency for operations of antiferromagnets that combine ultimate stability with THz dynamics.

</details>


### [26] [Real-time exciton dynamics in two-dimensional materials under ultrashort laser pulses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06446)

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合第一性原理方法和精确数值方案，理论研究了二维六方氮化硼（h-BN）和硫化锗（GeS）单层材料在超短激光脉冲下的激子动力学，阐明了多体效应在二维材料超快激子过程中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料中由于库仑相互作用的屏蔽减弱，激子效应显著影响其光学响应。准确模拟激子形成和实时动力学对于理解其超快光学特性至关重要，这对光电子和光子应用具有重要意义。

Method: 研究结合了先进的第一性原理（ab initio）方法和高精度数值方案，通过多体微扰理论（MBPT）推导的非局域自能算符在含时绝热GW（TD-aGW）近似下纳入电子-空穴相互作用，使用全电子LAPW+lo方法在exciting软件包中实现。

Result: 分析了二维h-BN和GeS单层材料在单光子和双光子激发机制下对外部场的响应，阐明了多体效应在塑造二维材料超快激子过程中的作用。

Conclusion: 该研究为光电子和光子应用所需的基础理解做出了贡献，揭示了多体效应在二维材料超快激子动力学中的关键作用。

Abstract: The optical response of two-dimensional materials is often significantly impacted by excitonic effects due to the reduced screening of attractive Coulomb interactions in low-dimensional systems. Accurate modeling of exciton formation and real-time dynamics is essential to understanding their ultrafast optical properties. In this study, we theoretically investigate the exciton dynamics in a two-dimensional hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) and a germanium sulfide (GeS) monolayers exposed to an ultrashort laser pulse. We analyze the system's response to the external field in one- and two-photon excitation regimes. For our calculations, we combine a state-of-the-art ab initio approach to study exciton dynamics with a highly precise numerical scheme. We incorporate electron-hole interactions through a non-local self-energy operator derived from the many-body perturbation theory (MBPT) within the time-dependent adiabatic $GW$ (TD-a$GW$) approximation. We implement this approach using the full-electron LAPW+lo method in the all-electron exciting package. Our results elucidate the role of many-body effects in shaping ultrafast excitonic processes in two-dimensional materials, contributing to the fundamental understanding necessary for optoelectronic and photonic applications.

### [27] [Revisiting the symmetry and optical phonons of altermagnetic $α$-MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06460)
*Ece Uykur,Marcos V. Gonçalves-Faria,Sahana Rößler,Victoria A. Ginga,Marcus Schmidt,Stephan Winnerl,Manfred Helm,Alexander A. Tsirlin*

TL;DR: 该研究通过红外、拉曼光谱与高分辨率X射线衍射相结合，澄清了反铁磁α-MnTe材料中的争议问题，揭示了机械应力导致的布拉格峰展宽效应，并确认了该材料的本征光学声子模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解决反铁磁（altermagnetic）α-MnTe材料中存在的多个争议性问题，特别是关于其光谱特征和相纯度的争议，这些争议源于先前研究中观察到的不可重复现象。

Method: 采用红外（IR）和拉曼（Raman）光谱技术结合高分辨率X射线衍射，辅以空间分辨拉曼光谱和第一性原理计算（ab initio calculations），对α-MnTe晶体进行了系统表征。

Result: 研究发现机械应力会导致布拉格峰（Bragg peaks）显著展宽，掩盖样品中的次级相；约175 cm⁻¹的拉曼模式源于MnTe₂次级相而非α-MnTe本征特征；确认了α-MnTe在室温下的本征光学声子模式，包括约155 cm⁻¹的红外活性声子（E₁ᵤ）和约100 cm⁻¹的拉曼活性声子（E₂g）。

Conclusion: 研究澄清了α-MnTe的光谱特征争议，建立了其本征声子模式，并确认该材料在实验分辨率内同时保持六重旋转对称性和反演对称性，为理解其物理性质提供了可靠基础。

Abstract: Using infrared (IR) and Raman spectroscopies combined with high-resolution x-ray diffraction, we address several controversial aspects of altermagnetic $α$-MnTe. We show that mechanical stress applied to crystals of this material causes a drastic broadening of Bragg peaks that conceals signatures of additional phases present in the sample. Indeed, spatially resolved Raman spectroscopy reveals that the modes around 175 cm$^{-1}$ often reported in $α$-MnTe are not reproducible across different positions and samples and originate from the secondary phase of MnTe$_2$. By combining spectroscopic probes with ab initio calculations, we establish the IR-active optical phonon of $α$-MnTe around 155 cm$^{-1}$ ($E_{1u}$) and the Raman-active optical phonon around 100 cm$^{-1}$ ($E_{2g}$) at room temperature. Two intense Raman modes around 120 and 140 cm$^{-1}$ are shown to be intrinsic, even though they can not be assigned to $Γ$-point optical phonons. These modes couple to magnetic order in $α$-MnTe and also to the transient reflectivity resulting in coherent oscillations. Both 6-fold rotation symmetry and inversion symmetry are preserved in $α$-MnTe within our experimental resolution.

### [28] [Structural Commonalities in Different Classes of Non-Crystalline Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06484)
*I. Rodriguez,D. Hinojosa-Romero,R. M. Valladares,A. Valladares,A. A. Valladares*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究比较了非晶态固体（non-crystalline solids）中半导体玻璃（amorphous semiconductors）与金属玻璃（metallic glasses）的结构差异，重点分析其对分布函数（Pair Distribution Functions, PDF）的第一和第二峰特征，并探讨了半金属（semimetals）和合金（alloys）的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索不同类别非晶态固体（包括半导体和金属玻璃）的结构趋势异同。过去几十年研究界已探索了非晶固体的多样结构和制备方法，但需要系统比较不同类别材料的结构特征差异。

Method: 研究方法基于对分布函数（Pair Distribution Functions, PDF）的结构分析，重点关注第一和第二峰的特征。通过比较半导体网络形成材料（network-forming materials）和金属系统的PDF模式来识别结构差异。

Result: 研究发现半导体玻璃的PDF具有相似的第一和第二峰，峰间值接近零；而金属系统在峰间具有明确定义的非零值，并显示出"象峰（elephant peak）"特征。半导体网络形成材料的性质相似，而金属系统的性质与前者显著不同。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明不同类别的非晶态固体存在明显的结构差异：半导体玻璃显示简单的峰结构，而金属玻璃具有复杂的峰间特征和"象峰"。这些结构差异反映了材料性质的本质不同，研究还探讨了半金属和合金的情况。

Abstract: In the past decades, the research community has explored diverse structures and new fabrication methods of non-crystalline solids. Glassy materials that belong to the semiconductor realm and to the metallic type are the most studied both experimentally and theoretically. The present work investigates similar structural trends whenever they exist and different trends among different classes. Amorphous semiconductors display Pair Distribution Functions (PDF) that are very similar among themselves, and this indicates that these network-forming materials have properties that are alike. Analogously, metallic systems have comparable PDFs but different from the network forming materials, as it should be, since the properties between these two classes are quite different. Here we pay attention to the first and second peaks of their structures. Whereas the semiconductor structures display a simple first and second peak with a near-zero value between them. In contrast, the metallic systems have a very well-defined non-zero value between the first and second peaks, and they also display what we have come to identify as an 'elephant peak'. We also discuss semimetals and alloys.

</details>

*Patrick J. Strohbeen,Soohyun Im,Tamalika Samanta,Zachary LaDuca,Dongxue Du,Estiaque H. Shourov,Jessica L. McChesney,Fanny Rodolakis,Paul M. Voyles,Jason K. Kawasaki*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We report the epitaxial stabilization of GdAuSb films and GdAuSb/LaAuSb superlattices via molecular beam epitaxy on (0001)-oriented Al$_{2}$O$_{3}$ substrates. GdAuSb crystallize in the Au-Au dimerized YPtAs structure type (space group $P6_{3}/mmc$), the same structure as the Dirac semimetal LaAuSb. Angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) measurements show similar near $E_F$ bandstructures for GdAuSb and LaAuSb, plus a rigid band shift for GdAuSb towards more hole-like behavior and core-like Gd $4f$ states $\sim 9$~eV below the Fermi energy. LaAuSb/GdAuSb superlattices exhibit sharp superlattice fringes by X-ray diffraction and atomically-precise interfaces by scanning transmission electron microscopy. Superlattices display two transitions in temperature-dependent resistvity, compared to a single Néel temperature for thick GdAuSb films. Superlattices of $Ln$AuSb materials ($Ln=$ rare earth) with atomically abrupt interfaces offer a new epitaxial platform for control of magnetic and topological order via tunable intralayer exchange and reduced dimensionality.

Abstract: Accurate knowledge of the atomistic transition pathways in materials and material surfaces is crucial for many material science problems. Here, we demonstrate how transformers can be trained to predict atomistic transitions in nano-clusters. We show how we evaluate physical validity of the predictions and how a multitude of additional, different microstates can be generated by slightly varying the data provided to the model.

### [31] [Deterministic Electrical Switching in Altermagnets via Surface Antisymmetry Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06537)
*K. D. Belashchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了表面反对称群框架，用于确定d波交变磁体中可实现确定性电学切换的表面取向设计规则，这些规则基于表面反对称点群，对对称等效表面刻面和平衡粗糙度具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为共线双分反铁磁体薄膜中奈尔矢量（Néel vector）的确定性电学切换建立设计规则，特别是在体电流诱导力矩消失的d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnets）中，需要理解界面响应如何产生交错有效场。

Method: 研究开发了表面反对称群（surface antisymmetry group）框架，用于确定给定表面取向下允许的张量形式，同时分析自旋电导率张量（spin conductivity tensor）结构以识别哪些表面取向允许通过自旋分裂效应（spin-splitter effect）产生横向自旋流。

Result: 研究确定了d波交变磁体中哪些表面取向可以作为自旋扭矩异质结构（spin-torque heterostructures）中确定性可切换的自旋流源，这些设计规则完全基于表面反对称点群，所需的交错轴向响应对对称等效表面刻面和平衡粗糙度的平均具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 表面反对称群框架为d波交变磁体中奈尔矢量的确定性电学切换提供了可靠的设计规则，这些基于对称性的规则确保了交错轴向响应的鲁棒性，为自旋扭矩异质结构中的可控自旋流源设计奠定了基础。

Abstract: A surface antisymmetry group framework is developed to establish design rules for deterministic electrical switching of the Néel vector in a film of a collinear bipartite antiferromagnet. In centrosymmetric $d$-wave altermagnets, where current-induced torques vanish in the bulk, staggered effective fields can nevertheless exist as an interfacial response, whose allowed tensor form is determined by the surface antisymmetry subgroup for the given surface orientation. Separately, the structure of the spin conductivity tensor determines which surface orientations allow transverse spin current generation via the spin-splitter effect. Taken together, these symmetry-enforced properties establish which surface orientations of $d$-wave altermagnets can serve as deterministically switchable spin current sources in spin-torque heterostructures. Because the design rules are based solely on the surface antisymmetry point group, the required staggered axial response is robust against averaging over symmetry-equivalent surface facets and equilibrium roughness.

### [32] [Predictive Coding Graphs are a Superset of Feedforward Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06142)
*Björn van Zwol*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文证明预测编码图（PCGs）构成了前馈人工神经网络（多层感知机）的数学超集，从而将预测编码网络更牢固地定位在当代机器学习框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测编码图（predictive coding graphs, PCGs）作为预测编码网络（predictive coding networks）的推广，是一种受神经科学启发的概率潜变量模型。本文旨在阐明PCGs与主流机器学习模型的关系，特别是与前馈人工神经网络（feedforward artificial neural networks）的数学联系。

Method: 通过数学证明方法，论证预测编码图（PCGs）构成了前馈人工神经网络（multilayer perceptrons）的数学超集（mathematical superset）。该方法从理论层面建立了两种模型之间的包含关系。

Result: 证明了预测编码图（PCGs）定义了一个数学超集，包含了前馈人工神经网络（多层感知机）。这一结果将预测编码网络更紧密地定位在当代机器学习（contemporary machine learning, ML）框架内。

Conclusion: 该研究强化了先前关于使用非层次神经网络（non-hierarchical neural networks）进行机器学习任务的提议，并更广泛地支持了神经网络拓扑结构（topology in neural networks）概念的研究价值。

Abstract: Predictive coding graphs (PCGs) are a recently introduced generalization to predictive coding networks, a neuroscience-inspired probabilistic latent variable model. Here, we prove how PCGs define a mathematical superset of feedforward artificial neural networks (multilayer perceptrons). This positions PCNs more strongly within contemporary machine learning (ML), and reinforces earlier proposals to study the use of non-hierarchical neural networks for ML tasks, and more generally the notion of topology in neural networks.

</details>


### [33] [A recipe for scalable attention-based MLIPs: unlocking long-range accuracy with all-to-all node attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06567)
*Eric Qu,Brandon M. Wood,Aditi S. Krishnapriyan,Zachary W. Ulissi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出AllScAIP模型，采用基于注意力机制（attention-based）和能量守恒（energy-conserving）的设计，通过数据驱动的全节点注意力（all-to-all node attention）组件处理长程相互作用问题，模型可扩展到1亿（O(100 million)）训练样本规模。

Result: 模型在分子系统上达到最先进的能量/力预测精度，在基于物理的评估（OMol25）中表现优异，在材料（OMat24）和催化剂（OC20）系统上具有竞争力。能够进行稳定、长时间尺度的分子动力学模拟，准确恢复实验观测值，包括密度和汽化热预测。

Conclusion: 在低数据/小模型情况下，归纳偏置（inductive biases）能提高样本效率，但随着数据和模型规模扩大，这些优势减弱甚至反转。全节点注意力对于捕捉长程相互作用至关重要，AllScAIP为大规模系统提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have advanced rapidly, with many top models relying on strong physics-based inductive biases. However, as models scale to larger systems like biomolecules and electrolytes, they struggle to accurately capture long-range (LR) interactions, leading current approaches to rely on explicit physics-based terms or components. In this work, we propose AllScAIP, a straightforward, attention-based, and energy-conserving MLIP model that scales to O(100 million) training samples. It addresses the long-range challenge using an all-to-all node attention component that is data-driven. Extensive ablations reveal that in low-data/small-model regimes, inductive biases improve sample efficiency. However, as data and model size scale, these benefits diminish or even reverse, while all-to-all attention remains critical for capturing LR interactions. Our model achieves state-of-the-art energy/force accuracy on molecular systems, as well as a number of physics-based evaluations (OMol25), while being competitive on materials (OMat24) and catalysts (OC20). Furthermore, it enables stable, long-timescale MD simulations that accurately recover experimental observables, including density and heat of vaporization predictions.

### [34] [Shape-Independent Fluidization in Epithelial Cell Monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05548)
*Pradip K. Bera,Anh Q. Nguyen,Molly McCord,Dapeng Bi,Jacob Notbohm*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了上皮组织流体化的几何框架，发现了一种与细胞形状无关的流体化模式。降低细胞间粘附会显著增加流动性，但细胞形状、密度等参数保持不变，揭示了当前顶点模型的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织流动性调控胚胎发育、伤口愈合和癌症转移等关键生物过程。传统范式认为，在细胞填充分数固定的汇合上皮中，固体样阻塞态与流体样非阻塞态之间的转变由几何细胞形状指数决定，该指数受皮质张力与细胞间粘附平衡调控。

Method: 研究通过实验观察上皮单层中降低细胞-细胞粘附（cell-cell adhesion）对流动性的影响，发现流体化发生时细胞形状、细胞密度、基底牵引力和连接线张力均无变化。为解释这一现象，扩展了理论框架以考虑粘附的双重性质。

Result: 实验显示降低细胞间粘附会触发流动性显著增加，但这一过程完全独立于细胞形状变化。形状与流动性的解耦表明，当前将粘附仅视为界面张力贡献的顶点模型（vertex models）是不完整的。

Conclusion: 扩展的理论框架同时考虑了粘附的热力学角色（设定细胞-细胞连接处的界面粘附能）和动力学角色（细胞滑动时产生粘性阻力）。这一广义模型定量捕捉了实验数据，证明粘附能量学与耗散摩擦的相互作用对于全面理解上皮流动性至关重要。

Abstract: Tissue fluidity regulates many critical biological processes, including embryonic development, wound healing, and cancer metastasis. In confluent epithelia, where cell packing fraction is effectively fixed, the prevailing paradigm postulates that transitions between solid-like jammed and fluid-like unjammed states are governed by a geometric cell shape index determined by the balance of cortical tension and intercellular adhesion. Here, we challenge this geometric framework by reporting a mode of fluidization in epithelial monolayers that is entirely shape-independent. We observe that reducing cell-cell adhesion triggers a substantial increase in fluidity, yet this occurs without any corresponding change in cell shape, cell density, substrate traction, or junctional line tension. This decoupling of shape and fluidity reveals that current vertex models, which treat adhesion solely as a contribution to interfacial tension, are incomplete. To reconcile these findings, we extend the theoretical framework to account for the dual nature of adhesion -- its thermodynamic role in setting interfacial adhesion energy at the cell-cell junctions and its kinetic role in generating viscous drag as cells slide past their neighbors. This generalized model quantitatively captures the experimental data, demonstrating that the interplay between adhesive energetics and dissipative friction is essential for a complete understanding of epithelial fluidity.

### [35] [Network-based drug repurposing for MYH9-related nephritis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06112)
*Muhammed Ali,Tommaso Gili,Guido Caldarelli*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究采用网络理论方法分析MYH9导向药物库在化学空间中的组织模式，通过多描述符框架揭示了化合物库的高度模块化结构，并识别出结构核心与描述符平衡的关键化合物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在利用网络理论工具分析药物库在化学空间中的组织模式，通过多描述符框架理解化合物库的结构特性，为虚拟筛选和药物发现提供统计验证的网络表示。

Method: 从ZINC数据库选取6004个分子，经预处理获得5000个结构有效且描述符完整的化合物。使用Tanimoto距离计算Morgan指纹相似度，并计算xLogP、HBD、HBA、分子量和可旋转键等单描述符距离。为每种表示构建k-最近邻网络，并应用Louvain-Leiden算法识别社区。

Result: 所有网络均表现出高度显著的模块性（Q=0.91-0.99），表明跨描述符存在明显的非随机化学组织。通过1250万分子对的共聚类矩阵量化跨描述符稳健性，发现稀疏的高共识核心。最小生成树分析揭示了不同的骨架拓扑：支架驱动的稀疏结构与紧凑的枢纽丰富的共识网络。

Conclusion: 研究提供了化学空间的统计验证网络表示，并提出了提取共识稳定化合物的原则性策略，这些化合物既具有结构中心性又保持描述符平衡，适用于下游筛选。

Abstract: Using tools from network theory, we analyze the organization of a MYH9-oriented drug-like library in chemical space using a multi-descriptor framework. The dataset is drawn from ZINC, a publicly available database of commercially accessible compounds curated for virtual screening and drug discovery. Starting from 6004 molecules, preprocessing yields 5000 structurally valid and descriptor-complete compounds. Similarity is defined via Tanimoto distance on Morgan fingerprints and single-descriptor distances for xLogP, HBD, HBA, molecular weight, and rotatable bonds. For each representation, we construct k-nearest-neighbor networks and identify communities using the Louvain-Leiden algorithm. All networks exhibit highly significant modularity (Q=0.91-0.99) relative to degree-preserving null models, demonstrating pronounced nonrandom chemical organization across descriptors. Cross-descriptor robustness is quantified through a co-clustering matrix over 1.25 X 10^7 molecular pairs, measuring how consistently compound pairs co-occur within the same community across descriptor-specific networks. Although most pairs show limited agreement, a sparse high-consensus core emerges, highlighting the complementarity of the descriptors. Minimum spanning trees derived from structural and consensus similarities reveal distinct backbone topologies: a scaffold-driven, sparse structure versus a compact, hub-rich consensus network. Betweenness centrality on these backbones identifies compounds that are both structurally central and descriptor-balanced. These results provide a statistically validated network representation of chemical space and a principled strategy to extract consensus-stable compounds for downstream screening.

### [36] [Continuum field theory of matchgate tensor network ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06202)
*Maksimilian Usoltcev,Carolin Wille,Jens Eisert,Alexander Altland*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究建立了二维费米子匹配门（matchgate）张量网络随机系综的连续场论描述，揭示了无序驱动的普适长程行为对应于具有拓扑项的D类非线性σ模型，建立了随机匹配门网络与热量子霍尔问题的直接对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量网络为量子多体系统提供了离散表示，但其与连续场论的精确联系仍相对缺乏理解。研究旨在通过典型性（typicality）概念，为具有空间涨落参数的二维费米子匹配门张量网络随机系综建立连续描述。

Method: 采用典型性概念，分析费米子两点函数的无序平均矩（disorder-averaged moments），在平坦几何和双曲圆盘两种几何结构中进行研究，其中曲率重塑了长距离结构。

Result: 无序驱动了由具有拓扑项的D类非线性σ模型（nonlinear sigma-model of symmetry class D）支配的普适长程行为，将随机匹配门网络与热量子霍尔问题直接对应。所得相结构包括局域化相、量子霍尔临界性以及具有扩散关联和自发复本对称性破缺的鲁棒热金属相。

Conclusion: 典型性为从离散张量网络系综到连续量子场论提供了一条路径。弱非高斯形变将对称性约化为离散置换，产生Goldstone模质量，并抑制长程关联。

Abstract: Tensor networks provide discrete representations of quantum many-body systems, yet their precise connection to continuum field theories remains relatively poorly understood. Invoking a notion of typicality, we develop a continuum description for random ensembles of two-dimensional fermionic matchgate tensor networks with spatially fluctuating parameters. As a diagnostic of the resulting universal physics, we analyze disorder-averaged moments of fermionic two-point functions, both in flat geometry and on a hyperbolic disk, where curvature reshapes their long-distance structure. We show that disorder drives universal long-distance behavior governed by a nonlinear sigma-model of symmetry class D with a topological term, placing random matchgate networks in direct correspondence with the thermal quantum Hall problem. The resulting phase structure includes localized phases, quantum Hall criticality, and a robust thermal metal with diffusive correlations and spontaneous replica-symmetry breaking. Weak non-Gaussian deformations reduce the symmetry to discrete permutations, generate a mass for the Goldstone modes, and suppress long-range correlations. In this way, typicality offers a route from ensembles of discrete tensor networks to continuum quantum field theories.

### [37] [Ultra-slow orbital and spin dynamics in an electrically tunable quantum dot molecule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05610)
*Christopher Thalacker,Michelle Lienhart,Markus Stöcker,Nadeem Akhlaq,Irina Ivanova,Nikolai Bart,Arne Ludwig,Johannes Schall,Stephan Reitzenstein,Dirk Reuter,Steffen Wilksen,Christopher Gies,Krzysztof Gawarecki,Paweł Machnikowski,Kai Müller,Jonathan Finley*

TL;DR: 该研究展示了隧道耦合量子点分子（QDMs）中单电子和双电子自旋态的光学制备与调控，实现了超过100μs的长自旋-三重态弛豫时间，证实了QDMs在零磁场下通过可调自旋交换耦合和光学驱动创建多维光子簇态的潜力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用静态电场广泛调节轨道耦合，同时通过光学驱动实现量子光产生。通过光学泵浦（optical pumping）初始化单自旋和双自旋态，并探索轨道和自旋弛豫动力学随能量失谐（energy detuning）和轨道态杂化（hybridization）的变化。

Conclusion: 研究结果为单自旋和双自旋态动力学提供了新的定量理解，并证实了QDMs通过利用零磁场下可调自旋-自旋交换耦合（spin-spin exchange couplings）结合光学驱动来创建多维光子簇态（multidimensional photonic cluster states）的适用性。

Abstract: Tunnel-coupled optically active quantum dot molecules (QDMs), have the potential to operate as spin-photon-interfaces with coupled spins that interact with two different photon frequencies at the same time. A prerequisite is to deterministically prepare two (electron or hole) spins in the QDM and be able to electrically tune the orbital state couplings. Here, we demonstrate the sequential optical charging of a single QDM with two electron spins while simultaneously maintaining the ability to widely tune orbital couplings using static electric fields and optically drive the system for quantum light generation. We optically prepare one- and two-spin states, initialize via optical pumping and explore orbital and spin relaxation dynamics for one and two-spin states as a function of the energy detuning and hybridization of orbital states. For two-spin states, remarkably long S-T relaxation times are observed extending beyond $\sim 100μs$ with strong dependence on the relative energy of ground and excited two-spin states. Qualitative agreement is observed with $\mathbf{k \cdot p}$ calculations of phonon-mediated spin-relaxation. Our results provide new quantitative understanding of the dynamics of one and two-spin states and confirm their suitability of QDMs for creating multidimensional photonic cluster states by exploiting tunable spin-spin exchange couplings at zero magnetic fields combined with optical driving.

### [38] [Efficiently gate-tunable ferromagnetism in ferromagnetic semiconductor-Dirac semimetal p-n heterojunctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05770)
*Emma Steinebronn,Saurav Islam,Abhinava Chatterjee,Bimal Neupane,Alex Grutter,Christopher Jensen,Julie A. Borchers,Timothy Charlton,Wilson J. Yanez-Parreno,Juan Chamorro,Tanya Berry,Supriya Ghosh,K. A. Nivedith,K. Andre Mkhoyan,Tyrel McQueen,Yuanxi Wang,Chaoxing Liu,Nitin Samarth*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究利用分子束外延技术制备了可栅极调控的p-n异质结，该异质结由狄拉克半金属Cd₃As₂和具有垂直磁各向异性的铁磁半导体In₁₋ₓMnₓAs组成。通过反常霍尔效应测量发现，铁磁居里温度（T_C）可通过约10V的栅压有效调控，对应电场灵敏度约为10K/MV/cm。这种非单调调控行为表明狄拉克半金属与铁磁半导体之间存在相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种新型异质结平台，用于探索对称性破缺、拓扑性和磁性之间的相互作用。通过结合狄拉克半金属（Cd₃As₂）和铁磁半导体（In₁₋ₓMnₓAs），为研究拓扑半金属中的涌现现象（emergent phenomena）提供潜在平台。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）技术制备栅极可调谐的p-n异质结。通过测量顶栅（top-gated）Cd₃As₂/In₁₋ₓMnₓAs器件的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect），研究铁磁居里温度（Curie temperature, T_C）的电场调控特性。

Result: 实验发现铁磁居里温度可通过约10V的栅压有效调控，对应电场灵敏度ΔT_C/ΔE约为10K/MV/cm。T_C的电压调控在Cd₃As₂的电荷中性点（charge neutrality point）附近达到饱和，并在适当设计的异质结构中于正栅压下消失。这种非单调行为无法仅用In₁₋ₓMnₓAs中的空穴介导铁磁性（hole-mediated ferromagnetism）解释。

Conclusion: Cd₃As₂/In₁₋ₓMnₓAs异质结中T_C的非单调电场调控表明狄拉克半金属与铁磁半导体之间存在相互作用。该异质结为研究对称性破缺（broken symmetry）、拓扑性和磁性在拓扑半金属中的相互作用提供了一个有吸引力的平台。

Abstract: We use molecular beam epitaxy to develop a gate tunable p-n heterojunction that interfaces a canonical Dirac semimetal, Cd$_3$As$_2$, and a ferromagnetic semiconductor, In$_{1-x}$Mn$_x$As, with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy. Measurements of the anomalous Hall effect in top-gated Cd$_3$As$_2$/In$_{1-x}$Mn$_x$As devices show that the ferromagnetic Curie temperature ($T_\mathrm{C}$) can be efficiently tuned using a modest gate voltage of $\sim 10$ V, corresponding to a sensitivity to electric field ($E$) of $ΔT_{\mathrm{C}}/ΔE \sim 10$ K/MV/cm). The voltage tuning of $T_\mathrm{C}$ saturates near the charge neutrality point of Cd$_3$As$_2$ and vanishes at positive gate voltage in appropriately designed heterostructures. This non-monotonic behavior cannot be explained solely by hole-mediated ferromagnetism in the In$_{1-x}$Mn$_x$As alone, suggesting an interaction between the Dirac semimetal and the ferromagnetic semiconductor. Our results identify Cd$_3$As$_2$/In$_{1-x}$Mn$_x$As heterojunctions as a potentially attractive platform for studying emergent phenomena arising from the interplay between broken symmetry, topology, and magnetism in a topological semimetal.

### [39] [Influence of Hopping Integrals and Spin-Orbit Coupling on Quantum Oscillations in Kagome Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05816)
*Xinlong Du,Yuying Liu,Chao Wang,Juntao Song*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受CsTi$_3$Bi$_5$和RbTi$_3$Bi$_5$实验结果的启发，研究旨在理解kagome晶格模型中跃迁积分和自旋轨道耦合对量子振荡的影响，特别是解释两种材料不同的拓扑响应特征。

Method: 采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding models）研究kagome晶格，重点分析次近邻跃迁项$t_2$和自旋轨道耦合的作用，通过讨论磁击穿（magnetic breakdown）机制来解释量子振荡特征。

Result: 当$t_2=0$时，相邻能带间的小杂化间隙允许磁击穿发生，掩盖了本征拓扑特性；当$t_2\neq0$时，杂化间隙显著增大，抑制磁击穿，揭示出非平庸贝里相位（Berry phase $\phi_B\approx\pi$）。

Conclusion: 次近邻跃迁项$t_2$是调控CsTi$_3$Bi$_5$和RbTi$_3$Bi$_5$中拓扑相实验可观测性的关键参数，表明通过调节晶格参数可以有效控制量子输运中的拓扑特征。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experiments on CsTi$_3$Bi$_5$ and RbTi$_3$Bi$_5$~[Rehfuss \textit{et al.}, Phys.\ Rev.\ Mater.\ \textbf{8}, 024003 (2024)], we theoretically investigate the effects of hopping integrals and spin-orbit coupling (SOC) on quantum oscillations in kagome lattice models. Our tight-binding models successfully capture the distinct quantum oscillation features observed in experiments, when a relatively strong SOC is included. It is more important that, by discussing the effect of the next-nearest-neighbor term $t_2$, we provide a coherent explanation for their different topological responses. For the case of $t_2 = 0$, the small hybridization gap between adjacent bands with opposite Berry curvatures allows magnetic breakdown to occur under a strong magnetic field, enabling charge carriers to tunnel between the bands and thereby effectively masking the intrinsic topological character. In contrast, for $t_2 \neq 0$, the hybridization gap is significantly enlarged by $t_2$, which suppresses magnetic breakdown and confines electrons to individual orbits with opposite Berry curvatures, thereby revealing the nontrivial Berry phase ($φ_B \approx π$). Consequently, we identify the lattice-driven hopping $t_2$ as a critical control parameter that regulates the experimental observability of the topological phase in CsTi$_3$Bi$_5$ and RbTi$_3$Bi$_5$. These findings underscore the key role of the $t_2$ term and show that tuning lattice parameters can effectively control topological signatures in quantum transport.

### [40] [Triple Antidot Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05891)
*Naomi Mizuno,Dmitri V. Averin,Xu Du*

### [45] [Universal Dynamical Scaling of Strong-to-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking in Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06363)
*Chang Shu,Kai Zhang,Kai Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究一维开放量子系统中强到弱自发对称破缺（SWSSB）的涌现动力学，发现其晚期时间标度由Lindbladian的对称性类别而非Liouvillian谱结构决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强到弱自发对称破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking, SWSSB）在一维开放量子系统中的动力学涌现，该相变在混合态中具有非线性可观测量（如Rényi-2关联子）的长程有序，而传统线性关联保持短程。

Method: 通过追踪Rényi-2关联长度的晚期时间增长，分析Lindbladian演化控制的一维开放量子系统，研究不同对称性类别（$\mathbb{Z}_2$和U(1)）下的动力学标度行为。

Result: 发现SWSSB转变的时间依赖性（指数型与代数型）完全由对称性决定：$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称动力学中Rényi-2关联长度随时间指数增长（即使谱无隙），而U(1)对称动力学显示代数标度，填充依赖的动力学指数从有限填充的弹道增长过渡到零填充极限的扩散标度。

Abstract: Strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SWSSB) defines a mixed-state phase of matter--without a pure-state counterpart--in which nonlinear observables such as the Rényi-2 correlator develop long-range order while conventional linear correlations remain short-ranged. Here we study the emergence of SWSSB in one-dimensional open quantum systems governed by Lindbladian evolution, where the transition time diverges with system size and SWSSB appears only asymptotically in the steady state. By tracking the late-time growth of the Rényi-2 correlation length, we uncover a universal dynamical regime controlled purely by the symmetry class of the Lindbladian. Contrary to the conventional expectation that late-time dynamics are governed by the low-lying Liouvillian spectrum, we find that the time dependence of the SWSSB transition--exponential versus algebraic--is dictated solely by symmetry, independent of details of the Lindbladian, including whether the Liouvillian spectrum is gapped or gapless. For $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric dynamics, the Rényi-2 correlation length grows exponentially in time--even when the spectrum is gapless--yielding an effective transition time $t_c \propto \operatorname{ln} L$ and enabling rapid preparation of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ SWSSB steady state. In contrast, U(1)-symmetric dynamics exhibit algebraic scaling, $t_c \propto L^α$, with a filling-dependent dynamical exponent: ballistic growth ($α\approx 1$) at finite filling crosses over to diffusive scaling ($α= 2$) in the zero-filling limit. These results establish symmetry--rather than spectral gap structure--as the controlling principle for SWSSB late-time dynamical scaling, and open a new route to nonequilibrium symmetry breaking in open quantum systems.

### [46] [Linearly Polarized Light-Induced Anomalous Hall Effect and Topological Phase Transitions in an Altermagnetic Topological Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06486)
*Yichen Liu,Tongshuai Zhu,Haijun Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过周期驱动的线性偏振光（LPL）调控交变磁体（AMs）拓扑绝缘体，发现交变磁体与传统反铁磁体（AFMs）对LPL的响应截然不同：LPL可在交变磁体中诱导反常霍尔效应（AHE）并驱动其进入完全自旋极化的陈绝缘体相，而传统反铁磁体则无此响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets, AMs）作为一种具有零净磁化但展现非常规自旋分裂的新型共线磁序，其非常规自旋分裂及相关能带拓扑的控制为实现新颖的自旋和拓扑输运现象提供了机遇。本研究旨在探索利用周期性驱动的线性偏振光（LPL）对交变磁体拓扑绝缘体进行光诱导控制。

Method: 采用弗洛凯工程（Floquet engineering）方法，利用周期性驱动的线性偏振光（LPL）对交变磁体系统进行调控。通过分析LPL对时间反演对称性（$\mathcal{T}$）和宇称-时间反演对称性（$\mathcal{PT}$）的破坏作用，研究交变磁体与传统反铁磁体（AFMs）在光场下的不同响应。

Result: 研究发现交变磁体与传统反铁磁体在LPL照射下表现出截然不同的响应：由于LPL既不破坏时间反演对称性也不破坏宇称-时间反演对称性，它无法在传统反铁磁体中产生自旋分裂或诱导反常霍尔效应（AHE）。相反，交变磁体本身缺乏这两种对称性，其自旋向上和自旋向下能带通过时间反演与晶体旋转的联合对称性相关联，LPL能够破坏这些对称性，从而在交变磁体中触发有限的反常霍尔效应。此外，LPL可将交变磁体拓扑绝缘体驱动进入完全自旋极化的陈绝缘体（Chern insulating）相。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅为区分交变磁体与传统反铁磁体提供了可靠的实验方案，而且为无耗散自旋电子学应用开辟了一条有前景的途径。研究结果揭示了交变磁体在光场调控下的独特拓扑响应特性。

Abstract: A recently identified class of collinear magnetic order, characterized by vanishing net magnetization yet unconventional spin splitting, known as altermagnets (AMs), has attracted significant research interest. Controlling the unconventional spin splitting and the associated band topology in AMs offers opportunities for realizing novel spin and topological transport phenomena. In this work, using Floquet engineering with periodically driven linearly polarized light (LPL), we explore light-induced control of an AM topological insulator. Remarkably, we find that AMs and conventional antiferromagnets (AFMs) exhibit distinct responses under LPL irradiation. Specifically, since LPL breaks neither time-reversal ($\mathcal{T}$) symmetry nor parity-time-reversal ($\mathcal{PT}$) symmetry, it is incapable of generating spin splitting or inducing an anomalous Hall effect (AHE) in conventional AFMs. In contrast, AMs intrinsically lack both $\mathcal{T}$ and $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetries. Their spin-up and spin-down bands are related by the combined symmetry of time reversal $\mathcal{T}$ and a crystal rotation. We show that LPL readily breaks these symmetries, thereby triggering a finite AHE exclusively in AMs. Furthermore, LPL can drive the AM topological insulator into a fully spin-polarized Chern insulating phase. Our findings not only provide a robust experimental scheme to distinguish AMs from conventional AFMs, but also establish a promising pathway toward dissipationless spintronic applications.

### [47] [Altermagnets Enable Gate-Switchable Helical and Chiral Topological Transport with Spin-Valley-Momentum-Locked Dual Protection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06487)
*Xianzhang Chen,Jiayong Zhang,Bowen Hao,Jiahui Qian,Ziye Zhu,Igor Zutic,Zhenyu Zhang,Tong Zhou*

Abstract: We establish a unified, symmetry-driven framework that combines the alternating spin splitting of altermagnets with valley topology to realize and electrically interconvert helical and chiral topological phases within a single material platform. Large-scale quantum transport simulations show these SVML edge states exhibit fully quantized spin conductance robust against nonmagnetic and long-range magnetic disorder, reflecting their dual topological protection, while remaining vulnerable to short-range magnetic disorder. Exploiting that the counterpropagating SVML modes are linked by crystal rotation symmetry, we introduce a gate-tunable sublattice-staggered potential that selectively gaps one valley and converts the helical state into a chiral quantum anomalous Hall phase with Csv = 1, robust against all disorder types. Reversing the potential switches the transmitted spin-valley polarization. Our first-principles calculations identify monolayer V2STeO and VO families as realistic platforms supporting both helical and chiral topological phases and their electrical switching. These results establish altermagnets as electrically programmable platforms for robust topological devices across charge, spin, and valley.

Motivation: 理解局部结构有序性如何调控电子关联效应对于揭示二维磁体中涌现行为的微观机制至关重要。Fe₅₋ₓGeTe₂中的本征Fe位点无序为探究这种相互作用提供了天然平台。

Method: 结合高分辨扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）与密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，建立了Fe位点有序性与局部电子结构之间的直接原子尺度关联。

Result: STM识别出两种共存表面相：与有序Fe(1)构型相关的√3×√3超结构，以及Fe(1)缺失区域中未畸变的1×1六方Te晶格。√3有序畴呈现金属行为，而Fe(1)空缺区域在费米能级附近显示抑制态密度（DOS），表明存在赝能隙电子态。第一性原理计算揭示Fe 3d与Te 5p轨道对称允许的杂化重构了低能电子结构。

Conclusion: 这些结果为范德华磁体中原子尺度结构有序性与纳米尺度电子不均匀性之间的联系提供了微观框架，表明Fe位点有序性驱动的电子相分离是理解该体系电子性质的关键机制。

Abstract: Understanding how local structural order governs electronic correlations is essential for revealing the microscopic mechanism underlying emergent behavior in two-dimensional magnets. In the layered van der Waals ferromagnet Fe\textsubscript{5-x}GeTe\textsubscript{2}, intrinsic Fe-site disorder provides a natural platform to probe this interplay. Here, we establish a direct atomic scale correlation between Fe-site ordering and local electronic structure by combining high-resolution scanning tunneling microscopy with density functional theory calculations. Scanning tunneling microscopy resolves two coexisting surface phases, a $\sqrt{3} \times \sqrt{3}$ superstructure associated with ordered Fe(1) configurations and an undistorted $1 \times 1$ hexagonal Te lattice in Fe(1)-deficient regions. Spatially resolved spectroscopy shows that the $\sqrt{3}$-ordered domains exhibit metallic behavior, whereas Fe(1) vacant areas display a suppressed density of states(DOS) near the Fermi level, indicative of pseudogapped electronic states. The nanoscale coexistence of these distinct electronic responses provides direct evidence of electronic phase separation driven by Fe-site ordering. First-principles calculations reveal that symmetry allowed hybridization between Fe 3d and Te 5p orbitals reconstructs the low-energy electronic structure, giving rise to the contrasting tunneling signatures of ordered and disordered phases. Bias-dependent local DOS simulations reproduce the experimentally observed contrast evolution and reveal that hybridization induced out of plane orbital character governs the spatial modulation of tunneling conductance. These results provide a microscopic framework linking atomic-scale structural order to nanoscale electronic inhomogeneity in van der Waals magnets.

</details>
