### [49] [Operational Emergence of a Global Phase under Time-Dependent Coupling in Oscillator Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05668)
*Veronica Sanz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个操作性涌现标准，用于判断振荡器网络中宏观相位何时具有操作意义，分析了时变耦合下的同步动力学，发现了协议速率与冻结效应之间的竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨振荡器网络中全局相位Ψ何时具有操作意义（operationally well-defined），特别是在时变耦合条件下。传统上使用复序参量$R e^{iΨ}$描述集体同步，但未明确说明Ψ在何种条件下真正成为有意义的宏观坐标。

Method: 研究方法包括：提出操作性涌现标准，通过规范固定相位滞后波动量化相位可估计性；使用拉普拉斯模式约简（Laplacian-mode reduction）分析相干态附近的动力学；数值提取操作性冻结时间（operational freeze-out time）并分析谱协议参数（spectral protocol parameter）$λ_2τ$。

Result: 研究结果表明：宏观相位的涌现由$NR^2$控制；非自治耦合引入的斜坡时间尺度与弛豫竞争，当$K(t)λ_2$主导斜坡速率时有序化跟踪协议，而快速斜坡导致冻结；在非空间网络中，冻结时的残余非相干性相对于谱协议参数$λ_2τ$呈现坍缩行为。

Conclusion: 结论指出：在周期晶格上，拓扑扇区（topological sectors）和缺陷介导的有序化阻碍完全对齐，导致协议依赖的长寿命部分同步态，并出现相对于谱坍缩的系统性偏差。

Abstract: Collective synchronization is often summarized by a complex order parameter $R e^{iΨ}$, implicitly treating the global phase $Ψ$ as a meaningful macroscopic coordinate. Here we ask when $Ψ$ becomes \emph{operationally well-defined} in oscillator networks whose coupling varies in time. We study damped (and optionally inertial) phase-oscillator models on graphs with time-dependent coupling $K(t)$, covering standard Kuramoto dynamics as a limit and including network and spatial topologies relevant to engineered settings.
  We propose an operational emergence criterion: a macroscopic phase is emergent only when it is robustly estimable, which we quantify via gauge-fixed phase-lag fluctuations under weak noise and finite sampling. This yields a quantitative threshold controlled by $NR^2$ and makes explicit why $Ψ$ is ill-posed in incoherent states even when formally definable. Nonautonomous coupling introduces a ramp timescale that competes with relaxation. Using a Laplacian-mode reduction near coherence, we derive a graph-spectral rate criterion: ordering tracks the protocol when $K(t)λ_2$ dominates the ramp rate, while faster ramps induce freeze-out. Numerically, we extract an operational freeze-out time from an energy-based tracking diagnostic and show that, for non-spatial networks, the residual incoherence at freeze-out collapses when plotted against the spectral protocol parameter $λ_2τ$ across Erdős--Rényi and small-world graph families. Finally, on periodic lattices we show that topological sectors and defect-mediated ordering obstruct complete alignment, leading to protocol-dependent, long-lived partially synchronized states and systematic deviations from spectral collapse.

</details>


### [50] [Critical dynamics govern the evolution of political regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05994)
*Joshua Uhlig,Paula Pirker-Díaz,Matthew Wilson,Ralf Metzler,Karoline Wiesner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了全球民主系统的兴衰动态，发现政治体制演化呈现弱非遍历性（weakly non-ergodic）特征，在由民主多样性数据集构建的二维体制空间中，稳定性盆地（basins of stability）稀疏且漂移，体制变迁遵循重尾分布（heavy-tailed distributions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球民主系统的兴起与衰退引发了关于政治变革动态的基本问题。与自由主义民主作为稳定终点的观念相反，近期向非民主体制的回潮凸显了体制演化的非平稳性（non-stationary nature）。

Method: 研究基于民主多样性（Varieties of Democracy）数据集的主成分分析构建了二维体制空间，分析各国在该空间中的历史轨迹。采用连续时间随机游走模型（continuous time random walk model）来模拟近三十年的动态。

Result: 观察到弱非遍历性动态在有效景观中展开，其特征是稀疏且漂移的稳定性盆地。在临界体制附近，描述该动态的步长和停留时间遵循重尾分布，均值似乎发散。连续时间随机游走模型能够以显著精度再现最近三十年的动态。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，政治体制演化的某些方面遵循普遍的随机原则，同时仍受到独特历史路径的间断性影响。体制变迁动态具有间歇性和异质性特征。

Abstract: The emergence and decline of democratic systems worldwide raises fundamental questions about the dynamics of political change. Contrary to the idea of a stable endpoint of liberal democracy, recent backsliding towards less democratic regimes highlights the non-stationary nature of regime evolution. Here, we analyse the historical trajectories of countries within a two-dimensional regime space derived from the principal components of the Varieties of Democracy dataset. We observe weakly non-ergodic dynamics unfolding in an effective landscape characterised by sparse and shifting basins of stability. Step sizes and sojourn times characterising this dynamics follow heavy-tailed distributions near the critical regime, in which mean values appear to diverge. These facts point to the intermittent and heterogeneous nature of the regime change dynamics. A continuous time random walk model reproduces the dynamics of the three most recent decades with remarkable accuracy. Together, these results suggest that some aspects of political regime evolution follow universal stochastic principles, while remaining punctuated by unique historical pathways.

</details>


### [51] [Dynamical scaling method improved by a deep learning approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06008)
*Yusuke Terasawa,Yukiyasu Ozeki*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度学习的改进型动力学标度分析方法，相比传统高斯过程回归，该方法显著降低了计算成本并提高了精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动力学标度分析中广泛使用的高斯过程回归（Gaussian process regression）在参数优化时计算成本较高，尤其处理大规模数据集时成为限制因素。因此需要开发更高效的计算方法。

Method: 本文采用神经网络（neural network）替代高斯过程回归，显著降低了计算成本，并能够利用传统方法无法处理的完整数据集。该方法应用于二维伊辛模型（2D Ising model）和二维三态波茨模型（2D 3-state Potts model）。

Result: 相比传统方法，该深度学习改进方法实现了更高的精度和计算效率。神经网络方法能够处理之前高斯过程回归无法访问的完整数据集。

Conclusion: 基于深度学习的动力学标度分析方法在计算成本和精度方面均优于传统高斯过程回归方法，为处理大规模数据集提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: We propose a dynamical scaling analysis improved by a deep learning approach. While Gaussian process regression has been widely employed for estimating scaling parameters, its computational cost for parameter optimization becomes a limitation in dynamical scaling analysis, where large datasets are involved. In contrast, the present method employs a neural network, which significantly reduces the computational cost and enables the use of the entire dataset that was inaccessible with Gaussian process regression. We applied the method to the 2D Ising model and the 2D 3-state Potts model, achieving higher accuracy and computational efficiency than conventional approaches.

</details>


### [52] [Absolute negative mobility in a one-dimensional overdamped system driven by active fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06070)
*K. Białas,P. Hänggi,J. Spiechowicz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明绝对负迁移率（absolute negative mobility, ANM）可在更简单的过阻尼系统中实现，仅需分段线性对称周期势和白泊松冲击噪声（white Poisson shot noise）驱动的主动涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝对负迁移率（absolute negative mobility, ANM）是一种反常输运现象，传统认为其最小实现需要惯性粒子在非平衡非稳态下受恒定偏置。本研究旨在降低系统复杂度，探索在更简单的过阻尼平衡态系统中实现ANM的可能性。

Method: 研究采用过阻尼粒子在分段线性对称周期势（piecewise linear symmetric periodic potential）中的系统，该系统处于平衡态，但受到白泊松冲击噪声（white Poisson shot noise）形式的主动涨落驱动。

Result: 研究显著降低了ANM现象的复杂度要求，证明在过阻尼平衡态系统中，仅需分段线性势和主动涨落驱动即可实现绝对负迁移率效应。

Conclusion: 该发现有助于解释生物细胞中出现的反常输运行为，其中动力学通常为过阻尼且受代谢活动产生的主动涨落辅助。同时，该机制可用于微观世界的有效分离策略，将涨落从干扰转化为功能资源。

Abstract: Absolute negative mobility (ANM) is one of the most paradoxical transport phenomena in which a setup moves on average in a direction opposite to the applied force. According to the state of the art a minimal system exhibiting this effect in a one-dimensional dynamics involves an inertial particle subjected to a constant bias when dwelling in a nonlinear symmetric periodic potential in a nonequilibrium} and nonstationary state generated by an external driving. In this work we remarkably reduce its complexity and show that it may occur in a system composed of an overdamped particle in piecewise linear symmetric periodic potential in an equilibrium state provided that it is driven by active fluctuations in the form of white Poisson shot noise. Our result may help to explain exotic transport behavior emerging in biological cells where dynamics is typically overdamped and assisted by active fluctuations derived from various metabolic activities. It can be also exploited for effective separation strategies in a microscopic world thus transforming fluctuations from a nuisance into a functional resource.

</details>


### [53] [Stochastic resonance in higher-order networks driven by colored noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06108)
*Zhongwen Bi,Dan Zhao,Qi Liu,Jürgen Kurths,Yong Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在有色噪声驱动下，包含成对耦合和2-单纯形耦合的过阻尼双稳态振子系统中的随机共振现象。研究发现高阶相互作用加剧了有色噪声对随机共振的抑制效应，降低了共振峰并改变了最优噪声强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索高阶相互作用（higher-order interactions）如何影响有色噪声（colored noise）驱动下耦合双稳态振子系统的随机共振（stochastic resonance）行为。传统研究多关注成对耦合，而高阶相互作用的影响机制尚不明确。

Method: 研究方法基于包含加权成对耦合和2-单纯形耦合（2-simplex coupling）的耦合过阻尼双稳态振子（coupled overdamped bistable oscillators）网络模型，该系统受到有色噪声驱动。通过分析网络同步水平（network synchronization level）的四阶段变化来阐明机制。

Result: 研究结果显示，高阶相互作用加剧了有色噪声对随机共振的抑制效应，表现为共振曲线峰值降低，最优噪声强度（optimal noise intensity）向更高值移动。同步极值（synchronization extremes）解释了高阶耦合和有色噪声对随机共振的影响机制。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，高阶相互作用不会逆转有色噪声引起的抑制效应，而是主要通过促进抑制效应的空间传播（spatial propagation）来加剧其对随机共振的负面影响。这为理解复杂网络中高阶相互作用对非线性响应的影响提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate stochastic resonance (SR) in an ensemble of coupled overdamped bistable oscillators driven by colored noise. The networks incorporate the weighted contributions of both pairwise coupling and 2-simplex coupling. Our findings show that these higher-order interactions further exacerbate the suppression effect of colored noise on SR, reducing the peak of resonance curves and shifting the optimal noise intensity toward higher values. To clarify the underlying mechanism, we establish a close connection between SR and the four-stage variation in network synchronization level. Specially, the synchronization extremes explain the effect of higher-order coupling and colored noise on SR. Our analysis reveals that higher-order interactions do not reverse, but primarily promote the spatial propagation of suppression effects due to colored noise.

</details>


### [54] [Floquet scars and prethermal fragmentation in a driven spin-one chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06111)
*Krishanu Ghosh,Diptiman Sen,K. Sengupta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了自旋-1链在方脉冲驱动下的周期动力学，发现了量子多体疤痕态（quantum many-body scar states）、遍历热化（ergodic thermalization）以及预热强希尔伯特空间碎片化（prethermal strong Hilbert space fragmentation）等多种动力学相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索具有大量Z_2守恒量的自旋链在周期驱动下的非平衡动力学行为，特别是研究不同驱动参数下系统的动力学相变和热化特性。

Method: 采用方脉冲驱动协议，通过分析具有固定W_ℓ值的特定扇区，结合解析和微扰理论分析，并利用精确对角化（exact-diagonalization, ED）方法对长度L≤24的有限链进行数值验证。

Result: 在W_ℓ=1扇区中，发现高驱动频率下存在量子多体疤痕态，导致振荡动力学和保真度恢复；降低频率时出现符合Floquet本征态热化假说的遍历热化。识别出特殊驱动频率ω_n^*和ω_n'，分别对应预热强希尔伯特空间碎片化和弱碎片化。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了周期驱动自旋链中丰富的动力学相，包括量子多体疤痕态、遍历热化以及不同强度的希尔伯特空间碎片化，为理解非平衡量子系统的热化行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the periodic dynamics of a spin-one chain driven using a square-pulse protocol with amplitude $Q_0$ and frequency $ω_D$. The Hamiltonian of the spin chain hosts a thermodynamically large number of $Z_2$-valued conserved quantities $W_{\ell}$ on the links $\ell$. This allows us to study the Floquet dynamics of this chain within a given sector with fixed values of $W_{\ell}$. For the sector with all $W_{\ell}=1$, we find signatures of quantum many-body scar states for $\hbar ω_D \gg Q_0$; they lead to oscillatory dynamics and fidelity revival for specific initial states. Upon lowering $ω_D$, we find an ergodic regime exhibiting fast thermalization consistent with the prediction of the (Floquet) eigenstate thermalization hypothesis. In addition, we identify special drive frequencies $ω_n^{\ast}= Q_0/(2n \hbar)$ (where $n = 1, 2, 3, \cdots$) at which the Floquet Hamiltonian exhibits prethermal strong Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF) with the largest fragment being ergodic; in contrast, a weak HSF is found at $ω'_n= Q_0/[\hbar(2n+1)]$ (where $n = 0, 1, 2, \cdots$). We also study the sector with $W_{\ell} =\{\cdots 1,1,-1,1,1,-1 \cdots \}$ which shows strong HSF at $ω_n^{\ast}$ but no fragmentation at $ω'_n$. Our analysis indicates that the strong HSF in this sector harbors an integrable largest fragment. We provide numerical support for our analytical and perturbative results using exact-diagonalization (ED) studies on finite chains of length $L\le 24$. Our numerical results for entanglement entropy, fidelity, and correlation functions of the driven chain provide definitive signatures of prethermal strong HSF for both sectors.

</details>


### [55] [Magnetoelastic signatures of thermal and quantum phase transitions in a deformable Ising chain under a longitudinal and transverse magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06125)
*David Sivy,Jozef Strecka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了可变形自旋-1/2伊辛链在纵向或横向磁场中的行为，通过磁弹性耦合机制统一描述了磁性和弹性性质，揭示了两种不同类型的相变：纵向磁场中的不连续热相变和横向磁场中的连续量子相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究可变形伊辛链（deformable spin-1/2 Ising chain）在磁场中的行为，旨在理解磁弹性耦合（magnetoelastic coupling）如何影响系统的磁性和弹性性质，特别是相变行为。

Method: 在谐波和静态绝热近似下，采用传递矩阵（transfer-matrix）和Jordan-Wigner费米子化（Jordan-Wigner fermionization）技术精确计算变分吉布斯自由能，然后对晶格畸变参数进行自洽最小化。

Result: 纵向磁场中的可变形伊辛链显示不连续热相变线，终止于临界点，伴随亚稳态和低温下的磁滞回线；横向磁场中则仅发生零温下的连续量子相变，无热相变迹象。

Conclusion: 磁弹性耦合系统在不同磁场配置下表现出截然不同的相变行为：纵向磁场导致不连续热相变，横向磁场引发连续量子相变，且弹性性质在相变点附近显著软化并伴随声衰减增强。

Abstract: We investigate a deformable spin-1/2 Ising chain subjected to either a longitudinal or a transverse magnetic field, which incorporates a magnetoelastic coupling linearly dependent on a lattice distortion parameter. Within the harmonic and static adiabatic approximations, the variational Gibbs free energy is evaluated exactly using transfer-matrix and Jordan-Wigner fermionization techniques and then minimized self-consistently with respect to the lattice distortion parameter. This approach enables a unified description of magnetic and elastic properties including the magnetization, magnetic susceptibility, lattice distortion, inverse compressibility, and relative change in the sound velocity. In a longitudinal magnetic field, the deformable Ising chain displays a line of discontinuous thermal phase transitions terminating at a critical point. The discontinuous transitions are accompanied by metastable states, which give rise to a hysteresis loop at low temperatures. In contrast, the deformable Ising chain in a transverse field undergoes exclusively a continuous quantum phase transition at zero temperature with no indication of thermal phase transitions. The magnetic susceptibility and inverse compressibility exhibit cusp- and dip-like anomalies at discontinuous phase transitions, while a diverging susceptibility and vanishing inverse compressibility characterize the continuous phase transitions. An elastic softening of the deformable chain near thermal and quantum phase transitions manifest itself also through a significant sound attenuation.

</details>


### [56] [Mean-Field Convective Phase Separation under Thermal Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06214)
*Meander Van den Brande,François Huveneers,Kyosuke Adachi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个动力学平均场模型，解释了温度梯度下吸引粒子系统如何形成周期性对流模式，通过线性稳定性分析和数值模拟揭示了稳态对流分离的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非平衡条件（nonequilibrium conditions）下系统相分离行为发生根本改变，温度梯度（temperature gradients）系统中吸引粒子会形成周期性模式和稳态对流，但缺乏明确的理论解释。

Method: 提出了一个动力学平均场模型（dynamical mean-field model），采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）研究从均匀态到周期性模式的转变，并通过数值模拟验证预测的相图。

Result: 线性稳定性分析表明，从均匀态到周期性模式的转变由主导不稳定模式（dominant unstable mode）的出现驱动；数值模拟确认了预测的相图，并证明稳态对流电流（steady convective currents）是稳态的鲁棒特征。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解温度梯度如何驱动稳态对流模式（steady-state convective patterns）的形成提供了直接方法，揭示了非平衡条件下对流相分离（convective phase separation）的机制。

Abstract: Nonequilibrium conditions fundamentally change how systems undergo phase separation. In systems with temperature gradients, attractive particles have been shown to form periodic patterns and steady convective currents, but a clear theoretical explanation for this behavior is still missing. Here, we present a dynamical mean-field model that describes the mechanism behind this convective phase separation. Using linear stability analysis, we show that the transition from a uniform state to a periodic pattern is driven by the emergence of a dominant unstable mode. Numerical simulations confirm the predicted phase diagram and demonstrate that these convective currents are a robust feature of the steady state, appearing regardless of the initial conditions. These results provide a direct approach for understanding how temperature gradients drive the formation of steady-state convective patterns.

</details>

### [57] [Entanglement measures and Bell-type spin-correlation observables in tau-lepton pairs at the Super Tau-Charm Facility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05846)
*Beizhi Yang,Yu Zhang,Zeren Simon Wang,Xiaorong Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在量子场论和标准模型框架下，分析了在中国超级陶粲装置（STCF）上通过$e^- e^+\to τ^-τ^+$过程测量纠缠度量和贝尔型自旋关联可观测量（Bell-type spin-correlation observables）的前景，重点关注$τ^\pm\to π^\pm ν$强子衰变道，并估计了在三种质心能量下的预期灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是在标准模型框架内，利用STCF装置研究$τ$轻子对产生过程中的量子纠缠和贝尔型关联。通过分析$e^- e^+\to τ^-τ^+$电弱过程，探索在实验上测量这些量子信息相关可观量的可行性。

Method: 研究方法基于量子场论和标准模型理论框架，重点关注$τ^\pm\to π^\pm ν$强子衰变道。利用可测量的产生运动学量（$τ$速度和质心系散射角）确定$τ^-τ^+$系统的自旋关联系数，并从中构建并发度（concurrence）和文献中定义的贝尔型关联组合。

Result: 研究结果表明，在标准模型假设下，相应的贝尔型关联组合在STCF装置上能够以高统计显著性被分辨。该分析考虑了三种质心能量（$\sqrt{s}=3.670,4.630,7.000$ GeV），假设每个能量点积分亮度为1 ab$^{-1}$，并纳入了实际探测器效率以及统计和系统不确定性。

Conclusion: 结论指出，在STCF装置上研究$e^- e^+\to τ^-τ^+$过程中的纠缠度量和贝尔型自旋关联可观测量具有良好前景，相应的贝尔型关联组合能够以高统计显著性被测量，为在粒子物理实验中探索量子信息特性提供了重要机会。

Abstract: Within the framework of quantum field theory and the Standard Model (SM), we investigate the prospects of studying entanglement measures and Bell-type spin-correlation observables in the electroweak process $e^- e^+\to τ^-τ^+$ at the center-of-mass (COM) energies of $\sqrt{s}=3.670,4.630$, and $7.000$ GeV at the proposed Super Tau-Charm Facility (STCF) in China. Focusing on the hadronic decay channel $τ^\pm\to π^\pm ν$, we determine the spin-correlation coefficients of the $τ^-τ^+$ system within the SM framework using measurable production kinematics, namely the $τ$ velocities and scattering angles in the COM frame. From these correlation coefficients, we construct concurrence and a Bell-type correlation combination as defined in the literature. Assuming an integrated luminosity of 1 ab$^{-1}$ for each considered COM energy, and incorporating realistic detector efficiencies as well as statistical and systematic uncertainties, we estimate the expected sensitivity to these observables at STCF. Our results indicate that, under the SM hypothesis, the corresponding Bell-type correlation combinations could be resolved with high statistical significance at STCF.

</details>


### [58] [On Thrust Resummation Ambiguities in $e^+e^-$ Annihilation into Hadrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06091)
*Luca Buonocore,Paolo Nason,Luca Rottoli,Paolo Torrielli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究比较了正负电子对撞中推力（thrust）分布的不同重求和（resummation）方法，发现不同但理论上等价的重求和方案会导致显著的数值差异，这些系统误差超过了通常引用的理论不确定性，表明在强耦合常数测定中需要更保守的理论误差估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在正负电子对撞形状变量研究中，特别是推力分布，固定阶量子色动力学（QCD）预测通常需要补充两喷注极限附近增强贡献的重求和。本研究旨在检验不同但理论上合法的重求和方案是否会导致显著的预测差异。

Method: 研究比较了两种重求和方案：共轭空间（或拉普拉斯空间）方法，其中重求和在推力的共轭变量中进行；以及直接空间方法，重求和直接在推力变量中执行。还考虑了避免共轭空间重求和推导中常用近似的方案。

Result: 在双对数水平上，逆拉普拉斯变换产生收敛的次领头项级数。从领头对数精度开始，由于朗道极点（Landau pole）的存在，展开变为渐近的，导致系数的对数阶乘增长。即使在最高可用对数阶重求和并与固定阶结果匹配时，两种空间得到的预测仍存在不可忽略的差异。

Conclusion: 不同重求和形式主义产生的系统误差通常超过引用的理论不确定性，这表明在使用推力分布测定强耦合常数时，需要更保守的理论误差估计。

Abstract: In $e^+e^-$ shape-variable studies, and in particular for the case of thrust, fixed-order QCD predictions are typically supplemented with the resummation of contributions enhanced near the two-jet limit.
  In this work we examine whether different, yet legitimate, resummation prescriptions can induce significant differences in the resulting predictions. This can occur because formally equivalent prescriptions may differ by terms that, although subleading, are characterised by asymptotic expansions and may therefore lead to slow convergence.
  We first compare two alternative formulations of resummation: the conjugate-space (or Laplace-space) approach, in which resummation is performed in a variable conjugate to thrust, such that the observable factorises exactly in the soft-collinear limit; and the direct-space formulation, where resummation is instead carried out directly in the thrust variable. We show that, at double-logarithmic level, the inverse Laplace transform generates a convergent tower of subleading terms. Starting from leading-logarithmic accuracy, the expansion becomes asymptotic due to the presence of the Landau pole, leading to a mild log-factorial growth of the coefficients. When including the highest available logarithmic order in the resummation, matched to fixed-order results, we still find non-negligible differences between predictions obtained in the two spaces.
  We then consider a formulation of the resummation that avoids certain approximations commonly used in the derivation of conjugate-space resummation. We observe that this also has a non-negligible numerical impact.
  In general, we find that the systematics stemming from the adoption of different formalisms typically exceeds the quoted theoretical uncertainties, suggesting the need for more conservative theory-error estimates when using the thrust distribution in determinations of the strong coupling.

</details>


### [59] [Next-to-next-to-leading order event generation for $t\bar{t}H$ production with approximate two-loop amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06143)
*Christian Biello,Chiara Savoini,Chiara Signorile-Signorile,Marius Wiesemann*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究首次将顶夸克对伴随希格斯玻色子产生过程（tt̄H）的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD修正与部分子簇射（parton shower）进行匹配，采用MiNNLOPS方法，并公开了相应的POWHEG生成器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强子对撞机上顶夸克对伴随希格斯玻色子产生过程（tt̄H）的精确理论预测，填补NNLO QCD修正与部分子簇射匹配的空白，为实验测量提供可靠的理论工具。

Method: 采用MiNNLOPS方法将NNLO QCD修正与部分子簇射匹配；对于双圈振幅，使用基于软希格斯玻色子极限和高能极限的两种近似，并首次构建了全色版本的高能极限近似，在相空间中进行逐点组合。

Result: 实现了tt̄H过程的首次NNLO+PS匹配，提供了稳健可靠的微分预测；通过保守的不确定性估计验证了方法的可靠性，并展示了NNLO修正和部分子簇射效应的显著影响。

Conclusion: 成功开发了公开可用的tt̄H MiNNLOPS生成器，为希格斯玻色子衰变到光子以及包含离壳顶夸克衰变的过程提供了精确的理论预测工具，显著提升了该过程的模拟精度。

Abstract: We study Higgs-boson production in association with a top-quark pair ($t\bar{t}H$) at hadron colliders and present the first matching of next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO) QCD corrections to parton showers using the MiNNLOPS method. For the two-loop amplitude, we employ two established approximations, based on the soft Higgs-boson and high-energy limits, respectively. For the first time, we also construct the latter in full colour and propose a pointwise combination of the two approximations across phase space. By assigning a conservative uncertainty estimate, which remains well below the perturbative uncertainties, we ensure robust and reliable differential predictions, explicitly validated at the one-loop level. Apart from the two-loop amplitude, all remaining ingredients of the MiNNLOPS calculation are included exactly. After thorough validation, we present a series of phenomenological results illustrating the impact of NNLO corrections and parton-shower effects. We consider fiducial predictions for the Higgs-boson decay into photons and include off-shell top-quark decays with tree-level spin correlations in both the dilepton and semileptonic channels.
  Our $t\bar{t}H$ MiNNLOPS generator is publicly available within the POWHEG framework.

</details>


### [60] [Vacuum Cherenkov Radiation for Nonminimal Isotropic Lorentz Violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05679)
*Albert Yu. Petrov,Marco Schreck,Alexandre R. Vieira*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析超高能宇宙射线（UHECRs）数据，对由非最小维度-5洛伦兹破缺（LV）算符引起的真空切伦科夫辐射效应施加严格约束，重点关注各向同性系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究真空切伦科夫辐射（vacuum Cherenkov radiation）效应，该效应由费米子扇区中的非最小维度-5洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz-violating, LV）算符引起。通过分析超高能宇宙射线（ultra-high-energy cosmic rays, UHECRs）实验数据，旨在对相关参数施加约束。

Method: 聚焦于两组独立各向同性（isotropic）的非最小系数集合。在假设真空切伦科夫辐射为预期现象的前提下，利用超高能宇宙射线（UHECRs）的实验数据进行分析。

Result: 基于超高能宇宙射线（UHECRs）数据，能够对夸克（quarks）中的各向同性系数施加严格约束（stringent bounds）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过分析超高能宇宙射线（UHECRs）观测数据，可以对由非最小维度-5洛伦兹破缺（LV）算符引起的真空切伦科夫辐射效应施加严格的实验约束，特别是对各向同性系数。

Abstract: In this work, we study the effects of vacuum Cherenkov radiation caused by nonminimal dimension-5 Lorentz-violating (LV) operators in the fermion sector. Explicitly, we focus on two independent isotropic pieces of each set of nonminimal coefficients. Under the assumption that vacuum Cherenkov radiation is an expected phenomenon, experimental data of ultra-high-energy cosmic rays (UHECRs) allow us to put stringent bounds on isotropic coefficients in quarks.

</details>


### [61] [Two Higgs Doublet Model from Six Dimensional Gauge Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05857)
*Kento Akamatsu,Takuya Hirose,Nobuhito Maru,Akio Nago*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文改进了先前提出的六维SU(4)规范理论模型，通过引入膜局域规范动能项，在T^2/Z_2轨形上构建了更完善的两希格斯二重态模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在改进先前提出的六维SU(4)规范理论模型，通过引入膜局域规范动能项（brane localized gauge kinetic terms）来完善两希格斯二重态（two Higgs doublet）模型的构建。

Method: 在六维SU(4)规范理论中，通过在T^2/Z_2轨形（orbifold）上引入膜局域规范动能项，将两希格斯二重态识别为六维规范场额外空间分量的无质量零模（massless zero modes）。

Result: 该模型的希格斯势在树级自动保持CP守恒和Z_2对称性，软破缺Z_2对称性的标量质量在一圈水平生成，标准模型希格斯质量可通过调节膜局域规范动能项的大小获得，同时实现了电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking）。

Conclusion: 该改进模型在六维规范对称性的约束下，自然地实现了普通两希格斯二重态模型中需人为假设的对称性特征，并能预测其他物理希格斯质量。

Abstract: We improve our previously proposed two Higgs doublet model of six-dimensional $SU(4)$ gauge theory compactified on an orbifold $T^2/Z_2$ by introducing the brane localized gauge kinetic terms. Since two Higgs doublets are identified with massless zero modes in extra spatial components of the six-dimensional gauge field, the Higgs sector in our model is constrained by the six-dimensional gauge symmetry. As a result, our Higgs potential at tree-level is automatically CP conserving and $Z_2$ symmetric, which are assumed by hand in the ordinary two Higgs doublet models. The scalar masses breaking the $Z_2$ symmetry softly are generated at one-loop. We show that the Standard Model Higgs mass can be obtained by tuning the size of the brane localized gauge kinetic terms as well as the electroweak symmetry breaking is realized. Other physical Higgs masses are predicted.

</details>


### [62] [Revisiting unitarity of single scalar field with non-minimal coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06296)
*Minxi He,Muzi Hong,Kyohei Mukaida,Tomoya Nishiki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 研究了具有四次自耦合的非最小耦合标量场的幺正性破坏尺度，通过计算Jordan框架和Einstein框架中的六点散射振幅，证明了结果的框架无关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型在文献中被广泛研究，但幺正性破坏尺度（unitarity violation scale）的估计尚未得到一致讨论，特别是在Jordan框架中。需要明确计算并验证框架无关性。

Method: 计算了Jordan框架和Einstein框架中标量粒子的六点散射振幅（six-point scattering amplitudes），并明确展示了结果的框架无关性。由于单场情况下共形模的扩展目标空间是平凡的，主要贡献来自标量场的势能。

Result: 在两个框架中得到了相同的结果，证明了幺正性破坏尺度估计的框架无关性。在自耦合消失极限下，两个框架的结果都变得平凡，符合预期。

Conclusion: 通过计算六点散射振幅，明确了非最小耦合标量场幺正性破坏尺度的框架无关性，解决了文献中估计不一致的问题，特别是在Jordan框架中的讨论。

Abstract: We have investigated the unitarity violation scale of a non-minimally coupled scalar field with quartic self-coupling. This model is widely studied in the literature but the estimation of the unitarity violation scale has not been consistently discussed, especially in the Jordan frame. We have calculated the six-point scattering amplitudes of the scalar particles in both the Jordan frame and the Einstein frame, and explicitly shown the frame-independence of the results. Since the extended target space with the conformal mode is trivial in the single-field case, the dominant contribution comes from the potential of the scalar field. The results in both frames become trivial in the vanishing self-coupling limit as expected.

</details>

### [63] [On solutions of the Euler equation for incoherent fluid on a rotating sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05737)
*B. G. Konopelchenko,G. Ortenzi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了旋转球面上可压缩无粘性流体在恒定压力下的运动，提出了欧拉方程的速端曲线方程，获得了一类由两个二元任意函数参数化的解，并分析了速度导数发散时的爆破曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旋转球面上可压缩无粘性流体在恒定压力下的运动，旨在建立相应的欧拉方程速端曲线方程，获得参数化解并分析其奇异行为。

Method: 采用速端曲线（hodograph）方法处理欧拉方程，推导出由两个二元任意函数参数化的解类，并考虑慢速和快速旋转球面的极限情况。

Result: 获得了欧拉方程的一类参数化解，给出了若干显式特解，描述了速度导数发散的爆破曲线，并提出了描述椭圆函数模变形的方程。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了旋转球面上可压缩无粘性流体运动的速端曲线方程框架，获得了丰富的解类并分析了其奇异行为，为相关流体动力学问题提供了新的解析工具。

Abstract: The motion of compressible, inviscid fluid under the constant pressure on a rotating sphere is studied. The hodograph equations for the corresponding Euler equation are presented. They provide us with the class of solutions of the Euler equation parameterized by two arbitrary functions of two variables. Several particular explicit solutions are given. The blow-up curves, on which the derivatives of velocitiy blows up, are described. The limiting cases of slowly and rapidly rotating sphere are considered. The equation describing the deformations of elliptic functions modulus is presented.

</details>


### [64] [Higher-Order Approximation of Coherent State Dynamics in Self-Interacting Quantum Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06026)
*Zied Ammari,Julien Malartre,Maher Zerzeri*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了自相互作用玻色量子场论中相干态传播的任意阶渐近展开，改进了先前仅识别主导项的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自相互作用玻色量子场论在半经典（平均场）区域中相干态的传播，旨在建立量子演化的系统渐近展开方法。

Method: 基于Hepp方法，结合对经典（非线性）和量子（线性）场动力学的详细分析，首先在空间截断的$P(φ)_2$模型中建立结果，然后扩展到一类非多项式解析相互作用。

Result: 成功构建了相干态量子演化的任意阶渐近展开，该结果在标准假设下确保哈密顿量的本质自伴性和经典流的适定性。

Conclusion: 这项工作改进并推广了早期仅识别展开式主导项的结果，为自相互作用量子场论中的相干态传播提供了更完整的渐近描述。

Abstract: We study the propagation of coherent states in self-interacting bosonic quantum field theories in the semi-classical (mean-field) regime. Relying on Hepp's method and a detailed analysis of the associated classical and quantum field dynamics, non-linear and linear respectively, we construct an asymptotic expansion of arbitrary order for the quantum evolution of coherent states. The results are first established for the spatially cutoff $P(φ)_2$ model, under standard assumptions ensuring essential self-adjointness of the Hamiltonian and well-posedness of the classical flow, and are then extended to a class of non-polynomial analytic interactions. This work refines and generalizes earlier results, which identified only the leading-order term of the expansion.

</details>


### [65] [Gaussian free field convergence of the six-vertex model with $-1\leqΔ\leq-\frac12$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06268)
*Hugo Duminil-Copin,Karol Kajetan Kozlowski,Piet Lammers,Ioan Manolescu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了在特定参数范围内，二维六顶点模型（six-vertex model）的高度函数（height function）在标度极限下收敛于全平面高斯自由场（full-plane Gaussian free field）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究各向同性六顶点模型在特定谱参数范围内的统计性质，特别是其高度函数在标度极限下的渐近行为。该研究旨在理解此类可积模型（integrable model）的普适性特征。

Method: 研究各向同性六顶点模型在$\mathbb{Z}^2$上的实现，其中权重参数满足$\mathbf{a}=\mathbf{b}=1$且$\mathbf{c}\in[\sqrt{3},2]$，对应谱参数$Δ\in[-1,-1/2]$。对于各向异性情况，采用适当的晶格嵌入方法。

Result: 证明在标度极限下，关联高度函数收敛于适当标度的全平面高斯自由场。该结果可通过合适的晶格嵌入方法推广到各向异性权重$\mathbf{a}\neq\mathbf{b}$的情况。

Conclusion: 六顶点模型在特定参数范围内的高度函数表现出高斯自由场的普适性行为，这一收敛性质在适当条件下可扩展至各向异性情况。

Abstract: We study the isotropic six-vertex model on $\mathbb{Z}^2$ with spectral parameter $Δ\in[-1,-1/2]$, that is, with weights $\mathbf{a}=\mathbf{b}=1$ and $\mathbf{c}\in[\sqrt{3},2]$. We show that the associated height function converges, in the scaling limit, to a properly scaled full-plane Gaussian free field. The result extends to anisotropic weights $\mathbf{a}\neq\mathbf{b}$ upon using a suitable embedding of the lattice.

</details>


### [66] [New results for Heisenberg dynamics for non self-adjoint Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06419)
*Fabio Bagarello*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文继续分析非自伴哈密顿量（non self-adjoint Hamiltonians）在海森堡动力学（Heisenberg dynamics）中的作用，特别关注"暴力归一化（brute-force normalized）"向量这一未充分探索的方面，主要研究守恒量（conserved quantities）及其时间演化条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文动机源于对非自伴哈密顿量在海森堡动力学中作用的持续研究兴趣，以及近期动力学系统（dynamical systems）相关成果的启发。作者旨在探索海森堡动力学中一个未充分研究的方面——需要使用"暴力归一化"向量的情况。

Method: 研究方法延续了先前论文的分析框架，聚焦于海森堡动力学中与"暴力归一化"向量相关的特定方面。分析重点放在守恒量及其时间演化条件上。

Result: 论文主要关注守恒量，以及保证系统某些可观测量（observables）或其平均值（mean values）不随时间演化的条件。这些结果涉及非自伴哈密顿量框架下的动力学特性。

Conclusion: 本文延续了对非自伴哈密顿量在海森堡动力学中作用的系统性分析，特别强调了"暴力归一化"向量这一独特方面，为理解量子系统守恒量和时间演化提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: In a previous paper we began our analysis on the role of non self-adjoint Hamiltonians in connection with the Heisenberg dynamics for quantum systems. Here, motivated by the growing interest on this topic and on some recent results on dynamical systems, we continue this analysis focusing on what we believe is an unexplored (or, at least, not so explored! aspect of Heisenberg dynamics, related to the need for using vectors which are {\em brute-force normalized}. ### [68] [Representations of the Flat Space Wavefunction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.17619)
*Tyler Dunaisky*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平直空间波函数是计算宇宙学关联函数（cosmological correlators）的关键成分，但需要建立其不同表示形式之间的严格数学关系。现有多种表示方法需要被系统化证明，特别是关于宇宙学多胞形表示和部分分式分解的猜想。

Method: 通过图论方法，从任意图G出发构造平直空间波函数，将其表示为顶点和边传播子（propagators）的积分。研究聚焦于三种具体表示：宇宙学多胞形的规范形式表示、部分分式分解表示，以及基于图连通性的子图集合表示。

Result: 严格证明了平直空间波函数的三种表示形式的正确性。特别地，证实了波函数可以从宇宙学多胞形的规范形式中直接读取，并解决了Fevola等人关于波函数部分分式分解的猜想。分解项对应于图G及其生成子图（spanning subgraphs）的连通子图集合。

Conclusion: 平直空间波函数的多种表示形式之间存在深刻的数学联系，这些表示揭示了波函数如何编码图G的连通性信息。部分分式分解的证实为理解波函数的结构提供了新的视角，将图论性质与宇宙学计算联系起来。

Abstract: From any graph $G$ arises a flat space wavefunction, obtained by integrating a product of propagators associated to the vertices and edges of $G$. This function is a key ingredient in the computation of cosmological correlators, and several representations for it have been proposed. We formulate three such representations and prove their correctness. In particular, we show that the flat space wavefunction can be read off from the canonical form of the cosmological polytope, and we settle a conjecture of Fevola, Pimentel, Sattelberger, and Westerdijk regarding a partial fraction decomposition for the flat space wavefunction. The terms of the decomposition correspond to certain collections of connected subgraphs associated to $G$ and its spanning subgraphs, reflecting the fact that the flat space wavefunction contains information about how $G$ is connected.

### [69] [Study of Collective Phenomena in Heavy-Ion Collisions Using CMS Open Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05798)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过测量新提出的观测值v_0(p_T)，探测重离子碰撞中形成的夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）的集体现象。该观测值对径向流（radial flow）直接敏感，能够表征径向流涨落的横向动量（transverse momentum, p_T）依赖性。

Method: 研究使用CMS开放数据门户（CMS Open Data portal）的公开数据，在√s_NN=2.76 TeV的铅-铅（PbPb）碰撞中测量了v_0(p_T)观测值。该方法旨在验证集体径向流的三个关键特征。

Result: 观测到集体径向流的三个关键特征：赝快度（pseudorapidity, η）中的长程关联、作为p_T函数的中心度无关形状，以及p_T中的因子化（factorization）。结果在误差范围内与ATLAS在√s_NN=5.02 TeV的测量基本一致。

Abstract: In this work, we present preliminary results from a measurement of the recently proposed observable, $v_0(p_T)$, in lead-lead (PbPb) collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=2.76 \text{ TeV}$, using public data from the CMS Open Data portal. This observable is directly sensitive to radial flow and characterizes the transverse momentum ($p_T$) dependence of radial flow fluctuations, serving as probe of collective phenomena in the quark-gluon plasma (QGP) formed in heavy-ion collisions. Consistently with the ATLAS results at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=5.02 \text{ TeV}$, we observe the three key features of collective radial flow: long-range correlations in pseudorapidity ($η$), a centrality-independent shape as a function of $p_T$, and factorization in $p_T$. The results presented in this work are generally compatible, within uncertainties, with the ATLAS measurements at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}=5.02\text{ TeV}$ reported in Phys. Rev. Lett. 136, 032301 (2026).

### [70] [Effects of Self-Interaction and of an Ideal Gas in Binary Mergers of Bosonic Dark Matter Cores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06329)
*Carlos Tena-Contreras,Ivan Alvarez-Rios,Francisco S. Guzman,Jens Niemeyer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚暗物质（BECDM）模型中暗物质核心的二元并合过程，特别关注标量自相互作用和引力耦合理想气体两种情景下的并合结果。

Result: 发现最终核心质量比在并合后达到稳定平均值；排斥性自相互作用增加最终孤子核心质量，而吸引性相互作用增强质量损失；在涉及理想气体的并合中，玻色成分总能形成稳定孤子核心。

Abstract: We study binary mergers of dark matter cores in the Bose-Einstein condensate (BECDM) model. We include two scenarios: scalar self-interaction and the presence of a gravitationally coupled ideal gas. Using 3D simulations of the Gross-Pitaevskii-Poisson and Schrödinger-Poisson-Euler systems, we analyze the properties of the resulting remnants. We find that the final core-mass ratio reaches a stable average value after the merger. Repulsive self-interaction increases the mass of the final solitonic core, while attractive interaction enhances mass loss. In mergers involving an ideal gas, namely of fermion-boson stars, a stable solitonic core always forms in the bosonic component, even when the gas dominates, whereas the gas itself does not form a compact core. We explain these results using energy scalings and find that self-interaction, equilibrium cores follow $E \propto -M^3$, which leads to an almost universal merger fraction. Self-interaction changes this scaling, because repulsive $g$ moves the system toward a milder $E \propto -M^2$ scaling and increases mass retention, while attractive $g$ strengthens binding and favors mass ejection. In the case of interaction with an ideal gas, this component only modifies the gravitational background and does not change the intrinsic scaling of the bosonic part. These results show that the merger outcome is not universal but controlled by the interaction strength, while solitonic BECDM cores remain robust across diverse environments including gas.

*Pierre Auclair,Christophe Ringeval*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文指出Ballardini等人[1]在慢滚功率谱（slow-roll power spectra）三阶修正项中的多项计算存在错误，并通过蒙特卡洛数值积分验证了Auclair & Ringeval[2]原始结果的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在纠正Ballardini等人[1]在慢滚功率谱三阶修正计算中的错误。作者发现该工作与Auclair & Ringeval[2]原始结果存在差异，但指出这种差异源于计算方法错误而非近似方案不同。

Method: 作者通过分析指出Ballardini等人错误地采用了"先积分后展开"而非"先展开后积分"的方法。为验证这一论断，作者对争议的三维定积分进行了蒙特卡洛数值积分（Monte-Carlo numerical integration）。

Result: 蒙特卡洛数值积分结果与Auclair & Ringeval[2]的解析值完全吻合，证实了Ballardini等人的计算错误。这表明两者结果的差异确实源于积分方法错误，而非近似方案不同。

Conclusion: Ballardini等人[1]在慢滚功率谱三阶修正计算中存在错误，其错误源于对三维定积分的错误处理方式。Auclair & Ringeval[2]的原始结果在相同波数标度下是正确的。

Abstract: We point out that several terms in the third-order corrections to the slow-roll power spectra presented by Ballardini et al. [1] are incorrect. The authors of that work claim that their result differ from the ones originally presented by Auclair & Ringeval [2] due to some different approximation schemes. However, in our original work, all terms at all orders have been derived exactly and any difference between two expansions performed at the same pivot wavenumber signals a problem. As we show in this comment, Ballardini et al. [1] have misevaluated some definite three-dimensional integrals by integrating a Taylor expansion instead of Taylor expanding an integral. Our claim is backed-up with a Monte-Carlo numerical integration of the incriminated three-dimensional integrals, which, unsurprisingly, matches the analytical value derived in Auclair & Ringeval [2].

### [72] [Physics of active polymers: scaling analysis via a compounding formula](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05652)
*Takahiro Sakaue,Enrico Carlon*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种透明的标度理论（scaling theory），通过复合公式捕捉活性聚合物（active polymer）中标记单体的均方位移（MSD），将单体运动分解为孤立活性粒子运动与聚合物连接性因子的乘积，从而直观揭示非平衡动力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性聚合物系统展现出丰富的非平衡现象，但现有理论主要依赖活性Rouse模型（active Rouse model）的变体，其形式解虽精确但物理直观性有限。当前缺乏能够清晰分离活性效应与聚合物连接性影响的理论框架。

Method: 本文发展了一种透明的标度理论，提出复合公式：聚合物单体的均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）等于孤立活性粒子的MSD乘以编码聚合物骨架张力传播的连接性因子。该方法将活性作用与聚合物连接性效应分离开来。

Result: 标度预测与多种广义活性聚合物模型（generalized active polymer models）的精确计算结果一致，证明了该框架对不同噪声统计（noise statistics）的鲁棒性。理论直观揭示了涌现的动力学区域（dynamical regimes）。

Conclusion: 该标度理论提供了一个简单且可扩展的理论结构，适用于复杂且解析难处理的活性聚合物系统，为理解非平衡聚合物动力学（non-equilibrium polymer dynamics）提供了统一视角。

Abstract: Active polymeric systems exhibit a rich spectrum of non-equilibrium phenomena arising from stochastic forces that explicitly break detailed balance. Despite the rapid growth of experimental and numerical studies, analytical progress remains limited. To date, theoretical understanding relies largely on variants of the active Rouse model, whose formal solutions, though exact, are often obscured by summations over Rouse modes and therefore provide limited direct physical insight. In this work, we develop a transparent scaling theory that captures the tagged-monomer mean-squared displacement (MSD) in active polymers through a compounding formula: the MSD of a monomer in the chain is expressed as that of an isolated active particle, modulated by a connectivity factor encoding tension propagation along the polymer backbone. This approach isolates the role of activity from that of polymer connectivity and reveals the emergent dynamical regimes in a physically intuitive manner. We test the scaling predictions against exact calculations for a broad class of generalized active polymer models driven by diverse noise statistics. The agreement demonstrates the robustness of the scaling framework across microscopic details. Our results provide a simple and extensible theoretical structure that can be applied to complex and analytically intractable active polymer systems, thereby offering a unifying perspective on non-equilibrium polymer dynamics.

Method: 提出了SAFT-P方法，将局部簇视为缔合超粒子（associating superparticles），并将其自由能收缩（contracting）回单体密度。通过巨正则蒙特卡洛模拟（Grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations）验证了该方法对二元和三元混合物的预测能力。

Conclusion: 在斑块尺度上解析关联为建模具有拓扑敏感局部结构的复杂凝聚物和自组装提供了一条分析途径，超越了传统SAFT方法的局限性。

Abstract: We introduce SAFT-P, a plaquette-level extension of Statistical Associating Fluid Theory for patchy particles. By treating local clusters as associating superparticles and contracting their free energy back to monomer densities, SAFT-P retains information about patch topology that is lost in conventional SAFT. Grand-canonical Monte Carlo simulations of binary and ternary mixtures show that SAFT-P captures topology-dependent critical points and coexistence curves and discriminates between particles with identical valence but different patch layouts. Beyond topology, incorporating plaquette-scale correlations also improves predictions in regimes where patch specific interactions are absent. Results indicate that resolving correlations at the plaquette scale provides an analytical route to model complex condensates and self-assembly with topology-sensitive local structure.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统信息引擎实验通常假设马尔可夫环境（Markovian environments），但许多物理系统存在环境记忆效应，隐藏自由度与系统历史保持相关性。这种隐藏记忆能否作为热力学资源利用仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 采用光学捕获的平衡态布朗粒子，实施时间分辨测量（time resolved measurements）和时间延迟双测量协议（time delayed double measurement protocol），通过信息回流（information backflow）从隐藏浴自由度中检索信息。

Result: 实验证明信息回流改变弛豫动力学，可独立于初始状态效应进行量化，适当利用时可增强功提取。在某些区域，提取的功甚至超过可观测自由度单独存储的能量。

Conclusion: 环境记忆被确立为实验可及的热力学资源，非马尔可夫动力学可系统性地用于提升时间相关环境中信息引擎的性能。

Abstract: Thermodynamics establishes that information acquired through measurement can be converted into work, as exemplified by Maxwell's demon and Szilard engines. Most experimental realizations of information engines, however, implicitly assume Markovian environments, in which information exchanged with the surroundings is irreversibly lost. Many physical systems instead exhibit environmental memory, with hidden degrees of freedom retaining correlations with the system's past and giving rise to non Markovian dynamics. Whether and how such concealed memory can be harnessed as a thermodynamic resource has remained an open question. Here we experimentally demonstrate work extraction from environmental memory. Using time resolved measurements on an optically trapped Brownian particle in equilibrium, we implement a time delayed double measurement protocol that retrieves information via backflow from hidden bath degrees of freedom. We show that this information backflow alters relaxation dynamics, can be quantified independently of initial state effects, and when appropriately exploited enhances work extraction. Notably, we identify regimes in which the extracted work exceeds the energy stored in the observable degree of freedom alone. Our results establish environmental memory as an experimentally accessible thermodynamic resource and reveal how non Markovian dynamics can be systematically explored to improve the performance of information engines operating in time-correlated environments.

Motivation: 无序颗粒物质（amorphous particulate matter）广泛存在于自然和合成材料中，但其无序微观结构与复杂动力学行为的耦合机制尚未完全理解，这对从地貌演化到肿瘤转移中细胞解阻塞（unjamming）等现象有重要影响。

Method: 引入线性控制理论（linear control theory）工具量化系统对外部输入的响应，并将其应用于应力作用下阻塞无序材料（jammed amorphous materials）的动力学分析。

Result: 平均可控性（average controllability）与准静态剪切（quasistatic shear）下颗粒重排（particle rearrangement）强相关，表明其是重排动力学的准确预测指标；最优时间尺度参数的调优能优化预测能力，该参数值揭示了剪切过程中多个重排颗粒参与低能振动本征模式（vibrational eigenmodes）的物理机制。

Conclusion: 线性控制理论是预测和设计无序介质（disordered media）力学响应的有前景的数学框架，为理解无序材料微观结构与动力学行为的耦合提供了新工具。

Abstract: Amorphous particulate matter constitutes a wide range of natural and synthetic materials. Despite this ubiquity, the way in which these systems' disordered microstructure couples to their often subtle and complex dynamical behavior is not yet fully understood, with profound consequences for phenomena ranging from landscape evolution to cellular unjamming during tumor metastasis. With this paper, we introduce tools from linear control theory that quantify system response to external input, and demonstrate their utility in elucidating the dynamics of jammed amorphous materials under stress. Our results indicate that average controllability, the response of a system to perturbation, strongly correlates with particle rearrangement in systems subject to quasistatic shear, implying that average controllability is an accurate predictor of rearrangement dynamics in certain contexts. Moreover, we show that the time scale over which average controllability is calculated can be tuned to optimize its predictive capacity for particle rearrangement. Values of the optimal time scale provide physical insight into the system; namely, that multiple rearranging particles participate on average in vibrational eigenmodes of lower and lower energy as the system is sheared until the rearrangement event. Broadly, our study demonstrates that linear control theory is a promising mathematical framework for predicting and designing mechanical response in disordered media.

</details>


### [77] [Inference of the 3D pressure field exerted by a single cell from a thin membrane transverse deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06527)
*Quentin Bédel,Loïc Dupré,Nicolas Destainville*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种逆问题（inverse problem）解决方案，用于从突起力显微镜（Protrusion Force Microscopy）技术获得的一维AFM测量数据中重建三维压力场。该方法探索了在实验背景下的适用性范围。

Result: 该研究开发了从一维高度剖面重建三维压力场的数学框架，并确定了该方法在实验条件下的适用性范围（regime of applicability）。

Conclusion: 通过解决这一逆问题，研究为从高空间分辨率的AFM测量中准确获取细胞施加的三维压力场提供了理论和方法基础。

Abstract: Numerous cell types relate to their immediate environment by exerting a three-dimensional pressure field on their environment, with components both longitudinal and transverse to the cell membrane. This pressure field can in principle be measured by traction force microscopy experiments. Compared to other approaches, the technique of Protrusion Force Microscopy gives access with high spatial resolution to the pressure field by measuring the deformation of a thin elastic membrane using atomic force microscopy (AFM). However, while the pressure field under interest is three-dimensional, the height profile measured by AFM is only one-dimensional. We propose a solution to this inverse problem and we explore its regime of applicability in the experimental context.

### [78] [Pathologies of dimension-zero scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05683)
*James M. Cline,Anamaria Hell*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文驳斥了先前研究中关于四阶拉格朗日标量场能解决宇宙常数问题并产生原初密度扰动的观点，指出该理论包含鬼态（ghost）导致经典不稳定性和量子幺正性破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对一系列声称四阶拉格朗日标量场能解决宇宙常数问题并替代暴胀产生原初密度扰动的论文，本文旨在质疑这些主张的科学有效性。

Method: 通过理论分析四阶拉格朗日标量场$\sim(\Box\varphi)^2$的谱结构，证明其包含鬼态（ghost），并研究该场与标准模型粒子的耦合效应。

Result: 发现该理论存在经典不稳定性并破坏量子幺正性（unitarity），新标量粒子无法抵消标准模型对宇宙常数的贡献，且与标准模型的耦合会产生限制性第五力（confining fifth force）。

Conclusion: 四阶拉格朗日标量场既不能解决宇宙常数问题，也无法作为早期宇宙密度扰动的来源，其理论存在根本性缺陷。

Abstract: It has been claimed in a series of papers that scalar fields with a fourth-order Lagrangian $\sim(\Box\varphi)^2$ can solve the cosmological constant problem by canceling the loop contributions from standard model fields, and that their fluctuations can be the source of the primordial density perturbations of the Universe, without the need for inflation. We dispute these claims. The spectrum of the theory includes a ghost, which leads to classical instabilities and quantum violation of unitarity. We show that the new scalar particles cannot cancel the standard model contributions to the cosmological constant, unless they include a unitarity-violating ghost at the quantum level. Further, the coupling of such scalars to the particles of the standard model induces a confining fifth force which rules it out as a source of density perturbations in the early Universe.

### [79] [Exact one-loop QED actions in global $\mathrm{(A)dS}_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05826)
*Chiang-Mei Chen,Sang Pyo Kim,Cristian Andres Rivera Medina*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文使用in-out形式论推导了二维全局(反)德西特时空((A)dS₂)中均匀电场下旋量场的一圈量子电动力学有效作用量。该有效作用量通过Bogoliubov系数与真空持续振幅和粒子-反粒子对自发产生相关联，揭示了电场与时空曲率之间的强相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确计算二维全局(反)德西特时空((A)dS₂)中均匀电场下旋量场的一圈量子电动力学有效作用量。这有助于理解弯曲时空背景下量子场论的基本性质，特别是电场与时空曲率之间的相互作用。

Method: 采用in-out形式论，通过将out真空与in真空相关联的散射矩阵来确定有效作用量。该方法利用相应Klein-Gordon或Dirac方程的Bogoliubov系数，这些方程同时考虑了规范场和弯曲时空背景。

Result: 获得了带电标量和旋量场在全局(A)dS₂中的有效作用量，这些结果以固有时间积分和Hurwitz zeta函数表达。真空持续振幅（一圈有效作用量虚部的两倍）通过Bogoliubov关系与背景场自发产生的粒子-反粒子对平均数量相关联。

Conclusion: 推导出的量子电动力学有效作用量揭示了电场与时空曲率之间的强相互作用，并正确再现了纯(A)dS₂时空和闵可夫斯基空间中均匀电场的极限情况。这些结果为理解弯曲时空中的量子电动力学现象提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: Using the in-out formalism, we derive the exact one-loop QED effective actions for spinor field in a uniform electric field in two-dimensional global (anti-)de Sitter (A)dS$_2$ spacetime. The one-loop effective action probed by a scalar or spinor field is determined by the scattering matrix relating the out-vacuum to the in-vacuum, which is in turn fixed by the Bogoliubov coefficients of the corresponding Klein-Gordon or Dirac equation in the presence of both a gauge field and curved spacetime. Remarkably, the vacuum persistence amplitude -- twice the imaginary part of the one-loop effective action -- is related, via the Bogoliubov relations, to the mean number of particle-antiparticle pairs spontaneously produced by the background fields. The Bogoliubov coefficients or mean number of pair-production for charged scalar and spinor fields in global (A)dS$_2$ lead to QED effective actions expressed in terms of both proper-time integrals and Hurwitz zeta functions. These effective actions reveal a strong interplay between the electric field and spacetime curvature and correctly reproduce the limiting cases of pure (A)dS$_2$ spacetime and a uniform electric field in Minkowski space. We further discuss the physical implications of the resulting QED effective actions in (A)dS$_2$.

### [80] [On amplitudes in Chiral Higher Spin Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06044)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从手征高自旋引力的协变运动方程中提取三次相互作用；分类扭量理论（twistor theory）中手征场的所有可能三次振幅；推导任意自旋在费曼/洛伦兹规范（Feynman/Lorenz gauges）下的传播子；使用这些传播子求解Berends-Giele递推关系。

Result: 计算的三次振幅与光锥规范（light-cone gauge）早期结果一致；完成了扭量理论（twistor theory）手征场所有可能三次振幅的分类；对于自对偶杨-米尔斯理论（self-dual Yang-Mills theory）的高自旋扩展，所有树图级振幅为零。

Conclusion: 成功从协变框架提取手征高自旋引力（Chiral Higher Spin Gravity）的三次相互作用，验证了振幅计算的一致性，并建立了自对偶杨-米尔斯理论（self-dual Yang-Mills theory）高自旋扩展的树图级振幅为零的重要结果。

Abstract: We extract cubic interactions from the covariant equations of motion of Chiral Higher Spin Gravity and compute the corresponding amplitudes. These amplitudes are found to agree with earlier results obtained in the light-cone gauge. We also classify all possible cubic amplitudes that can be constructed from chiral fields arising in twistor theory. In addition, we derive propagators for arbitrary spin in the Feynman/Lorenz gauges. These propagators are then used to solve Berends--Giele recursion relations for a truncation of Chiral Higher Spin Gravity, which is a higher-spin extension of self-dual Yang--Mills theory. We confirm that all tree-level amplitudes vanish.

Result: 研究发现，在相同类别中存在更一般函数形式导出的可接受模型。识别出支持具有非平凡内部结构的连续扭结族的新模型，这些扭结可解释为由多个局域化能量块组成的复合构型。

While cubic polynomial superpotentials naturally generate quartic interactions, we show that more general functional forms also lead to admissible models within the same class. ### [82] [OPE in a generally covariant form](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06246)
*Anatoly Konechny*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了D维欧几里得共形场论中算子乘积展开（OPE）的一般协变性，提出按测地线距离组织展开，并发现曲率项在共形平坦流形OPE中的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨D维欧几里得共形场论（Euclidean conformal field theories）中算子乘积展开（operator product expansion, OPE）的一般协变性（general covariance），特别是在弯曲空间背景下OPE的结构特性。

Method: 方法包括：1）提出按两个插入点间的测地线距离（geodesic distance）幂次组织OPE展开；2）使用测地线切向量（tangent vector）与张量算子进行缩并；3）对共形平坦流形（conformally flat manifolds）进行显式计算。

Result: 结果显示：1）在共形平坦流形中，OPE会出现特定曲率项；2）对于D>2情况，两个标量原初算子（scalar primaries）的OPE恒等通道（identity channel）中，此类曲率项的首项与Schouten张量（Schouten tensor）成正比；3）这些曲率项在一般度规下普遍存在，但高阶展开中可能存在系数不由平坦空间OPE确定的曲率项。

Conclusion: 结论指出所发现的曲率项具有实际应用价值，特别是在弯曲空间上的共形微扰理论（conformal perturbation theory）计算中，这些项是普遍存在的且对理论计算有重要意义。

Abstract: We discuss the general covariance of operator product expansion in D-dimensional Euclidean conformal field theories. We propose to organise the expansion in powers of geodesic distance between two insertion points and to use the tangent vector to the geodesic for contractions with tensor operators. For conformally flat manifolds we show by explicit calculation that certain curvature terms arise in the OPE. For example for D>2 the leading term of this type in the identity channel of OPE of two scalar primaries is proportional to the Schouten tensor. We further argue that the terms we found are present for a general metric and are thus universal but there may be curvature terms at higher order in the expansion whose coefficients are not determined by the flat space OPE. The curvature terms we discuss are of practical interest in conformal perturbation theory calculations on curved spaces.

Method: 研究方法基于渐近对称群(asymptotic symmetry groups)的幺正不可约表示(unitary irreducible representations, UIRs)理论。论文研究了超动量(supermomentum)本征态，并将此构造与红外安全振幅的修饰态(dressed-state)方法进行对比分析。

Conclusion: 论文结论指出，渐近对称群的幺正不可约表示为理解QED和引力理论的红外结构提供了新视角。通过基于这些表示构建红外有限的S矩阵，为解决红外发散问题提供了不同于修饰态方法的替代方案。

Abstract: The infrared structure of QED and gravity is known to be governed by an infinite-dimensional symmetry group which extends the Poincaré group to include, respectively, large $U(1)$ transformations and BMS supertranslations. We describe how the unitary irreducible representations (UIRs) of these asymptotic symmetry groups encode universal infrared features of a scattering process. Motivated by the goal of defining an infrared-finite $S$-matrix based on these UIRs, we also study supermomentum eigenstates and contrast our construction with the dressed-state approach for infrared-safe amplitudes.

### [84] [Spinor moving frame, type II superparticle quantization, hidden $SU(8)$ symmetry of linearized 10D supergravity, and superamplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06404)
*Igor Bandos,Mirian Tsulaia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过协变量子化（covariant quantization）IIB和IIA型超粒子（superparticles）的旋量运动框架（spinor moving frame）表述，揭示了线性化II型超重力（supergravity）的隐藏SU(8)对称性，并建立了与解析超振幅（analytic superamplitudes）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在揭示线性化II型超重力理论中隐藏的SU(8)对称性，并通过协变量子化方法建立超粒子量子态与解析超振幅之间的对应关系，为统一描述IIA和IIB型超重力多重态（supergravity multiplets）提供理论基础。

Method: 采用旋量运动框架（Lorentz harmonic）形式体系，对IIB和IIA型超粒子进行协变量子化。该方法通过引入参数化复结构选择的辅助变量，将量子态矢量实现为解析壳上超场（analytic on-shell superfield）。

Result: 研究发现IIA和IIB型超重力多重态可以用相同的解析壳上超场描述，差异仅在于时空解释。IIA情形需要引入协变常数SO(8)矢量，这与IIA和IIB超空间之间的T-对偶变换（T-duality transform）相关。文献中讨论的最简单IIB超振幅同样描述IIA过程。

Conclusion: 论文建立了II型超重力多重态的解析超场描述框架，揭示了SU(8)对称性，并指出该方法在计算多粒子IIA振幅时的限制。同时初步探讨了包含D0-膜（Dirichlet superparticles）的IIA超振幅，指出了该方向需要解决的关键问题。

Abstract: A covariant quantization of type IIB and type IIA superparticles in their spinor moving frame formulation reveals the hidden $SU(8)$ symmetry of the linearized type II supergravity. It acts on auxiliary variables parameterizing the possible choices of complex structures which is necessary to arrive at the realization of the quantum state vector as an analytic on-shell superfield, the one-particle counterpart of analytical superamplitudes for type IIB and type IIA supergravity multiplets.
  The description of the type IIA supergraity multiplet in terms of an analytic on-shell superfield is then identical to that for type IIB supermultiplet; the difference is in spacetime interpretation. However, the definition of suitable auxiliary variables in type IIA case requires introduction of covariantly constant $SO(8)$ vector which can be related to T-duality transform between type IIA and type IIB superspaces.
  The simplest analytic IIB superamplitudes discussed in the literature thus also describe type IIA processes. We elaborate on these using the spinor moving frame (Lorentz harmonic) formalism and point out the restrictions on computation of many particle type IIA amplitudes in this approach. We also briefly discuss the initial steps towards type IIA superamplitudes involving, besides supergravity multiplets, also D$0$-branes (Dirichlet superparticles), which was recently quantized in the similar formalism, and indicate some problems which appear are to be solved to proceed on this way.

</details>


### [85] [Chiral-Maxwell Cavity EFT: Photon Condensation and Quantum-Optics Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06547)
*Fabrizio Canfora,Mauricio Ipinza,Simon Riquelme*

Motivation: 研究动机在于建立有限密度强子物理与实验上熟悉的非线性腔体诊断之间的具体桥梁。通过解析描述强子介质如何诱导腔体中的光子凝聚现象，为理解强子-光子耦合系统提供理论框架。

Method: 方法基于领头阶手征微扰理论（leading-order Chiral Perturbation Theory）与麦克斯韦理论的最小耦合，构建了包含最低强子模式和规范模式的截断理论。通过单圈积分（one loop）重强子模式得到规范不变的有效势，并在相反能级下积分规范模式得到sine-Gordon型有效场论（EFT）。

Result: 研究获得了光子凝聚窗口的解析判据，并发现约化理论可映射到标准非线性量子光学哈密顿量，包括双光子拉比极限（two-photon Rabi limit）和四次单模光子模型。凝聚分支与平凡分支遵循不同的选择定则（selection rules）。

Conclusion: 该工作为有限密度强子物理与实验上熟悉的非线性腔体诊断之间建立了具体桥梁，揭示了尺度分离失效时需保持完整耦合系统，并通过离散缠绕和横向完整数据保留了三维腔体记忆。

Abstract: We develop an analytic, fully field-theoretic description of how a hadronic medium can induce photon condensation in a cavity. Starting from leading-order Chiral Perturbation Theory minimally coupled to Maxwell theory, we construct a consistent truncation to the lowest hadronic and gauge modes that still supports a non-vanishing baryon (topological) density. The resulting reduced dynamics is an effective \(1+1\) theory whose couplings retain memory of the three-dimensional cavity through discrete winding and transverse holonomy data. Integrating out the heavy hadronic mode at one loop yields a gauge-invariant effective potential for the lowest photonic cavity mode, from which we derive analytic criteria for a condensed window. In the opposite hierarchy, integrating out the gauge mode produces a one-loop deformation of a sine--Gordon-type EFT for the chiral mode and makes explicit where scale separation fails and the full coupled system must be kept. Upon quantization, the reduced theory maps onto standard nonlinear quantum-optics Hamiltonians, including a two-photon Rabi limit and quartic single-mode photonic models whose trivial and condensed branches obey distinct selection rules. This provides a concrete bridge between finite-density hadronic physics and experimentally familiar nonlinear-cavity diagnostics.

</details>


### [86] [Higher-dimensional BKL dynamics in AdS black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06560)
*Elena Cáceres,Ángel J. Murcia,Ayan K. Patra,Juan F. Pedraza*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在D≥4维渐近AdS黑洞内部构造了真实的BKL混沌动力学，证明了奇点附近的演化简化为紧致区域内的台球运动，并揭示了高维下更丰富的时代（era）内部结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BKL混沌动力学为描述类空奇点（spacelike singularities）提供了标准框架，但黑洞内部的具体实现较少，尽管全息原理（holography）重新激发了相关兴趣。本研究旨在构建具有真实BKL动力学的渐近AdS黑洞。

Method: 在D≥4维构建了渐近AdS黑洞的广泛类别，分析其内部动力学。在近奇点区域，演化简化为紧致区域内的台球运动（billiard-like motion），该区域形成规则的(D-2)-单纯形。推导了任意维度Kasner指数的闭式反弹规则。

Result: 证明了由此产生的混沌动力学。对于D≥5，发现了更丰富的时代内部结构：不同时期（epoch）之间的不等价跃迁导致不同的Kasner季节（seasons），为电墙和引力墙（electric and gravitational walls）产生了新的时期/时代结构模式。

Conclusion: 研究还探讨了全息诊断工具——热a函数（thermal a-function），其单调流（monotonic flow）能够捕捉单个时期和时代，并在合适的Kasner区域中表现出近行走行为（near-walking behavior）。

Abstract: Chaotic BKL dynamics provides a canonical description of the approach to spacelike singularities as a sequence of Kasner epochs grouped into eras. While this paradigm is well established for cosmological singularities, explicit realizations inside black holes have been scarce, despite renewed interest from holography. Here, we construct a broad class of asymptotically AdS black holes in $D\ge 4$ whose interiors exhibit bona fide BKL dynamics as the singularity is approached. In the near-singularity regime, the evolution reduces to billiard-like motion in a compact domain that forms a regular $(D-2)$-simplex. We derive closed-form bouncing rules for the Kasner exponents in arbitrary dimension and prove the ensuing chaotic dynamics. A key novelty for $D\ge 5$ is a richer internal organization of eras: inequivalent transitions between epochs lead to distinct Kasner seasons, yielding new patterns of epoch/era structure for both electric and gravitational walls. Finally, we investigate a holographic diagnostic, the thermal $a$-function, whose monotonic flow captures individual epochs and eras and can display near-walking behavior in suitable Kasner regimes.

### [87] [An ode to instantons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06575)
*Oliver Janssen,Joel Karlsson,Flavio Riccardi,Mattia Varrone*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种量子力学中的半经典时间演化形式体系，通过识别实时间中的复鞍点、复时间中的实鞍点以及复时间中的复鞍点，重现了经典问题中的已知解。对于亚稳态衰变，发现了有限时间和有限能量的"反弹"类比，这些解没有严格的零模或负模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在学习如何在具有非平凡时间依赖性的量子场论中计算衰变率，为此首先回归到量子力学的领域进行基础性探索。作者希望通过理解量子力学中的半经典时间演化，为更复杂的量子场论问题奠定基础。

Method: 作者建立了一个基于百年研究积累的半经典时间演化形式体系。该方法的核心是识别三种类型的鞍点：实时间中的复鞍点（complex saddle points in real time）、复时间中的实鞍点（real saddle points in complex time）以及复时间中的复鞍点（complex saddle points in complex time）。

Result: 该形式体系成功重现了经典问题中的已知解。对于亚稳态衰变，发现了有限时间和有限能量的"反弹"（bounce）类比，这些解没有严格的零模或负模。同时讨论了波函数的一圈相位（one-loop phase）以及晚期时间反弹解的多重性。

Conclusion: 通过回归到量子力学的基础研究，本文为理解具有时间依赖性的量子场论衰变率计算提供了重要的理论框架。所提出的半经典时间演化形式体系为处理更复杂的量子场论问题奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present a formalism for semiclassical time evolution in quantum mechanics, building on a century of work. We identify complex saddle points in real time, real saddle points in complex time, and complex saddle points in complex time that reproduce the known answers in classic problems. For the decay of a metastable state, we find finite time and finite energy analogs of the "bounce" which do not have strict zero or negative modes. The one-loop phase of the wave function and the multiplicity of bounce solutions at late times are discussed. The motivation of this work is to learn how to compute decay rates in quantum field theory in situations with non-trivial time dependence, by first taking a humble step backwards to the fascinating world of quantum mechanics.

</details>

### [88] [Restoring the Point-and-Charge Gradient Expansion for the Strong Interaction Density Functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06018)
*L. A. Constantin,F. Naeem,3 E. Fabiano,F. Sarcinella,F. Della Sala*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种用于强相互作用泛函的元广义梯度近似模型（ePC），该模型基于精确约束构建，在原子和多种模型系统中展现出良好的整体精度和更广泛的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强相互作用泛函 $W_\infty[n]$ 和 ${W'}_\infty[n]$ 在密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory）的绝热连接方法中具有重要作用。虽然严格关联电子方法可以精确计算这些泛函，但即使对于小型电子系统，计算成本也非常高昂，因此需要发展半局域近似方法。

Method: 本研究开发了一种元广义梯度近似（meta-generalized gradient approximation, meta-GGA）模型，称为增强点电荷模型（enhanced point-and-charge, ePC），该模型基于精确约束构建。ePC恢复了PC模型的二阶梯度展开，这对于维格纳晶体（Wigner crystals）的平衡性质相关，并确保了 ${W'}_\infty[n]$ 的非负性。

Result: 研究评估了ePC模型在原子和多种模型系统中的表现：胡克原子（Hooke's atoms）、双电子指数密度、s-和p-氢原子壳层、准二维无限势垒模型、微扰均匀电子气和H$_2$解离。结果表明ePC模型具有良好的整体精度。

Conclusion: ePC模型比任何先前的半局域模型实现了更广泛的适用性，为强相互作用泛函提供了一种准确且计算可行的近似方法。

Abstract: The strong-interaction functionals $W_\infty[n]$ and ${W'}_\infty[n]$ play an important role in the adiabatic-connection method of Density Functional Theory. The strictly-correlated electron approach can be used to exactly compute these functionals, yet calculations are computationally very expensive even for small electronic systems, and thus semilocal approximations have been proposed. In this work we develop a meta-generalized gradient approximation (meta-GGA) model for the strong-interaction functionals, enhanced point-and-charge (ePC), constructed from exact constraints. In particular, the ePC restores the second-order gradient expansion of the PC model, that is relevant for the equilibrium properties of Wigner crystals, and ensures the non-negativity of ${W'}_\infty[n]$. We assess the ePC model for atoms and various model systems: Hooke's atoms, two-electron exponential densities, s- and p-hydrogenic shells, quasi-two-dimensional infinite barrier model, perturbed uniform electron gas and H$_2$ dissociation. We prove a good overall accuracy of the ePC model, that achieves a broader applicability than any previous semilocal models.

</details>


### [89] [Anisotropic extension of the Parratt formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06074)
*Szilárd Sajti,László Deák*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于各向异性系统的广义帕拉特方法（generalized Parratt method），该方法避免了特征矩阵法（method of characteristic matrices）在厚样品掠入射情况下的数值不稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子与X射线反射法（neutron and X-ray reflectometry）是研究薄多层系统的重要方法。传统的帕拉特方法仅适用于各向同性系统，而特征矩阵法虽能处理各向异性问题，但在厚样品掠入射（grazing angle incidence）时存在数值不稳定性。

Method: 本文推导了适用于各向异性系统的广义帕拉特方法，该方法能够同时计算反射率（reflectivity）和透射率（transmissivity）。通过比较不同方法获得的计算结果，验证了新方法的稳定性。

Result: 新方法有效避免了特征矩阵法中的数值不稳定性问题。研究还处理了粗糙界面（rough interfaces）问题，并比较了不同近似方法在某些系统中的结果。

Conclusion: 广义帕拉特方法为各向异性系统的中子与X射线反射分析提供了稳定可靠的数值计算框架，解决了传统方法在特定条件下的局限性。

Abstract: Neutron and X-ray reflectometry are important methods for studying thin multilayer systems. The Parratt method and the method of characteristic matrices, also referred to as transfer matrices, are used for simulation, evaluation of experimental results, and designing optical systems, like mirrors. The Parratt method had been derived for isotropic systems. The method of characteristic matrices can also handle anisotropic problems, but it is burdened with numerical instabilities, which may arise in the case of thick samples at grazing angle incidence.
  In this paper, we derive a generalized Parratt method applicable to anisotropic systems. Furthermore, as we show, this is devoid of the numerical instabilities arising in the method of characteristic matrices. We derive formulae for both reflectivity and transmissivity. The stability of the new approach is demonstrated by comparing calculated results obtained via different methods. The problem of rough interfaces is also addressed, and the results gained by different approximations for some systems are compared.

</details>


### [90] [Trap-Enhanced Steep-Slope Negative-Capacitance FETs Using Amorphous Oxide Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06161)
*Yungyeong Park,Hakseon Lee,Yeonghun Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究将负电容（negative-capacitance）操作引入非晶氧化物半导体（amorphous oxide semiconductor）晶体管，通过建立模型发现：与传统MOSFET不同，随着沟道陷阱密度增加，负电容场效应晶体管（NCFET）的亚阈值摆幅（subthreshold swing）反而降低，这归因于陷阱电荷增强了负电容层的负电位降，从而实现陡峭开关特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非晶氧化物半导体（amorphous oxide semiconductors, AOSs）作为后端工艺线（back-end-of-line, BEOL）兼容晶体管的有前途沟道材料，但其高陷阱密度导致的器件性能退化一直是棘手问题。本研究旨在通过引入负电容（negative-capacitance）操作来解决这一挑战。

Method: 研究开发了AOS负电容场效应晶体管（negative-capacitance field-effect transistor, NCFET）模型，用于系统研究沟道内陷阱对陡峭斜率操作（steep-slope operation）的影响。该模型基于铁电层（ferroelectric layer）实现亚60 mV/decade亚阈值摆幅（subthreshold swing, SS）的原理。

Result: 研究发现，随着沟道陷阱密度增加，传统MOSFET的亚阈值摆幅（SS）增加，而NCFET的SS反而降低。物理机制在于：陷阱电荷增强了负电容（NC）层的负电位降，从而实现了器件的陡峭开关（abrupt device switching）。

Conclusion: 这一发现将加速基于AOS材料的BEOL晶体管及其他应用的发展，特别是结合负电容效应（NC effect）的应用。研究揭示了陷阱密度对NCFET性能的独特正面影响，为非晶氧化物半导体器件性能优化提供了新途径。

Abstract: Amorphous oxide semiconductors (AOSs) have recently gained attention as a promising channel material of back-end-of-line (BEOL)-compatible transistors for monolithic three-dimensional (3D) integrations. However, the degradation in device performance resulting from the high trap densities in AOS, compared to conventional crystalline channel materials, has remained an intractable issue. We introduce the negative-capacitance (NC) operation into the AOS-based transistors. Negative-capacitance field-effect transistors (NCFETs) have been proposed for low-power devices, enabling sub-60 mV/decade subthreshold swing SS induced by a ferroelectric layer. In this work, we develop an AOS NCFET model to investigate the influence of traps within the channel on the steep-slope operation. It is revealed that as the trap density of the channel increases, SS of the MOSFET increases, while the SS of the NCFET decreases. The physical interpretation for steep SS is attributed to the fact that the trapped charges enhance the negative potential drop of the NC layer, enabling the abrupt device switching. This finding will accelerate the development of BEOL transistors and other applications based on the AOS materials in conjunction with the NC effect.

</details>


### [91] [Density of States Weighted Decoherence Probe Formalism for Charge Transport in DNA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06461)
*Hashem Mohammad,M. P. Anantram*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于局域态密度（DOS）加权的退相干模型，用于改进DNA等纳米尺度分子系统的电荷输运模拟，避免了传统方法中能级过度展宽或虚假能级的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度分子系统如DNA需要原子级量子处理来准确描述其电学性质。模拟这些系统输运的核心挑战在于包含相位破坏散射（phase-breaking scattering），现有退相干探针（decoherence-probe）方法存在局限性：能量无关散射率会导致能级过度展宽，在能隙中产生非物理的大态密度；而能量相关模型可能引入虚假能级和传输峰，且需要额外拟合参数。

Method: 采用态密度加权（DOS-weighted）的退相干模型，其中散射率（scattering rate）及相应的退相干探针自能（decoherence probe self-energy）与局域态密度成正比。该模型通过迭代更新退相干自能和态密度直至达到自洽（self-consistency），从而获得能量和空间依赖的散射率。同时研究了避免人工电荷输运路径的分区方案（partitioning schemes）。

Result: DOS加权模型产生的能量和空间依赖散射率能够避免虚假能级，同时不会在能隙中过度展宽态密度。该模型为DNA及其他弱耦合分子系统的电荷输运模拟提供了改进且更物理的框架。

Conclusion: DOS加权退相干模型通过自洽迭代实现了物理上更合理的散射处理，避免了传统方法的缺陷，为纳米分子系统的电荷输运模拟提供了更可靠的框架。

Abstract: Nanoscale molecular systems such as DNA require an atomistic quantum treatment to accurately capture their electrical properties, owing to their small dimensions. A central challenge in modeling transport through these systems is the inclusion of phase-breaking scattering. Decoherence-probe methods enable such modeling for large systems, but existing implementations have limitations. Energy-independent scattering rates tend to overly broaden energy levels, yielding an unphysically large density of states (DOS) within energy gaps. Conversely, energy-dependent models may introduce spurious energy levels and transmission peaks and require additional fitting parameters. To address these issues, we use a DOSweighted decoherence model in which the scattering rate and equivalently, the associated decoherence probe self-energy is proportional to the local DOS. The model iteratively updates the decoherence selfenergy and the DOS until self-consistency is achieved. This approach yields energy and spatially dependent scattering rates that avoid spurious energy levels without the excessive broadening of DOS in energy gaps. We also examine the impact of partitioning schemes that prevent artificial pathways for charge transport and discuss how they can be avoided. Overall, the DOS-weighted model provides an improved and more physically grounded framework for simulating charge transport in DNA and potentially other weakly coupled molecular systems.

</details>


### [92] [Skyrmion Cyclotron Resonance in Ferrimagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06477)
*Eugene M. Chudnovsky,Dmitry A. Garanin*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文展示铁磁薄膜中斯格明子（skyrmion）的回旋共振现象，类似于金属中的电子回旋共振，可通过自旋电流或微波激发，为测量斯格明子质量提供明确方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究斯格明子回旋共振现象，旨在提供一种明确测量斯格明子质量的方法，该质量仅依赖于两个不同铁磁亚晶格之间的交换相互作用。

Method: 通过理论推导斯格明子质量的普适表达式，并以CoGd为例计算TM/RE铁磁体中斯格明子回旋频率的参数依赖性，研究单个斯格明子和斯格明子晶格中的回旋模式。

Result: 斯格明子回旋频率在角动量补偿点附近出现下降，并与铁磁共振发生杂化；该效应在微波和自旋电流实验中应足够强以被观测到。

Conclusion: 斯格明子回旋共振现象为测量斯格明子质量提供了可靠途径，其频率特性在角动量补偿点附近呈现显著变化，有望在实验中被观测和验证。

Abstract: We show that a resonance due to gyroscopic motion of skyrmions, conceptually similar to the electron cyclotron resonance in metals, can be excited in a ferrimagnetic film by a spin current or microwaves. It must permit unambiguous measurement of the skyrmion mass for which a universal expression depending solely on the exchange interaction between spins belonging to two different ferrimagnetic sublattices is derived. The dependence of the skyrmion cyclotron frequency on parameters is computed for a TM/RE ferrimagnet, using CoGd as an example. The cyclotron frequency exhibits a dip near the angular momentum compensation point, where it hybridizes with the ferromagnetic resonance. The skyrmion cyclotron mode is studied for individual skyrmions and for skyrmion lattices, where the effect must be strong enough to be observed in microwave and spin-current experiments.

</details>

### [93] [Proto-0: a prototype for validating key technologies of the DarkSide-20k experiment and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06347)
*Riccardo de Asmundis,Roberta Calabrese,Mauro Caravati,Giuliana Fiorillo,Leandro Flores,Gianfrancesco Grauso,Giuseppe Matteucci,Noemi Pino,Dmitrii Rudik,Maria Adriana Sabia,Yury Suvorov*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 论文报告了Proto-0的早期运行状态和单相调试结果，具体包括使用外部和内部校准源进行的闪烁光产额测量数据，为DarkSide-20k关键技术验证提供了实验依据。

Abstract: The DarkSide-20k experiment, currently under construction at LNGS, will employ a next-generation dual-phase liquid-argon Time Projection Chamber (TPC) with SiPM-based Photon Detector Units and low-background materials to achieve the ambitious goal of operating with an instrumental background close to zero. Proto-0 is a small-scale dual-phase argon TPC operated at INFN Naples, designed to validate the integration of DarkSide-20k key technologies in a realistic detector environment and to study charge extraction and electroluminescence signal formation. In this short paper we report on the early operation of Proto-0 and its single-phase commissioning. We focus on the measurement of the scintillation light yield using external and internal calibration sources.

</details>


### [94] [Recent GasPM advances: photon-feedback mitigation and LaB$_{6}$ photocathode studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06375)
*Simone Garnero,Kenji Inami,Kodai Matsuoka,Ryogo Okubo,Koichi Ueda*

Abstract: We report recent developments and tests with beams and cosmic rays of the gaseous photomultiplier (GasPM). In addition, the GasPM provides precise and efficient Cherenkov-based charged-particle identification if combined with a radiator. Our primary use case aims at an upgrade of the Belle II detector to suppress beam-induced background photons, preferably detected off-collision time, that degrade the performance of the electromagnetic calorimeter. In 2022 we achieved a promising single-photon time-resolution of 25 ps at 3.3 x 10$^6$ gain, using a picosecond-pulse laser and a LaB$_6$ photocathode. This work aims at addressing the principal causes of the time-resolution degradation. We primarily target ultraviolet-photon emission during excitation and de-excitation of the gas molecules, which leads to a secondary signal that overlaps the primary signal, spoiling time resolution (photon feedback). We design and execute an improved beam test. Along with several GasPM configuration changes, we introduce a new 10 GSPS frequency digitizer to better discriminate primary from secondary signals thus enabling the study of photon feedback. We also conduct a cosmic-ray test using a LaB$_6$ photocathode, which is known to have higher than CsI's resistance to ions drifting backwards onto the photocathode and to air exposure, to probe quantum efficiency in view of an upcoming beam test.

### [96] [Confined drying of a binary liquid mixture droplet: A quantitative interferometric study under humidity control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06282)
*Ole Milark,Jean-Baptiste Salmon,Benjamin Sobac*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合马赫-曾德尔干涉仪（Mach-Zehnder interferometry）、定制相对湿度控制室和受限二维液滴几何结构的方法，用于精确研究复杂流体的干燥过程及相关传输机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发精确的实验方法来研究复杂流体的干燥动力学和传输机制，特别是在受限几何结构中，以深入理解蒸发过程中的浓度场变化和传输特性。

Method: 采用马赫-曾德尔干涉测量法（Mach-Zehnder interferometry）结合定制相对湿度控制室和受限二维液滴几何结构，对水-甘油二元混合物进行高分辨率干涉成像（6 μm像素⁻¹，1帧/秒），同时测量干燥动力学和内部浓度场。

Result: 实验数据与准稳态等温模型高度吻合，能够提取浓度依赖的相互扩散系数D(φ)和水化学活性a_w(φ)，覆盖几乎整个甘油体积分数范围。荧光显微镜补充实验证实浮力驱动对流可忽略，质量扩散主导溶质传输。

Conclusion: 该方法验证了其作为定量框架的稳健性，适用于探测复杂流体的干燥动力学和传输过程，在受控蒸发研究中具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: We present a methodology that combines Mach-Zehnder interferometry, a custom relative humidity (RH) controlled chamber, and a confined two-dimensional droplet geometry to enable precise investigations of drying of complex fluids and the associated transport mechanisms. This approach is applied to a model binary mixture, water-glycerol, the concentration-dependent thermodynamic and transport properties of which are relatively well documented. High-resolution interferometric imaging (6 $μ$m pixel$^{-1}$, 1 frame s$^{-1}$) allows simultaneous measurement of drying kinetics and internal concentration fields with $\pm 0.5\%$ accuracy, characterized here over a wide range of RH (25-95%), and thus Péclet numbers. The experimental results closely match a quasisteady, isothermal model of vapor-diffusion-controlled evaporation coupled to diffusion within the droplet. These data enable extraction of both the concentration-dependent mutual diffusion coefficient $D(\varphi)$ and the water chemical activity $a_w(\varphi)$ over almost the entire range of glycerol volume fraction $\varphi$, even from a single low-RH experiment. While $a_w(\varphi)$ agrees well with literature values, our measurements yield a consistent fit for $D(\varphi)$. Complementary experiments with fluorescence microscopy confirm that buoyancy-driven convection, although present, remains negligible, so that mass diffusion dominates solute transport in this confined geometry. The overall agreement validates the methodology, demonstrating its robustness as a quantitative framework for probing drying dynamics and transport in complex fluids, with broad applicability to controlled evaporation studies.
