### [97] [Szegő type correlations for two-dimensional outpost ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06191)
*Yacin Ameur,Ena Jahic*

Main category: math.CV

TL;DR: 该论文研究二维库仑（Coulomb）系统中存在特定若尔当曲线（Jordan curve）形式"前哨"（outpost）时的关联函数渐近行为，发现这些关联具有普适性，可用特定希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）的再生核（reproducing kernel）表示，推广了Ameur和Cronvall的Szegő型边缘关联结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维库仑系统中存在若尔当曲线形式"前哨"时的关联函数渐近行为，探索此类系统的普适特性。该研究扩展了Ameur和Cronvall关于Szegő型边缘关联的工作，考虑更一般的几何构型。

Method: 分析二维库仑系统中重合集（coincidence set）包含特定若尔当曲线形式"前哨"的情况。研究沿"前哨"与液滴（droplet）外边界并集的关联函数渐近行为，采用再生核理论方法。

Result: 发现关联函数具有普适性，可用特定希尔伯特空间解析函数的再生核表示。该结果推广了Ameur和Cronvall的Szegő型边缘关联。此外还获得若干附加结果，包括存在"前哨"时插入外部点电荷（exterior point charge）的效应分析。

Conclusion: 二维库仑系统中存在若尔当曲线"前哨"时的关联函数渐近行为具有普适特性，可用再生核理论描述。该研究扩展了边缘关联理论，为理解此类系统的统计性质提供了新视角。

Abstract: We consider two-dimensional Coulomb systems for which the coincidence set contains an outpost in the form of a suitable Jordan curve. We study asymptotics for correlations along the union of the outpost and the outer boundary of the droplet. These correlations turn out to have a universal character and are given in terms of the reproducing kernel for a certain Hilbert space of analytic functions, generalizing the Szegő type edge correlations obtained recently by Ameur and Cronvall. There are several additional results, for example on the effect of insertion of an exterior point charge in the presence of an outpost.

### [98] [Frustrated supermolecules: the high-pressure phases of crystalline methane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06346)
*Marcin Kirsz,Miguel Martinez-Canales,Ayobami D. Daramola,John S. Loveday,Ciprian G. Pruteanu,Graeme J Ackland*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 甲烷（methane）复杂晶体结构可通过近球形超分子簇（supermolecular clusters）的简单堆积理解：相A基于13分子正二十面体（regular icosahedron），相B基于17分子Z16多面体的体心立方（bcc）堆积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 甲烷作为最简单的烃类，却表现出极其复杂的晶体相序列。非塑性相具有近乎但非完全立方对称性的大晶胞，且相变过程中的分子重组非常缓慢，这些现象需要理论解释。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟甲烷的有限温度晶体结构，分析其超分子簇堆积模式。

Result: 发现复杂相A基于13分子正二十面体（regular icosahedron），加上8个额外分子构成21分子晶胞；相B基于17分子Z16多面体的体心立方（bcc）堆积，每个晶胞中剩余12个分子位于四面体间隙（tetrahedral interstices）。

Conclusion: 甲烷复杂结构可理解为近球形超分子簇的简单堆积，非立方对称性源于分子的非球形特性。结构由高效堆积与熵（entropy）之间的权衡决定，分子间距离对分子取向敏感，导致受阻旋转（hindered rotation）和熵抑制。

Abstract: Methane is the simplest hydrocarbon, yet it exhibits an extraordinarily complicated series of crystal phases. Notably, the non-plastic phases have large unit cells with nearly, but not quite cubic symmetry. Furthermore, although non-polar molecules interact very weakly, their reorganisation across phase transitions is very sluggish. Here, we demonstrate that these complex structures can be understood as simple packing of near-spherical supermolecular clusters of methane molecules: the departure from cubic symmetry arising from the non-spherical nature of the molecules. We use molecular dynamics based on density functional theory calculations to simulate the finite-temperature crystal structures of methane, finding that the complex Phase A is based around a 13-molecule regular icosahedron, with 8 additional molecules forming the 21-molecule unit cell. Similarly, Phase B is based on a body-centred cubic bcc packing of 17-molecule Z16 polyhedra, with the remaining 12 molecules per cell in tetrahedral interstices. We demonstrate that the favored intermolecular separation depends sensitively on molecular orientation, leading to hindered rotation and suppressed entropy. The structures are determined by a trade-off between efficient packing and entropy.

</details>

### [99] [Fingerprinting fractons with pump-probe spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05594)
*Wei-En Tseng,Oliver Hart,Rahul Nandkishore*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文展示了如何利用泵浦-探测（pump-probe）技术对分形子（fracton）物相进行特异性诊断，通过探索X-cube相中的线子-平面子（lineon-planon）编织（braiding）过程如何被光谱学探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将传统自旋液体（spin liquids）中探测任意子（anyon）交换统计的光谱学方法扩展到分形子物相，揭示这些新型拓扑物相的独特特征。

Method: 采用泵浦-探测光谱学技术，分析X-cube相中线子-平面子的编织过程，该方法基于传统自旋液体中探测任意子交换统计的工作框架。

Result: 研究发现信号对三个关键特征敏感：三维非平凡编织统计的存在、分数化激发（fractionalized excitations）形成束缚态（bound states）的能力，以及部分激发具有线子（lineonic）特性（仅在一维可移动）。

Conclusion: 泵浦-探测光谱学不仅能探测分形子物相中任意子编织统计的存在，还能清晰区分其与传统（非分形子）自旋液体中的任意子，为分形子物相提供了特异性诊断工具。

Abstract: We demonstrate how pump-probe techniques enable specific diagnostics of fracton phases of matter by exploring how lineon-planon braiding in the paradigmatic X-cube phase may be probed spectroscopically. Our discussion builds on works explaining how to probe anyonic exchange statistics spectroscopically in traditional spin liquids. However, the extension to fracton phases reveals qualitatively new features coming from the existence of multi-anyon bound states, which alter the long-time asymptotic behavior of the signal. In particular, the signal we examine is sensitive to (i) the existence of nontrivial braiding statistics in three dimensions, (ii) the fact that some of the fractionalized excitations can form bound states, and (iii) that some of the fractionalized excitations are lineonic in nature (i.e., mobile only in one dimension). Thus, one can spectroscopically detect not only the existence of anyonic braiding statistics in fracton phases, but can crisply distinguish it from anyons in traditional (non-fractonic) spin liquids.

### [100] [The toric code under antiferromagnetic isotropic Heisenberg interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05707)
*Won Jang,Robert Peters,Thore Posske*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 研究各向同性反铁磁海森堡微扰对环面码（toric code）的影响，揭示拓扑序的微扰破坏机制及相变后的反铁磁奈尔相（Néel phase）形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究环面码在现实实现中自然出现的局域双自旋相互作用如何驱动拓扑序的破坏，理解拓扑相变机制及相变后新相的性质。

Method: 采用神经网络量子态（neural-network quantum states, NQS）计算基态，结合Schrieffer-Wolff（SW）变换的有效低能描述，通过保真度磁化率（fidelity susceptibility）、非可缩威尔逊环（non-contractible Wilson loops）的对数磁化率及拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）分析相变。

Result: 弱耦合区域数值结果与SW变换解析描述高度一致；海森堡微扰仅重整化局域算符，拓扑扇区混合需系统尺寸量级的微扰阶次；中间耦合强度下拓扑相破坏，临界点被确定；相变后出现四重简并对称破缺的反铁磁±X/±Z奈尔相。

Conclusion: 局域双自旋相互作用驱动环面码拓扑序破坏，SW方法为结合变分多体方法分析此类微扰提供了系统框架，揭示了拓扑相变到对称破缺相的转变机制。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of an isotropic antiferromagnetic Heisenberg perturbation on the toric code, focusing on the resulting quantum phase transition and the nature of the phase that emerges beyond topological order. Using neural-network quantum states (NQS), we compute ground states over a wide range of Heisenberg couplings while fully respecting the exact symmetries of the model. In the weak-coupling regime, the numerical results are in excellent agreement with an effective low-energy description derived from a Schrieffer-Wolff (SW) transformation, providing analytic control over the perturbative breakdown of topological order. We show that the Heisenberg perturbation only renormalizes local operators at low orders, whereas mixing between topological sectors occurs only at a perturbative order proportional to the system size. At intermediate values of the Heisenberg interaction, the topological phase breaks down. We estimate the critical point through a combination of the fidelity susceptibility and the logarithmic susceptibility of non-contractible Wilson loops for various system sizes. Furthermore, we utilize the topological entanglement entropy to provide a comprehensive characterization of the phase transition. Beyond the transition, an antiferromagnetic $\pm X/\pm Z$ Néel phase emerges, characterized by a fourfold-degenerate symmetry-broken manifold, which is explicitly probed using staggered-magnetization-based diagnostics. Our results show how local two-spin interactions, which naturally arise in realistic implementations of the toric code, drive the breakdown of topological order. Moreover, we establish the SW approach as a systematic framework for analyzing such perturbations in combination with variational many-body methods.

</details>


### [101] [Charge-ordered states in twisted MoTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05714)
*Sparsh Mishra,Tobias M. R. Wolf,Allan H. MacDonald*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过将扭曲MoTe₂的连续模型绝热映射到有效朗道能级问题，分析了自旋-谷极化第一价带微带中的相互作用驱动电荷密度波态。研究发现三角晶格电荷密度波态在魔角两侧占据主导，且在特定填充因子下可携带非零总陈数，为整数量子霍尔效应的重现提供了自然途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用绝热映射方法将连续模型转化为有效朗道能级问题，在投影到最低朗道能级后，通过求解多朗道能级希尔伯特空间中的自洽哈特里-福克方程来分析电荷密度波态的形成机制。

Result: 在魔角θ_c两侧，三角晶格电荷密度波态分别在MX/XM位点和MM位点占据主导；在ν_h=1/2附近出现条纹序；当ν_h>1/2时，电荷密度波态可携带非零总陈数，导致重现整数量子霍尔效应。

Conclusion: 扭曲MoTe₂系统中电荷密度波态的形成与魔角密切相关，这些态在特定条件下可呈现拓扑特性，为分数陈绝缘体与电荷密度波态之间的能量竞争提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We analyze interaction-driven charge-density-wave (CDW) states in the spin-valley polarized first valence miniband of twisted MoTe$_2$ (tMoTe$_2$) using an adiabatic mapping from the continuum model to an effective Landau-level (LL) problem. When projected to the lowest LL, the leading spatial harmonic of the moiré-periodic potential changes sign at a magic twist angle $θ_c$ where the band reaches its minimum bandwidth. By solving self-consistent Hartree-Fock equations in a multi-LL Hilbert space, we find that triangular-lattice CDW states with density maxima on MX (or XM) sites or on MM sites are favored on opposite sides of the magic angle at most filling factors and that stripe order appears near $ν_h=1/2$. We show that CDW states at $ν_h >1/2$ can carry a nonzero total Chern number, providing a natural route to reentrant integer quantum Hall effects and discuss the energy competition between fractional Chern insulator and CDW states.

### [102] [Coexisting Paramagnetic Spins and Long-Range Magnetic Order in Ba$_4$(Ru$_{0.92}$Ir$_{0.08}$)$_3$O$_{10}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05715)
*Farhan Islam,Jiasen Guo,Wei Tian,Bing Li,Xudong Huai,Thao T. Tran,Gang Cao,Zachary Morgan,Feng Ye*

TL;DR: 研究通过中子衍射、磁化率测量、原子模拟和第一性原理计算，探讨了稀Ir替代对三聚体钌酸盐Ba₄Ru₃O₁₀磁性的影响。Ir掺杂保持了母体的锯齿形反铁磁结构和磁矩大小，但降低了奈尔温度并引入了顺磁成分。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究稀Ir替代对三聚体钌酸盐Ba₄Ru₃O₁₀磁性的影响，特别是理解掺杂如何改变其磁有序和交换相互作用。

Method: 采用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）、磁化率测量（magnetic susceptibility measurements）、原子模拟（atomistic simulations）和第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）等多种实验与理论方法相结合的研究策略。

Result: Ir掺杂保持了母体的锯齿形反铁磁结构（zigzag antiferromagnetic structure），磁矩仍仅位于每个Ru₃O₁₂三聚体的两个外侧Ru(2)位点。8% Ir替代使奈尔温度（Néel temperature）从≈105K降至84.0(1)K，磁化率显示低温居里型上升，表明长程反铁磁有序与顺磁自旋共存。

Conclusion: 密度泛函计算表明Ir优先占据中心Ru(1)位点，其扩展的5d轨道破坏了Ru-Ru分子轨道网络和内外三聚体交换路径。结合顺磁稀释的原子模拟成功再现了被抑制的有序温度和有序/顺磁成分的共存现象。

Abstract: We investigate the effect of dilute Ir substitution on the magnetism of the trimer-based ruthenate Ba$_4$Ru$_3$O$_{10}$ using neutron diffraction, magnetic susceptibility measurements, atomistic simulations, and first-principles calculations. Neutron diffraction shows that Ir doping preserves the zigzag antiferromagnetic structure and the ordered-moment magnitude of the parent compound, in which the moments reside exclusively on the two outer Ru(2) sites of each $\rm Ru_3O_{12}$ trimer, while the central Ru(1) site remains nonmagnetic. The Néel temperature is reduced from $\approx\!105$ K to 84.0(1) K upon 8% Ir substitution, while magnetic susceptibility reveals a pronounced low-temperature Curie-like upturn, indicating the coexistence of paramagnetic spins with long-range antiferromagnetic order. Density-functional calculations shows that Ir preferentially occupies the central Ru(1) site, where its extended $5d$ orbitals disrupt the Ru-Ru molecular-orbital network and intra/inter-trimer exchange pathways. Atomistic simulations incorporating this paramagnetic dilution reproduce the suppressed ordering temperature and the coexistence of ordered and paramagnetic components.

### [103] [Magnetoelastic signatures of conical state and charge density waves in antiferromagnetic FeGe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05734)

Abstract: We present a unified magnetoelastic framework describing ultrasound velocity anomalies in antiferromagnetic FeGe under low magnetic fields applied along the $c$ axis. A global multi-field analysis reveals the pronounced low-temperature anomaly near 35 K originates from hybridization between longitudinal acoustic phonons and a field-dependent magnetic mode associated with the exchange-driven conical spin structure, while the shoulder near 100 K arises from a field-independent charge density wave (CDW) susceptibility channel. The fitted parameters exhibit strong internal scaling relations, allowing the data to collapse onto universal magnetic and CDW scaling curves. By explicitly connecting the magnetic scaling variable to the cone angle measured by neutron diffraction, we establish a quantitative link between ultrasound softening and the evolution of the transverse spiral component of the double-cone structure. Our results therefore unify elastic and neutron-scattering observations within a single phenomenological framework and demonstrate that $Δv/v$ provides a sensitive probe of coupled magnetic and electronic instabilities in FeGe.

Abstract: Evidence for multiple magnetic transitions and unconventional spin exchange interactions in the ilmenite insulator MnTiO3 is provided via neutron scattering. On cooling, while G-type antiferromagnetic (AFM) order sets in first at 63 K with a k1 = (000) characteristic wave vector, a weaker second magnetic transition with k2 = (00 3/2 ) appears near 42 K, giving rise to a noncollinear structure. Intrinsic buckling of the honeycomb lattice along c creates bond anisotropy and a distorted crystal field that can lead to exchange paths that modulate orbital overlap and spin-orbit coupling. The inelastic spectrum is best described by magnetic exchange anisotropy that breaks the local symmetry of the honeycomb, with competing AFM Heisenberg, Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya and alternate intra-planar ferromagnetic (FM) interactions, that may yield a weakly-coupled ladder system.

### [105] [Moiré-induced symmetry breaking of charge order in van der Waals heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05759)
*Sandra Sajan,Laura Pätzold,Tarushi Agarwal,Clara Pfister,Haojie Guo,Sisheng Duan,P. V. Sruthibhai,Mariana Rossi,Maria N. Gastiasoro,Sara Barja,Ravi P. Singh,Tim Wehling,Miguel M. Ugeda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过低温扫描隧道显微镜/谱学技术，探究了错配层状化合物(MS)₁₊δTaS₂中错配界面如何重塑嵌入的1H-TaS₂单层的电子基态，揭示了电荷密度波（CDW）在单轴莫尔势下的各向异性响应及其与超导性的不同敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 错配层状硫族化合物（misfit layered chalcogenides）结合了岩盐单硫族化合物的方形晶格和过渡金属二硫族化合物的六方晶格，为探索非公度性（incommensurability）和显式对称性破缺如何影响集体电子相提供了平台。

Method: 采用低温扫描隧道显微镜/谱学（low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy）技术探测错配化合物(MS)₁₊δTaS₂（M = Pb, Sn），并通过高分辨率STM成像和傅里叶分析研究电荷密度波（charge-density wave, CDW）的结构特征。

Result: CDW呈现非公度性并碎裂为纳米尺寸畴域，在错配层施加的单轴莫尔势（uniaxial moiré potential）下表现出显著的各向异性响应：其相干长度和有序波矢变得不等价，表明本征CDW不稳定性与对称性破缺莫尔场之间存在强非线性耦合。基于第一性原理的多尺度建模显示这种重组源于层间电荷转移和错配界面引入的空间各向异性能量景观的共同作用。

Conclusion: 超导性对莫尔势相对不敏感，表现出均匀的单全隙特征，与s波配对一致。该研究确立了异对称性堆叠（heterosymmetry stacking）作为调控范德华材料中关联态的一种途径。

Abstract: Layered materials that stack different lattice symmetries are rare in nature. Misfit layered chalcogenides, which combine square and hexagonal lattices of rocksalt monochalcogenides and transition-metal dichalcogenides, provide a platform to explore how incommensurability and explicit symmetry breaking impact collective electronic phases. Here we use low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy to probe the misfit compounds (MS)$_{1+δ}$TaS$_{2}$ with M = Pb, Sn and track how the misfit interface reshapes the electronic ground state of the embedded 1H-TaS$_{2}$ monolayers. High-resolution STM imaging and Fourier analysis reveal that the charge-density wave (CDW) is incommensurate and fragments into nanometer-sized domains. Strikingly, the CDW exhibits a pronounced and anisotropic response to the uniaxial moiré potential imposed by the misfit layer: its coherence lengths and ordering wavevectors become inequivalent, demonstrating a strong nonlinear coupling between the intrinsic CDW instability and the symmetry-breaking moiré field. First-principles-informed multiscale modeling shows that this reorganization arises from the combined effect of interlayer charge transfer and the spatially anisotropic energy landscape introduced by the misfit interface. In contrast, superconductivity is comparatively insensitive to the moiré, revealing a uniform, single full-gap consistent with s-wave pairing. Our results establish heterosymmetry stacking as a route to engineer correlated states in van der Waals materials.

### [106] [AKLT Hamiltonian from Hubbard tripods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06455)
*Claire Benjamin,Dániel Varjas,Gábor Széchenyi,Judit Romhányi,László Oroszlány*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究展示了如何从基于半填充哈伯德三脚架（Hubbard tripods）的微观费米子模型中涌现出自旋-1 AKLT哈密顿量。通过分析单三脚架、耦合对及三脚架系统，建立了从哈伯德团簇到价键固体自旋物理的具体自下而上路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索自旋-1 Affleck-Kennedy-Lieb-Tasaki（AKLT）哈密顿量如何从微观费米子模型中涌现。具体动机是建立从基于半填充哈伯德三脚架的微观模型到价键固体（valence-bond-solid）自旋物理的明确路径，为可调量子点阵列中的实现提供理论基础。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）与四阶准简并微扰理论（fourth-order quasi-degenerate perturbation theory）相结合的方法。首先分析单三脚架的低能流形，然后推导耦合三脚架对的有效双线性-双二次自旋模型（bilinear-biquadratic spin model），最后扩展到三脚架系统比较非等效耦合几何结构。

Result: 单三脚架展现出稳健的三重简并低能流形，对应有效S=1自由度，在宽泛相互作用范围内保持稳定。通过调节腿-中心跳跃（leg-center hopping）与两种对称不等价的腿-腿跳跃（leg-leg hoppings），可获得接近目标比值1/3的双二次-双线性比（biquadratic-to-bilinear ratio）。在三脚架系统中，找到了抑制不必要长程和多自旋项的策略，同时保留弱耦合区域的目标最近邻耦合。

Conclusion: 研究建立了从哈伯德团簇到价键固体自旋物理的具体自下而上路径，为在可调量子点阵列中实现AKLT哈密顿量提供了理论基础。通过适当调节跳跃参数和耦合几何结构，可在弱耦合区域获得目标最近邻相互作用。

Abstract: We investigate how the spin-1 Affleck-Kennedy-Lieb-Tasaki (AKLT) Hamiltonian can emerge from a microscopic fermionic model based on half-filled Hubbard tripods. We first show that a single tripod hosts a robust threefold-degenerate low-energy manifold corresponding to an effective $S = 1$ degree of freedom. This manifold prevails over a broad range of interactions and remains stable against moderate disorder. We then combine exact diagonalization with fourth-order quasi-degenerate perturbation theory to derive an effective bilinear-biquadratic spin model for a pair of coupled tripods and identify coupling regimes where the target ratio is approached. In particular, tuning leg-center hopping together with two symmetry-inequivalent leg-leg hoppings yields the characteristic singlet-triplet degeneracy associated with a biquadratic-to-bilinear ratio close to 1/3. Extending the analysis to three tripods, we compare nonequivalent coupling geometries and find a strategy that suppresses unwanted longer-range and multispin terms while preserving the target nearest-neighbor couplings in the weak-coupling regime. These results establish a concrete bottom-up route from Hubbard clusters to valence-bond-solid spin physics in tunable quantum-dot arrays.

### [107] [Parity readout in Majorana box qubits from the dispersive to the resonant regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06482)
*Sara M. Benjadi,Reinhold Egger*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究分析了马约拉纳盒量子比特中马约拉纳宇称自由度的电荷反射测量和电容读取的理论模型，考虑了退相干通道，并提供了从共振到非共振色散区域的全交叉覆盖的广义动力学磁化率表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立马约拉纳盒量子比特中马约拉纳宇称（Majorana parity）自由度读取的理论模型，特别关注电荷反射测量（charge reflectometry）和电容读取（capacitive readout）两种方案，同时考虑退相干通道（decoherence channels）的影响。

Method: 采用林德布拉德主方程（Lindblad master equation）框架分析退相干通道，推导出支配两种读取方案的宇称依赖动力学磁化率χ_z(ω)的广义表达式，并重新检验了在半经典因子化假设（semiclassical factorization assumption）下获得的先前结果。

Result: 研究提供了覆盖从共振区域（resonant regime）到非共振色散区域（off-resonant dispersive regime）全交叉的χ_z(ω)广义表达式。在色散区域，半经典近似在三种不同误差度量下得到定量验证；但在共振区域，与完整林德布拉德方程稳态数值解相比，发现存在约百分之几的偏差。

Conclusion: 半经典因子化近似在色散读取区域是合理的，但在共振区域需要更精确的处理，因为该近似会导致与精确数值解相比约百分之几的误差。

Abstract: We study theoretical models for charge reflectometry and capacitive readout of the Majorana parity degree of freedom in Majorana box qubits, taking into account decoherence channels within the framework of the Lindblad master equation. Noting that a parity-dependent dynamical susceptibility $χ_z(ω)$ governs both readout schemes, we provide a general expression for $χ_z(ω)$ which covers the full crossover from the resonant regime to the off-resonant dispersive regime. In addition, we re-examine previous results which were obtained under a semiclassical factorization assumption. Using three different error measures, we show that this approximation is quantitatively justified in the dispersive regime. In the resonant regime, however, we find deviations from exact reference data, obtained by numerical solution for the steady state of the full Lindblad equation. These deviations are typically of the order of a few percent in the considered error measures.

### [108] [Tomographic collective modes in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06518)
*Jeff Maki,Johannes Hofmann*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值精确求解线性化玻尔兹曼方程，分析了二维费米液体在磁场作用下从层析输运（tomographic transport）向常规输运转变的集体模式演化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维费米液体在低温下存在奇偶效应（odd-even effect），导致奇偶宇称费米面形变具有不同的弛豫速率，从而产生混合流体力学与无碰撞输运的层析输运（tomographic transport）新机制。然而，当磁场存在且回旋半径小于主导奇宇称平均自由程时，这种层析输运预期会向常规输运转变。

Method: 采用数值精确求解线性化玻尔兹曼方程（linearized Boltzmann equation）的方法，在广义弛豫时间近似（generalized relaxation time approximation）框架下分析奇宇称和偶宇称模式。同时使用变分方法（variational approach）处理费米面形变，以捕捉形变的角结构和临界磁场强度。

Result: 无磁场时，横向电导率呈现两个扩散型层析集体模式（diffusive tomographic collective modes）。在临界磁场下，其中一个层析模式消失，而持续存在的模式取决于朗道参数（Landau parameters）。高磁场下，剩余模式逐渐由流体力学模式主导。变分方法验证了形变角结构和临界磁场强度的分析结果。

Conclusion: 通过分析有限磁场中纵向和横向电流响应的阻尼，原则上可以观测到这些集体模式。该研究揭示了磁场如何调控二维费米液体从层析输运向常规输运的转变机制。

Abstract: Two-dimensional Fermi liquids at low temperatures have been theoretically established to exhibit an odd-even effect in the collective quasiparticle relaxation rates where even-parity deformations of the Fermi surface decay at a much faster rate than odd-parity ones. A predicted consequence of this effect is a new tomographic transport regime that mixes hydrodynamic and collisionless transport. In the presence of a magnetic field, however, the tomographic regime is expected to evolve towards conventional transport regimes as soon as the cyclotron radius becomes smaller than the dominant odd-parity mean free path. In this work, we examine this transition from the point of view of collective modes, using a numerically exact solution of the linearized Boltzmann equation within a generalized relaxation time approximation for the odd-parity and even-parity modes. In the absence of a magnetic field, the transverse conductivity exhibits two diffusive tomographic collective modes, and we find that at a critical magnetic field one of these two tomographic modes disappears. Which tomographic mode persists depends on the Landau parameters, with the remaining mode becoming increasingly dominated by hydrodynamic modes at high fields. We corroborate our analysis using a variational approach for the Fermi surface deformation that captures the angular structure of the deformation and the critical magnetic field strength. The collective modes discussed here can in principle be observed by examining the damping of longitudinal and transverse current responses in finite magnetic fields.

</details>

### [109] [Disentangling the Galactic binary zoo: Machine learning classification of stellar remnant binaries in LISA data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06341)
*Irwin Khai Cheng Tay,Valeriya Korol,Thibault Lechien*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 激光干涉空间天线（LISA）将探测数万个银河系致密双星系统，但不同种群（如双白矮星、中子星-白矮星）的引力波特征高度重叠。本研究评估了机器学习方法在仅基于LISA观测数据对这些双星进行分类的能力，发现梯度提升算法（如XGBoost）在高度不平衡数据集上表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA将在毫赫兹引力波频段开启新的观测窗口，探测银河系内数万个致密恒星残骸双星系统。然而，不同种群（如双白矮星WDWD、中子星-白矮星NSWD）的引力波特征存在强烈重叠，使得区分这些种群具有挑战性。

Method: 研究使用基于种群合成研究构建的银河系双星模拟目录，评估了一系列机器学习分类器。重点考察了集成方法，特别是梯度提升算法（如XGBoost），并将其性能与基于核密度估计的简单统计方法进行比较。

Result: 集成方法在高度不平衡数据集上表现最佳：双白矮星系统召回率约99%，高质量双星系统召回率≥85%。中子星-白矮星系统最难区分，但XGBoost仍能正确识别85.6%的NSWD系统，优于核密度估计方法。机器学习分类还能有效支持识别偏心双星和极稀有亚类。

Conclusion: 机器学习技术能够有效支持LISA数据的解释，特别是在高度不平衡的引力波源分类任务中。梯度提升算法在区分重叠特征的双星种群方面表现出色，为未来LISA观测数据的分析提供了有力工具。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will open a new observational window in the millihertz gravitational-wave band, enabling the detection of tens of thousands of compact stellar remnant binaries across the Milky Way. Most of LISA's sources will be double white dwarf (WDWD) systems, while neutron star-white dwarf (NSWD) binaries and higher-mass systems will be orders of magnitude rarer but of significant astrophysical interest. Disentangling these populations is challenging due to the strong overlap in their gravitational-wave features. In this work, we investigate the use of machine-learning techniques to classify LISA-detectable binaries based solely on LISA observables.
  Using mock catalogues of Galactic binaries constructed from population-synthesis studies, we evaluate a range of machine-learning classifiers. We find that ensemble-based methods-particularly gradient-boosting algorithms such as XGBoost-deliver the best performance on our highly imbalanced dataset. WDWD systems are identified with a recall of $\sim 99\%$, reflecting their dominant presence, and high-mass binaries are also classified with high recall ($\ge 85\%$). In contrast, NSWD systems remain the most challenging population to distinguish: their features overlap strongly with those of WDWD binaries, making them particularly prone to misclassification. Despite this, XGBoost correctly identifies 85.6% of NSWD systems in our simulated LISA detections, outperforming simple statistical approaches based on kernel density estimation. We further demonstrate that machine-learning classification can effectively support the interpretation of LISA data, enabling the identification of eccentric binaries and extremely rare subclasses.

</details>

Some of the abstract results involved can also be used to address similar questions about a rank-one perturbation of the Laplacian. Exact asymptotic properties are also obtained for the sojourn time, the scattering amplitude and time delay.

### [111] [A Lattice QCD study of $p-Λ$ scattering in continuum and chiral limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05854)
*Hang Liu,Liuming Liu,Jin-Xin Tan,Wei Wang,Haobo Yan,Qian-Teng Zhu*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究首次系统性地利用格点QCD（lattice QCD）计算了质子-Λ粒子（p-Λ）散射，通过七组(2+1)-味（flavor）格点系综（lattice ensembles）和Lüscher有限体积方法（finite-volume method），获得了两个S波通道的散射长度（scattering length）和有效力程（effective range），结果与实验测量一致，表明p-Λ系统存在吸引相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在首次系统性地从格点QCD（lattice QCD）角度研究质子-Λ粒子（p-Λ）散射，为核力理论（nuclear force theories）的统一和中子星状态方程（neutron star equations of state）的构建提供关键输入数据。

Method: 采用七组(2+1)-味（flavor）格点系综（lattice ensembles），覆盖π介子质量（pion masses）135-317 MeV和三个格点间距（lattice spacings）。使用Lüscher有限体积方法（finite-volume method）、有效力程展开（effective range expansion）以及手征/连续外推（chiral/continuum extrapolations）进行分析。

Result: 对于¹S₀通道，获得散射长度倒数（inverse of scattering length）为0.177(83) GeV，有效力程（effective range）为2.9(1.4) fm；对于³S₁通道，分别为0.016(76) GeV和1.8(1.1) fm。从S波相移（S-wave phase shifts）推导出p-Λ散射截面（scattering cross section），所有结果与实验测量吻合良好，表明系统存在吸引相互作用（attractive interactions）。

Conclusion: 该研究首次从格点QCD（lattice QCD）系统性地确定了p-Λ散射参数，为核力理论（nuclear force theories）的统一和中子星状态方程（neutron star equations of state）的构建提供了关键输入，证实了p-Λ系统存在吸引相互作用。

Abstract: We present a first systematic study of $I=1/2$ proton-$Λ$ ($p$-$Λ$) scattering from lattice QCD, using seven sets of $(2+1)$-flavor lattice ensembles with pion masses spanning 135-317 MeV and three lattice spacings with $a=(0.052,0.077, 0.105)$ fm. Using Lüscher's finite-volume method, effective range expansion and chiral/continuum extrapolations, we obtain the inverse of scattering length and effective range for the $^1S_0$ channel as 0.177(83) GeV and 2.9(1.4) fm, and for the $^3S_1$ channel as 0.016(76) GeV and 1.8(1.1) fm. From the derived S-wave phase shifts, we provide an estimate of the $p-Λ$ scattering cross section. Our results for scattering length, effective range and cross sections are in good agreement with available experimental measurements. We also find that the $p-Λ$ system sustains attractive interactions. These results provide critical input for the unification of nuclear force theories and the construction of neutron star equations of state.

</details>


### [112] [Hamiltonian Lattice QED$_3$ with One and Two Flavors of Wilson Fermions: Topological Structure and Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05616)
*Sriram Bharadwaj,Emil Rosanowski,Simran Singh,Alice di Tucci,Changnan Peng,Karl Jansen,Lena Funcke,Di Luo*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究澄清了(2+1)D量子电动力学中拓扑相模拟的关键障碍，发现交错费米子离散化具有精确的时间反演对称性，阻碍了非平凡拓扑相的出现。通过系统分析费米子离散化效应，证明威尔逊费米子能够自然实现具有非零陈数的拓扑区域，并为近期量子模拟提供了具体基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子模拟(2+1)D量子电动力学中的拓扑相为近期晶格实验实现拓扑现象提供了有前景的途径。然而，现有文献中存在混淆，因为哈密顿规范理论中常用的交错费米子离散化具有精确的时间反演对称性，阻碍了非平凡拓扑相的出现。

Method: 通过系统分析(2+1)D晶格哈密顿量中费米子与U(1)规范场耦合时的离散化效应，满足高斯定律。开发了拓扑响应的规范不变诊断方法，包括多体陈数和电流关联函数，这些在弱耦合下保持稳健。通过广泛的精确对角化计算，跨越两种味设置来表征谱、关联函数和拓扑不变量。

Result: 威尔逊费米子即使在最小单味理论中也能自然实现具有非零陈数的拓扑区域，而有限化学势下的双味扩展进一步丰富了可访问的拓扑结构。规范不变诊断方法在弱耦合下保持稳健，精确对角化计算提供了谱、关联函数和拓扑不变量的具体表征。

Conclusion: 该工作为晶格场论中拓扑相的近期量子模拟提供了具体基础，解决了交错费米子离散化带来的障碍。威尔逊费米子方法能够实现丰富的拓扑结构，相关结果在联合提交的文献[1]中进一步分析了其对晶格场论量子模拟的影响。

Abstract: The quantum simulation of topological phases in (2+1)D quantum electrodynamics with Wilson fermions provides a promising route toward realizing topological phenomena in near-term lattice experiments. We show that the commonly used staggered-fermion discretizations in Hamiltonian gauge theories possesses an exact time-reversal symmetry, which forbids the emergence of nontrivial topological phases and has led to confusion in the existing literature. In this work, we resolve this obstacle by systematically analyzing fermion discretization effects in (2+1)D lattice Hamiltonians of fermions coupled to U(1) gauge fields that satisfy Gauss' law. We show that Wilson fermions, already in the minimal one-flavor theory, naturally enable topological regimes with nonzero Chern numbers, and that the two-flavor extension at finite chemical potential further enriches the accessible topological structure. We develop gauge-invariant diagnostics of topological response, including many-body Chern numbers and current correlators that remain robust probes at weak coupling. Finally, through extensive exact diagonalization calculations across both flavor settings, we characterize the spectrum, correlators, and topological invariants, providing a concrete foundation for near-term quantum simulations of topological phases in lattice field theories. The implications of this work for quantum simulations of lattice field theory are analyzed in a joint submission [1].

### [113] [Failing to keep the balance: explicit formulae and topological recursion for leaky Hurwitz numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06094)
*Marvin Anas Hahn,Reinier Kramer*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了泄漏赫维茨数（leaky Hurwitz numbers）的枚举不变量，证明了其在热带几何框架下的分段多项式性质，并建立了与拓扑递归（topological recursion）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 泄漏赫维茨数作为对数交理论（logarithmic intersection theory）中的新型枚举不变量，其热带覆盖解释中平衡条件失效，需要深入研究其数学性质。

Method: 采用热带几何（tropical geometry）方法证明分段多项式性质，利用热带组合学（tropical combinatorics）和生成函数学（generatingfunctionology）推导闭式公式，并通过哈密顿流（Hamiltonian flows）将谱曲线（spectral curves）与切割-连接算子（cut-and-join operators）关联。

Result: 证明了泄漏完成循环赫维茨数（leaky completed cycles Hurwitz numbers）的分段多项式性质，发现了三次而非二次的壁交叉现象（wall crossing），推导了亏格0下一部分和两部分情况的闭式公式，并在固定泄漏性条件下证明了拓扑递归的满足性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了泄漏赫维茨数与拓扑递归的深刻联系，为Alexandrov-Bychkov-Dunin-Barkowski-Kazarian-Shadrin关于KP τ-函数（KP τ-functions）的工作提供了部分逆结果，特别适用于完成循环泄漏赫维茨数。

Abstract: Recently a new family of enumerative invariants called leaky Hurwitz numbers was introduced by Cavalieri-Markwig-Ranganathan in the context of logarithmic intersection theory. They admit an interpretation via tropical covers where the balancing condition fails. We employ tropical geometry to prove a generalisation of the piecewise polynomiality of Accadia-Karev-Lewanski for leaky completed cycles Hurwitz numbers, and a different wall crossing that is cubic instead of quadratic. Using tropical combinatorics and generatingfunctionology, we also find closed formulae for one-part and two-part completed cycles leaky Hurwitz numbers in genus $0$. Working more generally with a view towards topological recursion, we use Hamiltonian flows to associate spectral curves to very general cut-and-join operators. Under mild analytic constraints, we find the appropriate spectral curves, and in case the leakiness is fixed, we show that the resulting enumerative invariants satisfy topological recursion. This provides a partial inverse to recent work of Alexandrov-Bychkov-Dunin-Barkowski-Kazarian-Shadrin producing differentials satisfying topological recursion for KP $τ$-functions. In particular these results specialise to completed cycles leaky Hurwitz numbers.

### [114] [Universal Displacements in Linear Strain-Gradient Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05533)
*Dimitris Sfyris,Arash Yavari*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 该研究推导了三维线性应变梯度弹性理论中所有48个材料对称类别的普适位移场，建立了相应的普适偏微分方程，并确定了完整的普适位移集合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展Yavari (2020)的方法，在Toupin-Mindlin第一应变梯度理论框架下，系统研究三维线性应变梯度弹性中的普适位移场问题。重点在于为每个材料对称类别建立普适性条件。

Method: 基于Yavari (2020)的方法，通过要求平衡方程（无体力条件下）对给定对称类别的所有材料都成立，推导出每个材料对称类别的普适偏微分方程。采用完整的对称分类和弹性张量的紧凑矩阵表示，为所有48个应变梯度对称类别提供显式表征。

Result: 对于多个高对称性类别（如各向同性类别SO(3)和O(3)），应变梯度普适偏微分方程未施加超出经典理论的额外限制，普适位移族与经典线性弹性理论一致。对于低对称性类别，应变梯度普适偏微分方程比经典对应方程更严格，普适位移形成经典普适位移族的真子集。

Conclusion: 研究系统表征了三维应变梯度弹性中所有对称类别的普适位移场，揭示了应变梯度效应对普适位移的影响取决于材料对称性：高对称性类别保持经典结果，而低对称性类别则受到更严格的限制。

Abstract: We study universal displacement fields in three-dimensional linear strain-gradient elasticity within the Toupin-Mindlin first strain-gradient theory. Building on the approach of Yavari (2020), we derive, for each material symmetry class, the universality PDEs obtained by requiring the equilibrium equations (in the absence of body forces) to hold for any material in that class, and we determine the complete set of universal displacements. Using the full symmetry classification together with compact matrix representations of the elasticity tensors, we provide explicit characterizations for all 48 strain-gradient symmetry classes, including centrosymmetric and chiral classes. For several high-symmetry classes, the strain-gradient universality PDEs impose no additional restrictions beyond the classical ones, so the universal displacement families coincide with those of classical linear elasticity (for example, the isotropic classes SO(3) and O(3)). For lower symmetry classes, the strain-gradient universality PDEs can be stricter than their classical counterparts, so the universal displacements form proper subsets of the classical universal displacement families due to additional higher-order differential conditions.

Abstract: In this paper we consider the operad of holomorphic disk embeddings of the unit disk $\mathbb D \subset \mathbb C$. We introduce a suboperad $\mathbb{CE}_2^{HS}$ defined by square-integrability conditions and show that the symmetric algebra $\mathrm{Sym} A^{2}(\mathbb D)$ of the Bergman space carries a natural $\mathbb{CE}_2^{HS}$-algebra structure. Conformally flat factorization homology with coefficients in $\mathrm{Sym} A^{2}(\mathbb D)$ then yields metric-dependent invariants of two-dimensional Riemannian manifolds. Moreover, $\mathrm{Sym} A^{2}(\mathbb D)$ is identified with the ind-Hilbert space completion of the affine Heisenberg vertex operator algebra.

### [116] [Black bounce as a quantum correction from string T-duality: Thermodynamics, energy conditions, and observational imprints from EHT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05543)
*G. Alencar,T. M. Crispim,Diego Sáez-Chillón Gómez,Marcos V. de S. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 基于弦论（string theory）启发的T-对偶（T-duality）有效能量密度，构建了包含最小长度尺度$l_0$的非奇异几何，实现了从规则黑洞（regular black holes）到可穿越虫洞（traversable wormholes）的平滑过渡，并通过事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）观测数据约束了参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究在经典框架内实现了黑洞反弹（black bounce）场景的几何实现，构建了无奇异的静态球对称时空；通过观测数据约束了最小长度参数，分析了热力学稳定性与能量条件（energy conditions）违反情况，为弦论启发的量子引力效应提供了具体几何模型。

Abstract: Motivated by quantum gravity effects suggested by string theory, we investigate gravitational configurations sourced by an effective energy density inspired by T-duality. This density naturally introduces a minimal length scale $l_0$ that acts as an ultraviolet regulator, allowing the description of nonsingular geometries within a classical framework. By employing it as the matter source in the Einstein equations, we construct static and spherically symmetric spacetimes that interpolate smoothly between regular black holes and traversable wormholes, providing a geometric realization of the black bounce scenario. We examine the curvature invariants and confirm the absence of curvature singularities throughout the spacetime. The conditions for the existence of event horizons are analyzed in detail, which allows us to determine the causal structure of the solution. A comprehensive study of the geodesic motion is performed for both massive and massless particles, revealing the presence of photon circular orbits and an innermost stable circular orbit for massive particles. Using observational data from the Event Horizon Telescope, we constrain the minimal length parameter through the black hole shadow radius, finding that for $l_0 \lesssim 1.15\, M_{\text{ADM}}$ our solution remains consistent with observations within the $2σ$ confidence level. The optical appearance of spacetime is further investigated by considering a thin accretion disk surrounding the black bounce. From the heat capacity, we analyze the thermodynamic stability of the solution and identify the presence of a phase transition. Finally, we examine the energy conditions and discuss which of them are violated by the effective fluid supporting this geometry.

### [118] [Advancing the Effective-One-Body Framework in the Test-Mass Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05601)
*Nami Nishimura,Alessandra Buonanno,Guglielmo Faggioli,Maarten van de Meent,Gaurav Khanna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出SEOB-TML，一种针对测试质量极限优化的增强型有效单体框架，用于准圆形、自旋对齐的双黑洞系统。该框架通过四极因子化通量映射、现象学衔接处方和准正则模混合建模，显著提高了波形精度，特别是在逆行构型中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有有效单体（EOB）框架在测试质量极限（test-mass limit）下需要进一步优化，特别是在处理极端质量比系统时，需要更准确地捕捉复杂的物理调制效应，如逆行构型中的显著特征。

Method: 采用四极因子化（Q-factorized）处方将总能量通量（包括视界吸收）映射到单一(2,2)模基线；使用现象学假设替代传统的准圆形修正，实现灵活的模依赖衔接；利用qnmfinder从数值波形中提取准正则模系数，显式建模模混合效应；并在全波形中实现(2,0)模。

Result: 该框架显著降低了残差，特别是在逆行构型中捕捉了复杂的物理调制；生成了高度精确的晚期旋近-并合-铃荡波形，显著减少了失相并改善了近并合重建；与当前最先进的SEOBNRv5HM模型相比，展示了优越性能。

Conclusion: SEOB-TML框架通过专门化开发，将有效单体框架的可靠性扩展到测试质量极限，为极端质量比系统提供了高度准确的晚期旋近-并合-铃荡波形，显著提升了波形建模精度。

Abstract: We present SEOB-TML, an enhanced effective-one-body (EOB) framework for the test-mass limit, optimized for quasi-circular, spin-aligned binary black holes. On the dynamical side, we introduce a quadrupole-factorized (Q-factorized) prescription that maps the total energy flux-including horizon absorption-onto a single (2,2) mode baseline. This approach effectively captures higher-order multipole contributions without explicit mode summation, while simultaneously leading to a dramatic reduction in fractional flux errors. To ensure a smooth transition to the post-merger stage, we replace traditional next-to-quasicircular corrections with a phenomenological ansatz, enabling a flexible, mode-dependent attachment prescription. For the merger-ringdown stage, we utilize quasi-normal mode coefficients extracted from numerical waveforms via qnmfinder to explicitly model mode-mixing effects. These enhancements lead to a substantial reduction in residuals, capturing the complex physical modulations prominent in retrograde configurations. Additionally, we implement the (2,0) mode across the full waveform, further extending the model's physical coverage and accuracy. Overall, our framework generates highly accurate late inspiral-merger-ringdown waveforms for extreme-mass-ratio systems, significantly reducing dephasing and improving the near-merger reconstruction. We demonstrate the performance of SEOB-TML against the current state-of-the-art SEOBNRv5HM model, highlighting how our specialized developments extend the reliability of the EOB framework into the test-mass limit.

</details>


### [119] [The continuum spectrum of nonrelativistic multi-frequency Proca stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05602)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多频率Proca星的动机在于探索自引力大质量矢量场的激发平衡构型，这些构型与常规定态共存于s=1薛定谔-泊松系统的解空间中，并需要理解它们在超轻暗物质模型中证明粒子自旋的潜在意义。

Result: 研究发现多频率Proca星在恒定极化的离散定态之间形成连续插值，并且证明了这些多频率构型的一个子集对于一般扰动是线性稳定的。

Conclusion: 多频率Proca星作为自引力矢量场的激发平衡构型，其连续谱和稳定性分析为理解超轻暗物质模型中粒子自旋的证明提供了潜在的理论基础。

Abstract: Multi-frequency Proca stars are excited equilibrium configurations of a selfgravitating massive vector field that coexist with conventional stationary states in the solution space of the $s=1$ Schrödinger-Poisson system. In this paper, we present a systematic study of the continuum spectrum of spherical multi-frequency Proca stars and show that they interpolate between the discrete set of stationary states of constant polarization. Furthermore, we also analyze their stability and demonstrate that a subset of these multi-frequency configurations are linearly stable against general perturbations. We briefly discuss the potential implications of multi-frequency states for proving the particle spin in ultralight dark matter models.

### [120] [State-Selective Signatures of Quantum and Classical Gravitational Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05731)
*Partha Nandi,Sankarshan Sahu,Bibhas Ranjan Majhi,Francesco Petruccione*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究建立了一个统一框架，用于区分引力波背景是表现为经典场还是真正的量子环境。研究发现，量子化引力子浴在最低声子数流形内保持相干性，而经典随机引力波场即使在该子空间内也会引发退相干，这为使用介观光力学系统诊断引力波的经典或量子性质提供了操作标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一个统一框架，以确定引力波背景是表现为经典场还是真正的量子环境。这有助于解决引力波本质的基本问题，并为实验探测提供理论基础。

Method: 方法基于从测地线偏离导出的相同潮汐耦合，构建了统一的相互作用哈密顿量。关键区别在于将引力波自由度建模为经典相位随机相干态还是量子化引力子模式，在此共同框架下分析量子谐振子的约化动力学。

Result: 结果显示量子化引力子浴在最低声子数流形内保持相干性，形成受保护扇区；而经典随机引力波场即使在该子空间内也会引发退相干。这种结构差异为诊断引力波的经典或量子性质提供了操作标准。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，退相干结构（而不仅仅是其幅度）可作为引力量子性的敏感探针。该工作界定了此类测试可能变得可行的实验参数范围，为使用介观光力学系统探测引力波的量子本质奠定了基础。

Abstract: A unified framework is developed for determining whether a gravitational-wave (GW) background behaves as a classical field or as a genuinely quantum environment. Unified here means that both descriptions originate from the same tidal coupling derived from geodesic deviation, which yields an identical quadratic interaction Hamiltonian for the detector; the only distinction lies in whether the GW degrees of freedom are modeled as classical phase-randomized coherent states or as quantized graviton modes. Within this common framework, the reduced dynamics of a quantum harmonic oscillator exhibit a sharp structural contrast: a quantized graviton bath preserves coherence within the lowest phonon-number manifold, forming a protected sector at leading order, whereas a classical stochastic GW field inevitably induces decoherence even inside this subspace. This difference provides an operational criterion for diagnosing the classical or quantum nature of gravitational waves using mesoscopic optomechanical systems. Our results establish decoherence structure - not merely its magnitude - as a sensitive probe of gravitational quantumness and delineate the experimental regimes under which such tests may become feasible.

### [121] [Accelerating Numerical Relativity Simulations with New Multistep Fourth-Order Runge-Kutta Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05763)
*Lucas Timotheo Sanches,Steven Robert Brandt,Jay Kalinani,Liwei Ji,Erik Schnetter*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了显式四阶精度多步龙格-库塔（MSRK）方法，通过重用先前时间步的数据减少中间阶段计算量，旨在加速依赖龙格-库塔方法的高性能计算应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多求解微分方程的高性能计算（HPC）应用依赖龙格-库塔（Runge-Kutta）方法进行时间积分，其中四阶精度RK4方案尤为流行。该方案需要计算四个中间阶段，对于复杂问题计算代价高昂，因此需要开发更高效的方法。

Method: 本文开发了显式四阶精度多步龙格-库塔（Multistep Runge-Kutta, MSRK）方法，通过重用先前时间步的数据减少中间阶段计算。提出了一种通过调整稳定性区域来获取和优化方法系数的程序，以最大化时间步长。

Result: 新方法在数值相对论（Numerical Relativity）应用中使用EinsteinToolkit进行了验证和评估。结果表明这些方法能够有效减少计算量，并有望推广到其他使用显式龙格-库塔方法的应用中。

Conclusion: 开发的显式四阶精度多步龙格-库塔方法通过重用历史数据减少中间阶段计算，具有加速高性能计算应用的潜力。该方法在数值相对论应用中已验证有效，并预期可推广至其他使用显式龙格-库塔方法的领域。

Abstract: Many HPC applications that solve differential equations rely on the Runge-Kutta family of methods for time integration. Among these methods, the fourth-order accurate RK4 scheme is especially popular. This time integration scheme requires applications to evaluate four intermediate stages to take one time step. Depending on the complexity of the problem being solved, the evaluation of these intermediate stages can be computationally expensive. In this paper we develop explicit fourth-order accurate Multistep Runge-Kutta (MSRK) methods. The advantage of such methods is that they re-use data from previous time steps, thus requiring fewer intermediate stage evaluations and potentially speeding up applications. We outline a procedure to obtain and tune the method's coefficients by adjusting their stability regions in an attempt to maximize the size that a time step can take. We validate and evaluate our new methods in the context of Numerical Relativity applications using the EinsteinToolkit. We believe, however, that these methods and results should generalize to other applications using explicit Runge-Kutta methods.

### [122] [Searching for precessing binary systems with mode-by-mode filtering and marginalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05784)
*Zihan Zhou,Digvijay Wadekar,Javier Roulet,Oryna Ivashtenko,Tejaswi Venumadhav,Tousif Islam,Ajit Kumar Mehta,Jonathan Mushkin,Mark Ho-Yeuk Cheung,Barak Zackay,Matias Zaldarriaga*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究开发了新的进动（precessing）双黑洞引力波搜索方法，通过逐模滤波和边缘化技术处理自旋进动效应，结合机器学习优化模板库和先验采样，将搜索敏感体积提升了约10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）的双黑洞引力波搜索大多假设自旋与轨道角动量对齐，忽略了自旋进动（spin-precession）效应，可能导致错过重要信号。进动搜索面临两大挑战：自旋错位引入额外自由度导致模板数量激增，以及背景触发率增加。

Method: 采用Fairhurst等人（2019）的进动谐波分解（precession harmonic decomposition），对每个进动谐波（precessing harmonic）分别进行数据滤波。在检测统计量中对不同谐波的信噪比（SNR）进行边缘化（marginalization）而非最大化处理。结合机器学习方法：使用奇异值分解（singular value decomposition）和随机森林回归器（random forest regressor）减少主导进动谐波模板的冗余；利用归一化流（normalizing flows）为边缘化统计量生成谐波信噪比的最优先验样本。

Result: 研究表明，对谐波模式信噪比进行边缘化处理（而非最大化）可将搜索敏感体积（sensitive volume）提升约10%。该框架在LVK数据中的具体搜索结果将在后续论文中报告。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的进动信号模板库构建方法，结合逐模滤波、边缘化技术和机器学习优化，有效解决了自旋进动引力波搜索中的模板冗余和背景触发问题，显著提升了搜索效率。

Abstract: Nearly all previous binary black hole searches in LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA (LVK) gravitational wave data have assumed that the component spins are aligned with the orbital angular momentum, thereby neglecting spin-precession effects in the waveform, which can lead to potentially missing interesting signals. Precessing searches are challenging, because the extra degrees of freedom due to misaligned spins lead to: $(i)$ a much larger number of templates compared to the aligned-spin configurations, $(ii)$ an increased rate of background triggers. To address this, we develop novel precessing signal template banks using mode-by-mode filtering and marginalization methods. We use the precession harmonic decomposition from Fairhurst et al. (2019) and filter each precessing harmonic separately with the data. We then marginalize over the SNRs from different harmonics in our detection statistic. We also use machine learning methods to improve our search efficiency: $(i)$ we use singular value decomposition together with random forest regressor to reduce redundancy in the dominant precessing-harmonic templates; $(ii)$ we use normalizing flows to generate optimal prior samples for harmonic SNRs for the marginalized statistic. We show that marginalizing (instead of maximizing) over the harmonic mode SNRs increases the search sensitive volume by $\sim 10\%$. Results from searching in LVK data using this framework will be reported in a companion paper.

</details>

The app combines video feeds from the front- and rear-facing iPhone cameras and uses the black hole lensing equations to synthesize an onscreen image displaying the user's surroundings as if they were gravitationally lensed by a black hole within the cameras' field of view. Here, we describe how light rays are lensed by non-rotating (Schwarzschild) and rotating (Kerr) black holes, and we list the equations needed for computing black-hole-lensed images. ### [124] [Multi-Segment Consistency Tests of General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05835)
*Vaishak Prasad*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多参数多段一致性检验（MSCT）方法，通过确保信号外在特性在不同独立段之间的一致性，改进了对广义相对论的检验。该方法应用于GW250114事件，获得了4.61σ显著性的面积增加结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LIGO-VIRGO-KAGRA引力波探测器网络灵敏度提升，每年积累数百个引力波探测事件，迫切需要改进对广义相对论的检验。霍金面积增加定律（Hawking's law of area increase）和旋进-合并-衰荡一致性检验（Inspiral-Merger-Ringdown Consistency Test）已成为重要测试手段。

Method: 提出多参数多段一致性检验（Multi-Segment Consistency Test, MSCT），通过确保信号外在特性在不同独立段之间的一致性来改进现有测试方法。采用加速时域方法，并将改进的面积定律检验作为MSCT的投影。

Result: 将两段版本检验应用于GW250114事件的旋进和衰荡部分，保持部分外在参数在段间共享，获得了4.61σ显著性的面积增加结果。最终状态位于15%最高后验密度置信区间内，即使分析中排除了超过4个合并前周期。

Conclusion: MSCT方法通过引入物理一致性改进了面积定律检验，对观测到的双黑洞合并事件中估计面积的增加提供了更严格的约束，同时捕捉了参数间的协方差关系。

Abstract: As the LIGO-VIRGO-KAGRA Network of gravitational-wave detectors improves in sensitivity, accumulating hundreds of gravitational-wave detections per year, it becomes imperative to improve tests of general relativity in concert. The test of Hawking's law of area increase has gained prominence since GW250114, where black holes in General Relativity were tested with unprecedented precision, using the linear ringdown and pre-merger portions of the signal. A closely related test is the Inspiral-Merger-Ringdown Consistency Test, which assesses the consistency of the high- and low-frequency parts of the signals. In this letter, I present a multi-parameter Multi-Segment Consistency Test (MSCT) that generalizes and improves upon existing tests by ensuring that the extrinsic properties of the signal are consistent across its independent segments and by adopting an accelerated time-domain approach. The improved area law test is then presented as a projection of this MSCT test. These crucial improvements, which bring physical consistency to the area law test, lead to more stringent constraints on the increase in estimated area from observed binary black hole mergers, while also capturing covariances among the parameters.
  Applying the two-segment version of this test to the inspiral and ringdown parts of GW250114, and keeping some of the extrinsic parameters common between the segments, I test the signal to unprecedented accuracy, obtaining $4.61 ^{+0.24} _{-0.11}σ$ significant result for the area increase, even as more than 4 pre-merger cycles of the signal are excluded from the analysis. Also, I infer that the final state lies within the 15\% highest posterior density confidence interval.

*Vaishak Prasad*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种完全时域（fully time-domain）的引力波推断方法，通过结构化线性代数、软件和硬件加速实现大规模似然评估，并开发了tdanalysis工具来处理数据间隙、尖锐边界和多段不连续数据。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了一种自包含、端到端的完全时域（fully time-domain）引力波推断公式，通过利用结构化线性代数、软件和硬件加速实现大规模似然评估。实现了tdanalysis工具，能够处理数据间隙、尖锐边界和多段不连续数据段。

Result: 通过注入测试验证了该方法，并在现代GPU上展示了似然评估的加速效果。tdanalysis实现支持GPU加速，并能够处理实际观测中的复杂数据特征。

Conclusion: 完全时域方法为引力波推断提供了新的计算框架，克服了传统频域分析的局限性，展示了在引力波天文学中的多种应用潜力。

Abstract: Most current compact-binary searches and parameter-estimation pipelines evaluate the Gaussian-noise likelihood approximately using frequency-domain inner products with great success in analyzing gravitational-wave signals. This is historically motivated by (i) the approximate stationarity of detector noise on sufficiently long timescales, allowing a circulant approximation in the domain that diagonalizes the noise covariance in the Fourier basis, and (ii) the efficiency of matched filtering via fast Fourier transforms. However, the advantage of frequency-domain analysis comes with its own limitations. In this article, we develop a self-contained, end-to-end, \emph{fully time-domain} formulation of gravitational-wave inference and present an implementation that makes the likelihood evaluation practical at scale by exploiting structured linear algebra, software, and hardware acceleration. We validate the method using injections and demonstrate speedups for likelihood evaluation and on modern GPUs. We present \emph{tdanalysis}, an accelerated implementation that handles gaps, sharp boundaries, and multiple disjoint segments, and supports GPUs. We demonstrate some of its applications in gravitational wave astronomy.

### [126] [Cyclic cosmology from Cuscuton-Gallileons subjected to Lie point transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06117)
*Biswajit Paul,Pushpendra Kumar Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探索了扩展至伽利略子（Galileons）的Cuscuton模型，通过李点对称性分析发现模型仅有两个自由度，并揭示了原始Cuscuton项系数消失以及势能限制为指数形式等特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任何物理可行理论中的时空变换都应遵循李点对称性（Lie Point symmetry）。本研究旨在探索由de Rham等人提出的扩展至伽利略子的Cuscuton模型，分析其对称性特性。

Method: 通过将模型转换为等价的一阶模型来确定真实自由度；计算对应于李点变换的诺特对称性参数（Noether symmetry parameters）；使用基灵分析（Killing analysis）找出对应于基灵矢量（Killing vectors）和基灵张量（Killing tensors）的荷（charges）；通过动力学分析（dynamical analysis）检验宇宙学意义。

Result: 尽管是高阶导数模型，但仅有两个自由度；诺特对称性参数导致原始Cuscuton项系数消失，并将势能限制为指数形式；在系数a₂消失的条件下，状态方程参数（equation of state parameters）呈现阻尼振荡行为。

Conclusion: 扩展至伽利略子的Cuscuton模型在对称性分析下展现出独特的约束特性，包括原始Cuscuton项系数消失和势能形式受限，这些特性对宇宙学动力学行为产生重要影响。

Abstract: Spacetime transformations in any physically viable theory should follow Lie Point symmetry. In this work, we explore the Cuscuton model extended to Galileons, as introduced by de Rham et al in \cite{Rham2017}. We find the true degrees of freedom by converting the model into an equivalent first order model. Despite being a higher derivative model, it possesses only \textit{two} degrees of freedom. We calculate the Noether symmetry parameters corresponding to Lie point transformations, which lead to the vanishing of the original Cuscuton term's coefficient and restrict the potential to an exponential form. Interestingly, the coefficient corresponding to the original Cuscuton term vanish. Additionally, we also use the Killing analysis to find out the charges corresponding to the Killing vectors and the Killing tensors. The cosmological implications are examined through dynamical analysis, revealing that under the condition where the coefficient $a_2$ vanishes, the equation of state parameters exhibit damped oscillatory behavior .

</details>


### [127] [Energy Extraction and Particle Acceleration in String-Inspired Rotating Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton-Axion Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06273)
*Arindam Kumar Chatterjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子-轴子（EMDA）旋转黑洞中的能量提取和粒子加速，重点关注伸缩子毛发参数b≤0对近视界能量学的影响。发现负b值能显著增强彭罗斯过程的效率，增加可提取的旋转能量，并改变波超辐射和粒子碰撞的动力学特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子-轴子（Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton-Axion, EMDA）旋转黑洞中的能量提取机制，特别关注伸缩子毛发参数b≤0对近视界能量学的影响。通过与克尔（Kerr）黑洞的比较，分析负b值如何改变黑洞的能量提取能力和粒子加速过程。

Method: 采用解析方法推导彭罗斯过程（Penrose process）的最大效率表达式，计算不可约质量M_irr和可提取旋转能量E_rot。通过沃尔德（Wald）和巴丁-普雷斯-特科尔斯基（Bardeen-Press-Teukolsky）界限量化运动学约束，分析波超辐射（wave superradiance）的通量平衡和放大窗口，并研究两粒子碰撞的中心质量能量E_cm。

Result: 负b值显著增强彭罗斯过程的效率，在极端情况下（b=-0.3）达到约91%的理想增益。不可约质量M_irr随b值减小而单调下降，可提取旋转能量E_rot相应增加，表明更大的自旋能量储备。在极端情况下，EMDA黑洞的可提取旋转能量份额约为0.63，而b=0时降至克尔黑洞的约0.29。负b值还放宽了运动学约束，改变了波超辐射的视界角速度Ω_H，并扩大了负视界通量的参数区域。

Conclusion: EMDA黑洞中的伸缩子毛发同时放大了能量提取通道，并重塑了控制高能碰撞的近视界阈值。负b值增强了彭罗斯过程的效率，增加了可提取的旋转能量，并改变了波超辐射和粒子碰撞的动力学特性，为黑洞能量提取机制提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We study energy extraction and particle acceleration in the rotating Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton-Axion (EMDA) black hole, focusing on the impact of dilaton hair $b\le 0$ on near-horizon energetics relative to Kerr. For the Penrose process we derive analytic expressions for the maximum efficiency and show that negative $b$ can strongly enhance the ideal gain in the extremal regime (e.g., reaching $\sim 91\%$ for $b=-0.3$). We then compute the irreducible mass $M_{\rm irr}$ and the corresponding rotationally extractable energy $\mathcal{E}_{\rm rot}\equiv M-M_{\rm irr}$, finding that $M_{\rm irr}$ decreases monotonically as $b$ becomes more negative while $\mathcal{E}_{\rm rot}$ increases, indicating a larger spin-energy reservoir; at extremality the extracted share from rotation is $\mathcal{E}_{\rm rot}/M\simeq 0.63$ for EMDA, reducing to the Kerr value $\simeq 0.29$ at $b=0$. Kinematic constraints relevant to fragment production are quantified via the Wald and Bardeen--Press--Teukolsky bounds, which are progressively relaxed for more negative $b$. For wave superradiance we obtain the flux balance and the amplification window $0<β<kΩ_H$, with $Ω_H$ expressed through $Ξ=r_H^{2}+2br_H+a^{2}$; negative $b$ modifies $Ω_H$ and enlarges the parameter region exhibiting negative horizon flux. Finally, we analyse two-particle collisions and derive $E_{\rm cm}$, showing that the Bañados--Silk--West divergence persists at the horizon when one particle is tuned to the critical angular momentum $L_c=E/Ω_H$, while $E_{\rm cm}$ remains finite for generic angular momenta. Overall, dilaton hair in EMDA simultaneously amplifies energy-extraction channels and reshapes the near-horizon thresholds governing high-energy collisions.

</details>


### [128] [Constraints on BMS Transformations via Energy Conditions and implications on black hole geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06323)
*Nihar Ranjan Ghosh,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在经典能量条件约束下，邦迪-梅茨纳-萨克斯（BMS）群中形式无限维的超平移（supertranslation）扇区是否仍完全物理可容许。研究发现，强能量条件（SEC）和弱能量条件（WEC）在微扰的次领头阶（NLO）即对超平移函数施加非平凡角向限制，而零能量条件（NEC）和主导能量条件（DEC）的首次非平凡约束出现在次次领头阶（NNLO），其中NNLO的NEC简化为纯角向条件，提供了对可容许超平移的最强约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究在经典能量条件（energy conditions）的约束下，邦迪-梅茨纳-萨克斯（Bondi-Metzner-Sachs, BMS）群中形式无限维的超平移（supertranslation）扇区是否仍保持完全的物理可容许性。这涉及到量子引力背景下对称性物理实现的根本问题。

Method: 在微扰框架 $g_{ab}\rightarrow g_{ab}+h_{ab}$ 下，首先通过将曲率张量和里奇标量（Ricci scalar）按微扰 $h_{ab}$ 的幂次展开，发展了一套通用工具包。然后基于Raychaudhuri方程，将强、弱、零和主导能量条件（SEC, WEC, NEC, DEC）重铸为关于 $h_{ab}$ 的显式不等式。为获得具体约束，将形式专门化到史瓦西（Schwarzschild）背景上的标准BMS形式，并用超平移函数 $f(θ,φ)$ 参数化 $h_{ab}=\mathcal{L}_ηg_{ab}$。

Result: 研究发现，强能量条件（SEC）和弱能量条件（WEC）在微扰的次领头阶（next-to-leading order, NLO）即对超平移函数 $f$ 施加非平凡的角向限制。而零能量条件（NEC）和主导能量条件（DEC）在线性阶得以保持，其首次非平凡贡献仅出现在次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading order, NNLO）。值得注意的是，NNLO的NEC简化为一个纯角向条件（与径向坐标无关），这提供了对可容许超平移的最强约束。

Conclusion: 施加能量条件显著减少了物理可容许超平移的空间；虽然原则上允许的扇区仍是无限维的，但在实践中受到了实质性约束。这表明BMS群中形式无限维的超平移对称性在物理能量条件的限制下，其实际可实现的自由度被大幅削减。

Abstract: We investigate whether the formally infinite-dimensional supertranslation sector of the Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) group remains fully physically admissible once classical energy conditions are enforced. Working in a perturbative framework $g_{ab}\rightarrow g_{ab}+h_{ab}$, we first develop a general toolkit by expanding the curvature tensors and the Ricci scalar in powers of the perturbation $h_{ab}$ and recast the strong, weak, null and dominant energy conditions (SEC, WEC, NEC and DEC, respectively) as explicit inequalities on $h_{ab}$ following from the Raychaudhuri equation. The formalism is general, but to obtain concrete constraints we specialize to the standard BMS form on a Schwarzschild background and parametrize $h_{ab}=\mathcal{L}_ηg_{ab} $ by a supertranslation function $f(θ,φ)$. We find that the SEC and WEC impose nontrivial angular restrictions on $f$ already at next-to-leading order (NLO) in the perturbation, whereas the NEC and DEC are preserved at linear order and acquire their first nontrivial contributions only at next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO). Notably, the NNLO NEC reduces to a purely angular condition (independent of the radial coordinate), providing the strongest constraint on admissible supertranslations. Thus, imposing energy conditions substantially reduces the space of physically admissible supertranslations; the allowed sector, although remains infinite-dimensional in principle, is substantially constrained in practice.

</details>


### [129] [On the non-commutativity of geometric observables in different Lorentz frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06337)
*Mehdi Assanioussi,Jerzy Kowalski-Glikman,Ilkka Mäkinen,Ludovic Varrin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨几何可观测量（如长度、面积、体积）在不同观测者视角下的泊松对易性（Poisson commutativity），发现即使在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中，不同观测者测量的几何可观测量通常也不满足泊松对易关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于确定几何可观测量（如长度、面积、体积）在不同观测者视角下是否满足泊松对易关系（Poisson commute）。这有助于理解量子引力背景下是否存在基本尺度（fundamental scale）的相关问题。

Method: 研究方法以刚性杆（rigid rod）为例，计算两个不同测地线（惯性）观测者（geodesic/inertial observers）测量的两个长度之间的泊松括号（Poisson bracket）。其中一个观测者相对于杆静止，另一个相对于杆运动。

Result: 计算结果表明，不同观测者测量的几何可观测量通常不满足泊松对易关系，即使在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）中也是如此。这一非平凡结果（non-trivial result）为量子引力背景下基本尺度（fundamental scale）的存在性问题提供了重要见解。

Conclusion: 研究结论指出，几何可观测量在不同观测者视角下通常不满足泊松对易关系，这一发现对理解量子引力中的基本尺度问题具有重要意义，即使在平坦时空背景下也表现出非平凡的对易性质。

Abstract: Our aim is to establish whether geometric observables, such as length, area or volume of a physical object, viewed by different observers Poisson commute or not. To illustrate this, we compute the Poisson bracket of two lengths associated to a rigid rod and measured by two different geodesic (inertial) observers, one of which is at rest while the other is moving with respect to the rod. Our calculation shows that geometric observables measured by different observers generically do not Poisson commute, not even in Minkowski spacetime. This non-trivial result provides interesting insights into questions related to the presence of a fundamental scale in the context of quantum gravity.

</details>


### [130] [On Schwarzschild black hole singularity formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06451)
*Jorge Ovalle,Roberto Casadio,Alexander Kamenshchik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）能否作为非奇异性引力坍缩的连续终态，发现该过程无法保持连续性，存在时空光滑性破坏的"闵可夫斯基破缺"现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是检验史瓦西黑洞能否从非奇异（non-singular）构型通过引力坍缩（gravitational collapse）连续演化形成，探讨时空平滑演化的可能性。

Method: 采用正则史瓦西度规（regular Schwarzschild metric）的时间依赖扩展，追踪坍缩过程中几何结构的演化，分析度规函数在原点处的行为。

Result: 研究发现度规函数在原点处出现不连续性，导致时空光滑性破坏（"闵可夫斯基破缺"现象），且在史瓦西点源形成前就出现曲率奇点（curvature singularities）和柯西视界（Cauchy horizon）消失。

Conclusion: 时空无法平滑演化至史瓦西几何，史瓦西黑洞的形成涉及时空结构的离散变化，需要非连续（可能量子化）的框架来描述引力奇点（gravitational singularities）的出现或正则化。

Abstract: We examine whether the Schwarzschild black hole can emerge as the continuous end state of gravitational collapse from a non-singular configuration. Employing a time dependent extension of the regular Schwarzschild metric, we track the evolution of the geometry during collapse and find that the process cannot remain continuous. The metric function develops a discontinuity at the origin, marking a breakdown of spacetime smoothness, an effect identified as ``Minkowski breaking.'' Before the Schwarzschild point source can form at $r=0$, curvature singularities appear and the Cauchy horizon disappears. These results strongly suggest that spacetime may not evolve smoothly toward the Schwarzschild geometry. Instead, the formation of a Schwarzschild black hole appears to entail a discrete change in the structure of spacetime, pointing to the need for a noncontinuous, possibly quantized, framework to describe the emergence or regularization of gravitational singularities.

### [131] [Quantum Big Bounce in Wheeler-DeWitt scattering theory: Ekpyrotic and LQC-like transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06481)
*S. Lo Franco,G. Montani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究为充满自相互作用标量场的闭合各向同性宇宙，在与ekpyrotic势相互作用下，提出了量子大反弹（Quantum Big Bounce）的严格表述。研究展示了两种不同的反弹情景：一种类似于圈量子宇宙学（LQC-like）情景，另一种涉及内部时间流向反转的ekpyrotic情景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为闭合各向同性宇宙中的量子大反弹现象提供严格的数学表述框架，特别是探讨在ekpyrotic势相互作用下，量子引力效应如何避免宇宙学奇点（cosmological singularity）。

Method: 采用协变方法处理迷你超空间（minisuperspace），证明了以对数标度因子（logarithmic scale factor）和体积变量（volume variable）为参数的量子等价性。通过类比Wheeler-DeWitt方程与Klein-Gordon方程，并正确定义渐近态（asymptotic states），识别不同的反弹情景。

Result: 识别出两种不同的反弹情景：第一种在固定内部时间箭头方向发生过渡，类似于圈量子宇宙学（LQC-like）情景，但存在高能发散问题；第二种涉及内部时间流向反转，对应于ekpyrotic情景，在一阶微扰下在任何能量尺度都表现良好。WDW理论在特定能量阈值内有效。

Conclusion: 研究表明，Wheeler-DeWitt理论本身可以通过量子力学方式避免宇宙学奇点，但存在能量阈值限制。ekpyrotic情景在微扰一阶下表现良好，而Ashtekar学派的量子大反弹预期可在该框架中加入高能修正后恢复。

Abstract: We present a rigorous formulation of the Quantum Big Bounce for the closed isotropic Universe, filled with a self-interacting scalar field, that emerges from the interaction with an ekpyrotic potential. Working in a covariant approach to the minisuperspace, we demonstrate the quantum equivalence between parametrizations in terms of the logarithmic scale factor and the volume variable. The analogy between the Wheeler-DeWitt equation and the Klein-Gordon equation, alongside a proper definition of asymptotic states, allows the identification of two different bouncing scenarios: one in which the transition occurs over a fixed direction of the internal time arrow, corresponding to a LQC-like scenario, and one involving a reversal of the internal time flow. The high-energy divergence in the former case shows the incompleteness of the WDW theory and the need for regularization. Therefore, the WDW theory is valid up to a given energy threshold. The latter transition, corresponding to an ekpyrotic scenario, is instead well-posed at any energy scale at the first perturbative order. While the Ashtekar school Big Bounce is expected to be recovered when high-energy corrections are included in this scheme, the WDW alone can avoid the cosmological singularity in a quantum mechanical fashion.

### [132] [Hybrid quantum-classical simulations of semiclassical gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06511)
*Carlos Fulgado-Claudio,Daniel González-Cuadra,Jose Beltrán Jiménez,Alejandro Bermudez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种混合量子-经典算法，用于模拟与经典场耦合的相互作用量子场论中的实时动力学，重点关注半经典反作用（semiclassical backreaction）的自洽估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半经典反作用在物理学的多个领域具有重要意义，特别是在宇宙学中，量子物质涨落会影响引力场动力学。为了获得合理的连续极限，必须仔细考虑受控的重整化（controlled renormalization）。

Method: 通过离散化空间和时间，构建了一个迭代协议来模拟受动态经典场影响的量子场的Trotterized动力学。通过一组投影测量（projective measurements）估计特定的量子期望值，为经典场的运动方程提供源项，并数值求解这些方程，在迭代自洽循环中将其反馈到量子模拟中。

Result: 在标量-张量修正引力理论（scalar-tensor theories of modified gravity）的背景下对算法进行了基准测试，该理论展示了变色龙机制（chameleon mechanism）。在数值可处理的范围内，明确展示了算法在考虑连续极限和量子散粒噪声（quantum shot noise）效应时的收敛性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该工作为未来探索其他不可处理区域（non-tractable regimes）的实验铺平了道路，包括量子场的非微扰相互作用（non-perturbative interactions），以及这些相互作用如何改变反作用和引力动力学。

Abstract: We propose a hybrid quantum-classical algorithm for the simulation of real-time dynamics in interacting quantum field theories coupled to classical fields, focusing on the self-consistent estimation of semiclassical backreaction. By discretizing space and time, we construct an iterative protocol that simulates the Trotterized dynamics of the quantum fields subject to the dynamical classical fields. By estimating certain quantum expectation values through a set of projective measurements, we source the equations of motion of the classical fields, and solve them numerically to feed them forward to the quantum simulation in an iterative self-consistent loop. Semiclassical backreaction is relevant in various fields of physics, particularly in cosmology, where quantum matter fluctuations affect the gravitational field dynamics, and a controlled renormalization must be carefully considered to get a sensible continuum limit. We benchmark our algorithm in this context, focusing on scalar-tensor theories of modified gravity exhibiting a chameleon mechanism, such that a light classical scalar field driving cosmic acceleration becomes massive in high-density regions, effectively screening any possible yet unobserved fifth force. By focusing on numerically tractable regimes, we explicitly show the convergence and robustness of our algorithm when considering the continuum limit and the effect of quantum shot noise. Our work paves the way for future experiments exploring other non-tractable regimes, including non-perturbative interactions of the quantum fields and how these can change backreaction and the gravitational dynamics.

</details>

### [133] [Gurau's spectral density is not a probability measure for individual real symmetric tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05879)
*Maximilian Jerdee,Dmitriy Kunisky,Cristopher Moore*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: Gurau提出的高阶张量解析迹（resolvent trace）推广在随机张量系综中可得到类似Wigner半圆律和Marchenko-Pastur分布的矩序列，但对于某些确定性张量，该系数不构成任何概率测度的矩序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨Gurau提出的高阶张量解析迹（resolvent trace）推广的性质，特别是其系数在随机张量系综中表现出的类似随机矩阵理论中经典分布的特征，以及该概念在确定性张量上的适用性问题。

Method: 通过构造特定的确定性张量，分析Gurau解析迹的级数展开系数在这些张量上的表现，并与随机张量系综中的极限期望行为进行对比。

Result: 研究发现，虽然对于适当的大随机张量，Gurau解析迹系数的极限期望给出了类似Wigner半圆律（Wigner semicircle）和Marchenko-Pastur分布的矩序列，但对于某些确定性张量，相同系数不构成任何概率测度的矩序列。

Conclusion: Gurau解析迹所关联的"谱密度"（spectral density）概念在随机张量系综中具有平均意义，但对于所有个体张量而言，该概念无法点态定义（除非可能作为带符号测度）。

Abstract: Gurau (2020) proposed a generalization of the trace of the matrix resolvent to tensors of higher order, and recent work has explored analogs of the Wigner semicircle and Marchenko-Pastur distributions from random matrix theory as well as aspects of free probability theory from this perspective. In particular, when evaluated with appropriate large random tensors, the limiting expectations of the coefficients of a series expansion of Gurau's resolvent trace give the moment sequences of probability measures analogous to the above distributions. We construct, on the other hand, individual deterministic tensors such that the same coefficients evaluated on those tensors do not give the moment sequence of any probability measure. Thus, the "spectral density" associated to Gurau's resolvent trace, while in a sense defined on average for certain random tensor ensembles, is not defined pointwise (unless perhaps as a signed measure) for all individual tensors.

</details>


### [134] [Massive holomorphicity of near-critical dimers and sine-Gordon model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06498)
*Nathanaël Berestycki,Scott Mason,Lucas Rey*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在近临界二聚体模型中，中心化高度函数在网格尺寸趋于零时收敛于一个极限场，该场与电磁倾斜的正弦-戈登模型一致，解决了该领域的一个长期问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究近临界二聚体模型（near-critical dimer model）在等径向叠加（isoradial superpositions）和Temperleyan边界条件下的行为，旨在解决该领域的一个长期未决问题。

Method: 发展了离散质量全纯函数（discrete massive holomorphic functions）的概念和相关工具，特别是找到了逆Kasteleyn矩阵满足的离散形式的质量柯西-黎曼方程（massive Cauchy-Riemann equations）。

Result: 证明了中心化高度函数（centered height function）在网格尺寸趋于零时收敛于一个极限场，该场与电磁倾斜的正弦-戈登模型（electromagnetically tilted sine-Gordon model）一致，其导数相关性由格拉斯曼变量（Grassmann variables）描述。

Conclusion: 该研究解决了该领域的一个长期问题，关键创新在于允许质量不仅非常数，还可以是复数值（complex-valued），这相比先前研究是一个重要的新颖之处。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the near-critical dimer model in the setup of isoradial superpositions with Temperleyan boundary conditions. We show that the centered height function converges as the mesh size tends to zero to a limiting field which agrees with the (electromagnetically tilted) sine-Gordon model, whose derivative correlations are described by Grassmann variables (or equivalently determinants involving a massive Dirac operator). This answers a longstanding question in the field. A crucial part of the work is to develop a notion of discrete massive holomorphic functions and the tools to study such functions, in particular finding an exact discrete form of the massive Cauchy--Riemann equations, which is satisfied by the inverse Kasteleyn matrix. In comparison with previous studies, a key novelty of this part of our work is that the mass is not only allowed to be non-constant but can be complex-valued.

</details>


### [135] [A class of d-dimensional directed polymers in a Gaussian environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06574)
*Le Chen,Cheng Ouyang,Samy Tindel,Panqiu Xia*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文在Dalang条件下研究了一类连续有向聚合物（continuous directed polymers），使用Itô重整化随机热方程表示，建立了配分函数的结构性质，证明了路径的布朗型行为，获得了奇异性与等价性的测度理论二分法，并在高维高温区证明了扩散行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将Alberts-Khanin-Quastel框架从1+1维白噪声（white-noise）设置扩展到具有一般空间协方差的高维高斯环境（Gaussian environments）。研究在Dalang条件下由高斯环境驱动的连续有向聚合物（continuous directed polymers）的广泛类别。

Method: 采用Itô重整化随机热方程表示（Itô-renormalized stochastic-heat-equation representation）来分析连续有向聚合物。该方法允许建立配分函数（partition function）的结构性质，并在有限时间区间上证明路径的布朗型行为。

Result: 证明了配分函数的正定性、平稳性、标度性、齐次性和Chapman-Kolmogorov关系。在有限时间区间上，获得了Hölder连续性和二次变差的识别。建立了尖锐的测度理论二分法：淬火聚合物测度（quenched polymer measure）相对于维纳测度（Wiener measure）是奇异的当且仅当$\widehat f(\mathbb{R}^d)=\infty$（等价于噪声是非迹类（non-trace-class）的），否则是等价的。在$d\ge 3$维的高温区（high-temperature regime），证明了大时间下的扩散行为（diffusive behavior）。

Conclusion: 本文成功地将Alberts-Khanin-Quastel框架从1+1维白噪声设置推广到具有一般空间协方差的高维高斯环境。研究结果提供了连续有向聚合物在Dalang条件下的全面理论分析，包括结构性质、路径行为和测度理论特征。

Abstract: We introduce and analyze a broad class of continuous directed polymers in $\mathbb{R}^d$ driven by Gaussian environments that are white in time and spatially correlated, under Dalang's condition. Using an Itô-renormalized stochastic-heat-equation representation, we establish structural properties of the partition function, including positivity, stationarity, scaling, homogeneity, and a Chapman--Kolmogorov relation. On finite time intervals, we prove Brownian-type pathwise behavior, namely Hölder continuity and identification of the quadratic variation. We then obtain a sharp measure-theoretic dichotomy: the quenched polymer measure is singular with respect to Wiener measure if and only if $\widehat f(\mathbb{R}^d)=\infty$ (equivalently, the noise is non-trace-class), and it is equivalent otherwise. Finally, in dimension $d\ge 3$, we prove diffusive behavior at large times in the high-temperature regime. This extends the Alberts--Khanin--Quastel framework from the $1+1$ white-noise setting to higher-dimensional Gaussian environments with general spatial covariance.

### [136] [One-sided large deviations for the ground-state energy of spin glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06368)
*Hong-Bin Chen,Alice Guionnet,Justin Ko,Bertrand Lacroix-A-Chez-Toine,Jean-Christophe Mourrat*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在理解自旋玻璃系统中最大能量偏离其典型值的大偏差行为。研究动机源于对自旋玻璃最大能量统计特性的深入分析，特别是速率函数的数学结构及其与物理参数的关系。

Method: 方法基于帕里西型公式（Parisi-type formula）计算配分函数（partition function）的分数矩（fractional moments），进而推导最大能量的拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）极限。通过凸对偶论证（convex-duality arguments），将拉普拉斯变换重写为鞅（martingales）上的上确界，从而获得具有显式速率函数的大偏差原理。

Result: 研究确定了最大能量大偏差的显式速率函数，并证明该速率函数在其最小值附近渐近二次（asymptotically quadratic）当且仅当存在外加磁场。这一等价关系揭示了磁场对自旋玻璃最大能量统计特性的关键影响。

Conclusion: 论文建立了自旋玻璃最大能量大偏差的完整数学框架，揭示了速率函数的渐近二次性质与外加磁场的等价关系。这一结果为理解自旋玻璃系统的极端能量统计特性提供了新的理论工具和物理洞察。

Abstract: We describe the large deviations above its typical value of the maximal energy of a spin glass with +/-1 spins. Thanks to the relatively explicit description of the rate function we identify, we then show that the latter is asymptotically quadratic near its minimum if and only if an external magnetic field is present. The proof starts from a Parisi-type formula for the fractional moments of the partition function, which we then leverage to obtain the limit of the Laplace transform of the maximum energy. Using convex-duality arguments, we then rewrite this Laplace transform as a supremum over martingales, and thereby deduce the large-deviation principle with explicit rate function.

Conclusion: 李对称方法有效分析了非线性热扩散方程的对称性结构，为特定物理情形下的相似解构造提供了系统框架，揭示了系数函数关系对解性质的影响。

Abstract: We investigate the nonlinear heat-diffusion equation \( C(u)\,\frac{\partial u}{\partial t}
  = \frac{\partial}{\partial x}\!\left( K(u)\,\frac{\partial u}{\partial x} \right) \), where \( C(u) \) and \( K(u) \) are coefficients that depend on \( u \). By applying the classical Lie symmetry method, we determine the admitted Lie point symmetries and compute the corresponding infinitesimal generators according to the functional relationship between \( C(u) \) and \( K(u) \). The admitted symmetries are used to reduce the partial differential equation to ordinary differential equations and to construct invariant solutions. Particular cases of physical interest are analyzed in detail, including Storm-type materials and power-law dependence of \( C(u) \) and \( K(u) \) on \( u \). For these cases, similarity solutions are obtained.

Method: 采用系统互感（mutual inductance）研究，测量Nd₁₋ₓSrₓNiO₂在掺杂依赖的超导圆顶（superconducting dome）范围内的超流密度（superfluid density）。

Abstract: Nickelate superconductors provide a valuable new platform for the study of unconventional superconductivity that is complementary to the cuprates. One of the central puzzles about high-temperature superconductors is what factors determine the scale of their superconducting transition temperature ($T_\mathrm{c}$). To address this question for infinite-layer nickelates, we present a systematic mutual inductance study of the superfluid density across the doping-dependent superconducting dome of $\mathrm{Nd}_{1-x}\mathrm{Sr}_x\mathrm{NiO}_2$. We observe a weak superfluid stiffness that exhibits an approximately square-root correlation with $T_\mathrm{c}$. We also find a strong interplay between Nd magnetism and the superconducting phase, manifested as a substantial low-temperature suppression of superfluid density. These observations highlight the importance of superconducting phase fluctuations in limiting $T_\mathrm{c}$ and unexpectedly strong coupling between the Nd 4$f$ moments and the superfluid.

Conclusion: 分析揭示了费米能级电子态轨道特征的强烈不均匀性，这可能与观测到的多能隙超导性（multigap superconductivity）有关。BeAu的复杂拓扑结构为研究拓扑超导性提供了丰富平台。

As a member of the B20 crystal family (space group $P2_13$), its band structure hosts multifold fermions at high-symmetry points, unpaired Weyl points and even nodal surfaces. This renders BeAu an appealing system to investigate the interplay between superconductivity and topology. Here we present a comprehensive first-principles analysis of BeAu's electronic structure focusing on its Fermi surface's topology and the implications for superconductivity. Together with the presence of four- and six-fold fermions at high-symmetry points, we identify several additional isolated Weyl points near the Fermi level. We also determine the associated topological edge states -- the surface Fermi arcs. Computing the Chern number associated to different Fermi surface sheets, we show that BeAu harbors a $ν= 4$ topological superconducting phase in the presence of $s$-wave pairing of alternating sign ($s_\pm$ pairing). Notably, we also identify a Fermi surface with a Chern number of +6; the highest value reported to date. Finally, our analysis reveals strong inhomogeneity in the orbital character of electronic states at the Fermi level, suggesting a link to the observed multigap superconductivity.
