### [141] [Competition between Charge Density Wave and Superconductivity in a Janus MXene Mo2NF2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06284)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Udomsilp Pinsook,Graeme J Ackland*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算揭示了Janus MXene材料Mo2NF2中电荷密度波（CDW）与超导的竞争关系，发现压缩双轴应变可抑制CDW并增强超导转变温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（CDW）序与超导性在低维材料中常存在竞争关系，但它们在Janus MXenes中的相互作用尚未得到充分探索。本研究旨在系统探究Mo2NF2的结构、振动和电子性质，以阐明其CDW与超导的竞争机制。

Method: 采用全面的第一性原理（first-principles）计算，包括结构、振动和电子性质分析。通过声子（phonon）计算识别不稳定的软声子模式，分析声子线宽和裸电子磁化率的实部与虚部，并进行结构弛豫确定CDW相。

Result: 声子计算显示高对称结构中M点存在不稳定的软声子模式，表明CDW不稳定性。分析证实CDW并非由简单的费米面嵌套（Fermi-surface nesting）驱动，而是源于强烈的动量依赖电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）。结构弛豫得到具有Mo、N、F亚晶格键长调制的公度CDW相。

Conclusion: Mo2NF2是一个应变可调平台，其中超导性在竞争CDW相被抑制后出现。压缩双轴应变超过-3%可完全抑制CDW不稳定性，使高对称相的电子-声子耦合增强，超导转变温度（Tc）从约1K提升至约4K，突显了晶格控制在Janus MXenes中的关键作用。

Abstract: Charge-density-wave (CDW) order and superconductivity often compete in low-dimensional materials, yet their interplay in Janus MXenes remains largely unexplored. Here, we present a comprehensive first-principles investigation of the structural, vibrational, and electronic properties of Mo2NF2. Phonon calculations reveal an unstable soft phonon mode at the M point in the high-symmetry structure, signaling a CDW instability. Analysis of phonon linewidths and the real and imaginary parts of the bare electronic susceptibility demonstrates that the CDW is not driven by simple Fermi-surface nesting but instead originates from strong momentum-dependent electron-phonon coupling. Structural relaxation yields a commensurate CDW phase characterized by bond-length modulations involving the Mo, N, and F sublattices. We further show that charge doping alone is insufficient to stabilize the soft phonon, whereas compressive biaxial strain exceeding -3 percent completely suppresses the CDW instability. Electron-phonon coupling calculations indicate that the CDW phase exhibits a reduced coupling constant lambda = 0.40 and logarithmic phonon frequency omega_log = 219 K, leading to a low superconducting transition temperature Tc about 1 K. In contrast, the strain-stabilized high-symmetry phase shows enhanced coupling (lambda = 0.53, omega_log = 272 K) and a higher Tc about 4 K. Our results establish Mo2NF2 as a strain-tunable platform where superconductivity emerges upon suppression of a competing CDW phase, highlighting the crucial role of lattice control in Janus MXenes.

### [142] [Intrinsic decay rates and steady states of driven Josephson junction chains cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06371)
*Lucia Vigliotti,Andrew P. Higginbotham,Maksym Serbyn*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了约瑟夫森结链（Josephson junction chain）作为多模腔体时，多模相互作用对系统内禀相干性的影响。通过分析平衡态和非平衡态下的模式散射过程，揭示了不同驱动条件下线宽（linewidth）和分布函数的变化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约瑟夫森结链（Josephson junction chain）结合了超导相干性和微波电路可控性，为电路量子电动力学（circuit quantum electrodynamics）提供了强大平台。研究其多模相互作用如何影响内禀相干性（表现为额外线宽）具有重要意义。

Method: 研究基于长约瑟夫森结链实现具有非线性色散和多模相互作用的多模腔体。通过微波光谱学（microwave spectroscopy）在平衡态和非平衡驱动条件下探测个体模式，重点分析二对二模式散射（two-into-two mode scattering）作为主要弛豫过程。

Result: 在平衡条件下，弛豫速率（decay rate）由非共振过程主导。弱驱动特定模式偏离平衡态会增强共振散射，导致分布函数和线宽出现可观测特征。在强非平衡条件下，系统会过渡到性质不同的非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady state）。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森结链的多模相互作用显著影响系统相干性，不同驱动条件会导致不同的散射机制主导弛豫过程。平衡态下非共振过程占主导，而非平衡驱动可增强共振散射，最终在强驱动下系统进入新的非平衡稳态。

Abstract: Josephson junction (JJ) chains combine the coherence of superconductivity with the controllability of microwave-frequency circuits, making them a powerful platform for circuit quantum electrodynamics. In this work we consider a long JJ chain that effectively realizes a multi-mode cavity with nonlinear dispersion and additional multi-mode interactions. Individual modes appearing due to the finite size of the chain can be experimentally probed via microwave spectroscopy, both in equilibrium and in driven far-from-equilibrium settings. We study the role of multi-mode interactions in degrading internal coherence -- observable as excess linewidth -- in both equilibrium and driven regimes. Focusing on two-into-two mode scattering as the leading relaxation process, we classify the relevant scattering processes and derive their expected temperature- and frequency-scaling under equilibrium conditions. For experimentally relevant parameters, we show that the equilibrium decay rate is dominated by non-resonant processes, however weakly driving a particular set of modes out of equilibrium enhances resonant scattering, leading to observable signatures in the distribution function and linewidth. Finally, in the strong non-equilibrium regime we report a crossover to a qualitatively different non-equilibrium steady state.

### [143] [Exotic Pressure-Driven Band Gap Widening in Carbon Chain-Filled KFI Zeolite and Its Pathway to High-Pressure Semiconducting Electronics and High-Temperature Superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06412)
*C. T. Wat,K. C. Lam,W. Y. Chan,C. P. Chau,S. P. Ng,W. K. Loh,L. Y. F. Lam,X. Hu,C. H. Wong*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究发现在KFI沸石中，碳链在高压下表现出异常行为：不仅观察到从聚炔（半导体）到累积烯（金属）的转变，还在更高压力下出现聚炔的重新进入现象，且其带隙随压力增加而增大。同时，成功合成了超过5000个原子的长累积烯链，其超导转变温度达到约62K，超过了块体铁基超导体的最高报告值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体器件在高压下工作面临持续挑战，因为能带理论预测材料在压缩下会转变为更金属态。此外，长累积烯链的合成一直是实现高温有机超导性的长期难题。

Method: 研究采用KFI沸石作为基底，在其中合成碳链。通过对比约100种其他沸石（通常限制在约10个原子）与KFI沸石（可形成超过5000个原子的碳链）的表现，探索了非常规电荷密度波与显著扭转之间的相互作用。

Result: 在中等压力下观察到从聚炔（polyyne，半导体）到累积烯（cumulene，金属）的转变，但在高压下出现聚炔的重新进入现象，且其带隙随压力增加而增大。累积烯@KFI系统表现出约62K的超导转变温度，超过了块体铁基超导体的最高报告值。

Conclusion: 碳结构与超导性之间的相互作用不仅推进了对电荷密度波的理解，还预示着新型应用研究的新时代。KFI沸石为合成超长碳链提供了关键条件，突破了传统沸石的限制。

Abstract: Semiconducting devices face persistent challenges in operating at high pressure, as the band theory predicts that materials transition to a more metallic state under compression. However, our findings with carbon chains in KFI substrates reveal a conditional deviation from this norm. We not only witness the transition from polyyne (semiconductor) to cumulene (metal) at medium pressure, but we also observe an unexpected re-entrance of the polyyne at high pressures, where the band gap in the polyyne increases with pressure. In addition, the synthesis of long cumulene chains has posed a longstanding challenge in the quest for high-temperature organic superconductivity. We have identified critical conditions for synthesizing extended cumulene chains within zeolite frameworks, highlighting the interplay between unconventional charge density waves and significant torsions. The KFI zeolite facilitates the formation of carbon chains exceeding 5,000 atoms, in stark contrast to around 100 other zeolites that are limited to ~10 atoms. The cumulene@KFI system demonstrates a superconducting transition temperature reaching ~62 K, surpassing the highest reported values for bulk iron-based superconductors. This interplay between carbon structures and superconductivity not only advances our understanding of charge density waves but also heralds a new era in the study of novel applications

</details>


### [144] [Unifying description of competing chiral and nematic superconducting states in twisted bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06550)
*Lucas Baldo,Patric Holmvall,Annica M. Black-Schaffer*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了魔角双层石墨烯（TBG）中电子驱动和声子驱动配对的对应关系，通过将原子尺度电子驱动配对模型映射到有效的谷间、陈数内描述，分析了向列相和手性超导态的竞争机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示魔角双层石墨烯中电子驱动和声子驱动超导配对的统一对应关系，澄清手性和向列相超导态竞争的微观起源。

Method: 通过将原子尺度电子驱动配对模型映射到有效的谷间、陈数内（inter-valley, intra-Chern）描述框架，该框架最初为声子介导超导性提出，从而在统一的陈数内配对框架下分析向列相和手性超导态的竞争。

Result: 研究发现手性态对应极端陈数极化极限，在超导能隙内存在未配对平带，通常使其相对于向列相态处于不利地位。向列序在每个动量点局部优选，但由于旋转对称性破缺，布里渊区内最优向列方向不相容，这种动量空间挫败在大填充或弱相互作用下使手性基态成为可能。

Conclusion: 该研究为魔角双层石墨烯超导性提供了统一理解，揭示了电子和声子介导配对自然协作的机制，并阐明了手性和向列相超导态竞争的微观起源。

Abstract: We reveal a striking correspondence between electron- and phonon-driven pairing in twisted bilayer graphene (TBG) by mapping an atomistic electronically driven pairing model onto an effective inter-valley, intra-Chern description, originally proposed for phonon-mediated superconductivity. Within the unified framework of intra-Chern pairing, we analyze the competition between nematic and chiral superconducting states. The latter corresponds to the extreme Chern-polarized limit and thus hosts unpaired flat bands within the superconducting gap, which generally disfavors it relative to the nematic states. Crucially, nematic order is locally preferred at each momenta, but the optimal nematic directions are incompatible across the Brillouin zone due to the broken rotation symmetry. This momentum-space frustration enables a chiral ground state at large fillings or weak interactions. Our results thereby both provide a unified understanding of superconductivity in TBG, with a natural cooperation of electron- and phonon-mediated pairing, and clarify the microscopic origin of the competition between the chiral and nematic superconducting states.

</details>

R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次通过多通道联合分析确定奇特粲偶素态T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)的自旋宇称（J^P=1^+）并提取其极点位置和相对分支比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究奇特粲偶素态T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)的性质，特别是其自旋宇称量子数，这对于理解其内部结构和分类至关重要。

Method: 采用电子-正电子湮灭过程e^+e^-→π^+T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^- + c.c.，基于BESIII探测器在√s=4.395和4.416 GeV采集的数据，对三个衰变通道进行部分波分析（partial wave analysis）。

Result: 首次确定T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^-的自旋宇称为J^P=1^+，显著性达11.7σ；在复能量平面的黎曼面上提取极点位置；获得相对分支比：π^-J/ψ通道为(3.6±0.6±1.6)×10^{-3}，π^-h_c通道为(8.9±1.3±2.3)×10^{-2}。

Conclusion: 通过多通道联合分析成功确定了T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)的自旋宇称量子数，并提供了其衰变特性的精确测量，为理解这一奇特强子态的性质提供了关键信息。

Abstract: This paper reports the first multi-channel joint analysis to identify the properties of the exotic charmonium-like state $T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)$ via the electron-positron annihilation process $e^{+}e^{-}\toπ^{+}T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}+c.c$. A partial wave analysis is performed simultaneously in three decay channels $T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}\to {D}^{*0}D^{*-}$, $π^{-}J/ψ$, and $π^{-}h_{c}$, based on data samples taken at $\sqrt{s}=4.395$ and $4.416\,\mathrm{GeV}$ with an integrated luminosity of $1598.9\,\mathrm{pb}^{-1}$ collected with the BESIII detector operating on the BEPCII collider. For the first time, the spin-parity of the $T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}$ is determined to be $J^{P}=1^{+}$ with a significance $11.7σ$. Pole positions are extracted on the Riemann sheets with three branch points in the complex energy plane. Furthermore, the relative branching fractions are obtained as $\mathcal{B}[T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}\toπ^{-}J/ψ]/\mathcal{B}[T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}\to{D}^{*0}D^{*-}]=(3.6\pm0.6\pm1.6)\times10^{-3}$ and $\mathcal{B}[T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}\toπ^{-}h_{c}]/\mathcal{B}[T_{c\bar{c}}(4020)^{-}\to{D}^{*0}D^{*-}]=(8.9\pm1.3\pm2.3)\times10^{-2}$, where the first uncertainties are statistical, and the second are systematic.

</details>


### [146] [Agentic AI -- Physicist Collaboration in Experimental Particle Physics: A Proof-of-Concept Measurement with LEP Open Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05735)
*Anthony Badea,Yi Chen,Yen-Jie Lee*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文通过AI代理（OpenAI Codex和Anthropic Claude）在物理学家指导下，利用存档的ALEPH数据，对√s=91.2 GeV的e⁺e⁻碰撞中的推力分布进行了AI代理测量，获得完全校正的谱线，展示了AI辅助实验测量与理论计算的理论-实验循环前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索AI代理在基础物理发现中的应用，通过开发理论-实验循环（theory-experiment loop），使AI代理能够协助实验测量和理论计算，并通过比较结果综合见解，从而加速基础物理的发现周期。

Method: 采用AI代理（OpenAI Codex和Anthropic Claude）在专家物理学家指导下，利用存档的ALEPH数据，通过迭代贝叶斯展开（Iterative Bayesian Unfolding）和基于蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）的校正方法，对e⁺e⁻碰撞中的推力分布（thrust distribution）进行测量。

Result: 获得了完全校正的推力分布谱线（fully corrected spectrum），展示了利用开放LEP数据和先进理论框架进行精确物理测量的可行性，为开发科学应用的高级AI系统提供了理想的测试平台。

Conclusion: 这项工作代表了向理论-实验循环迈出的一步，其中AI代理协助实验测量和理论计算，并通过比较结果综合见解，从而加速基础物理的发现周期。研究表明，精确物理测量为开发科学应用的高级AI系统提供了理想的测试环境。

Abstract: We present an AI agentic measurement of the thrust distribution in $e^{+}e^{-}$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=91.2$~GeV using archived ALEPH data. The analysis and all note writing is carried out entirely by AI agents (OpenAI Codex and Anthropic Claude) under expert physicist direction. A fully corrected spectrum is obtained via Iterative Bayesian Unfolding and Monte Carlo based corrections. This work represents a step toward a theory-experiment loop in which AI agents assist with experimental measurements and theoretical calculations, and synthesize insights by comparing the results, thereby accelerating the cycle that drives discovery in fundamental physics. Our work suggests that precision physics, leveraging the open LEP data and advanced theoretical landscape, provides an ideal testing ground for developing advanced AI systems for scientific applications.

</details>

### [148] [Transformer-Based Pulse Shape Discrimination in HPGe Detectors with Masked Autoencoder Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06192)

Method: 基于Majorana Demonstrator AI/ML数据发布，训练Transformer模型以复现合作方提供的四种标准PSD截断的接受/拒绝标签，并进行校准能量回归。比较了三种方法：从头开始的监督训练、掩码自编码器（MAE）自监督预训练后微调，以及基于特征的梯度提升决策树（GBDT）基线模型。

Conclusion: 这些结果支持后续研究在不同探测器和操作条件下的鲁棒性，以及在QBB（双贝塔衰变能量）附近的性能表现。研究表明Transformer模型在脉冲形状鉴别任务中具有优势，自监督预训练能有效降低标注数据需求。

Abstract: Pulse-shape discrimination (PSD) in high-purity germanium (HPGe) detectors is central to rare-event searches such as neutrinoless double-beta decay (0vBB), yet conventional approaches compress each waveform into a small set of summary parameters, potentially discarding information in the full time series that is relevant for classification. We benchmark transformer-based models that operate directly on digitised waveforms using the Majorana Demonstrator AI/ML data release. Models are trained to reproduce the collaboration-provided accept/reject labels for four standard PSD cuts and to regress calibrated energy. We compare supervised training from scratch, masked autoencoder (MAE) self-supervised pre-training followed by fine-tuning, and a feature-based gradient-boosted decision tree (GBDT) baseline. Transformers outperform GBDT across all PSD targets, with the largest gains on the most challenging labels and on the combined PSD-pass definition. MAE pre-training improves sample efficiency, reducing labelled-data requirements by factors of 2-4 in low-label regimes. For energy regression, both transformer variants show a small common underestimation on the test split, while fine-tuning modestly narrows the residual distribution. *Jaret Heise*

Main category: hep-ex

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 桑福德地下研究设施（Sanford Underground Research Facility, SURF）自2007年开始运营，致力于推动引人注目的多学科科学研究。该设施旨在为物理实验提供超低本底环境和独特的地下条件。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，系统讨论SURF的历史沿革、设施特征和当前状态。同时介绍了该设施提供的超低本底环境、低本底分析能力以及现场生产的电铸铜（electroformed copper）。

Result: SURF是全球最深的地下实验室之一，拥有最大的科学研究占地面积，在4850英尺深度设有物理园区，容纳了LUX-ZEPLIN、MAJORANA DEMONSTRATOR和CASPAR等实验。该设施还设有长基线中微子设施（Long-Baseline Neutrino Facility, LBNF），将主办国际深地下中微子实验（Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment, DUNE）。

Conclusion: 本文全面介绍了SURF的设施概况、当前科学项目以及未来的发展规划和演进方向，强调了该设施在多学科前沿研究中的重要地位和独特优势。

Abstract: The Sanford Underground Research Facility (SURF) began operation in 2007 as a facility dedicated to advancing compelling multidisciplinary scientific research. SURF is one of the deepest laboratory sites and offers the largest footprint in the world for scientific pursuits, including physics campuses on the 4850-foot level where the LUX-ZEPLIN, MAJORANA DEMONSTRATOR, and CASPAR experiments are located. SURF is also home to the Long-Baseline Neutrino Facility (LBNF) that will host the international Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment (DUNE). SURF provides ultra-low background environments, low-background assay capabilities, and electroformed copper is produced at the facility. In this review, we discuss the history, features and status of the facility, as well as the current scientific program and future evolution and plans.

### [151] [Modern jet flavour tagging in hadronic Z decays with archived ALEPH data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06524)
*Matteo M. Defranchis,Jacopo Fanini,Apranik Fatehi,Gerardo Ganis,Taj Gillin,Loukas Gouskos,Luka Lambrecht,Michele Selvaggi,Birgit Stapf*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文对LEP实验ALEPH合作组的存档数据进行了重新分析，应用现代喷注味道标记技术改进了Z玻色子不同强子衰变道的分离，相比传统算法将b和c夸克喷注的误识别率降低了一个数量级，并首次在LEP数据中实现了奇异夸克喷注标记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在改进LEP实验ALEPH合作组存档数据的分析，通过应用现代喷注味道标记（jet flavour tagging）技术来提升Z玻色子不同强子衰变道的分离能力，为电弱精密观测量（electroweak precision observables）的改进测量铺平道路。

Method: 研究采用现代喷注味道标记技术，利用寿命信息、粒子识别和次级顶点信息，以及基于深度学习方法的现代分类器。同时使用标记与探测法（tag-and-probe method）在数据中对标记器进行校准。

Result: 相比最新ALEPH结果中使用的传统算法，在相同识别效率下，b和c夸克喷注的误识别率（misidentification rate）提高了最多一个数量级。首次在LEP数据中实现了奇异夸克喷注标记，能够选择富集Z→s\bar{s}的事件样本。所有夸克味道的数据与模拟结果都取得了良好的一致性。

Conclusion: 这些结果为利用LEP存档数据改进电弱精密观测量测量铺平了道路，并为未来正负电子对撞机的探测器和算法开发提供了指导。

Abstract: We present a reanalysis of archived data from the ALEPH experiment at LEP in the $\mathrm{Z \to q\bar{q}}$ final state. We apply modern jet flavour tagging techniques to improve the separation between the different hadronic decay channels of the Z boson, achieving up to one order of magnitude improvement in misidentification rate for b- and c-quark jets compared to the legacy algorithms used for the most recent ALEPH results, for the same identification efficiency. We also present the first implementation of strange quark jet tagging with LEP data, which allows for the selection of a $\mathrm{Z \to s\bar{s}}$ enriched event sample. These improvements in the flavour tagging performance are achieved by leveraging the lifetime, particle identification, and secondary vertex information, as well as modern classifiers based on a deep learning approach. We also demonstrate the calibration of the tagger in data using a tag-and-probe method, obtaining good data to simulation agreement for all quark flavours. These results pave the way for improved measurements of electroweak precision observables with LEP archived data, and can serve as a guidance for the development of detectors and algorithms for future electron-positron colliders.

### [152] [Spectral study of the pseudogap in unitary Fermi gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06102)
*Chuping Li,Lin Sun,Kaichao Zhang,Junru Wu,Yuxuan Wu,Dingli Yuan,Pengyi Chen,Qijin Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过超越先前赝能隙近似的迭代自能处理方法，对幺正费米气体的光谱数据进行了定量解释，为赝能隙的配对起源机制提供了微观理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上已确认幺正费米气体（unitary Fermi gases）中存在赝能隙（pseudogap），这为费米超流体中赝能隙的配对起源机制提供了有力支持。本研究旨在通过光谱分析定量理解实验数据，并提取光谱中的赝能隙信息。

Method: 采用超越先前赝能隙近似的迭代处理方法，基于包含粒子-粒子和粒子-空穴T矩阵（T matrices）的配对涨落理论（pairing fluctuation theory），对费米子自能（self energy）和谱函数（spectral function）进行自洽反馈计算。

Result: 研究结果不仅为实验数据提供了微观解释，而且通过将理论与实验测量的动量分辨射频或微波光谱（momentum-resolved rf or microwave spectra）进行定量比较，进一步强化了对配对诱导赝能隙物理和费米超流体配对涨落理论的支持。

Conclusion: 该研究通过改进的理论框架成功解释了幺正费米气体的光谱数据，为赝能隙的配对起源机制和费米超流体的配对涨落理论提供了坚实的理论和实验证据支持。

Abstract: The existence of a pseudogap in unitary Fermi gases has recently been established and measured experimentally [Li et al., Nature 626, 288 (2024)]. This lends strong support for the pairing origin as the mechanism of the pseudogap in Fermi superfluids. Here we present a spectral study of unitary Fermi gases, and show how the data can be understood quantitatively, when compared with theoretically calculated momentum-resolved rf or microwave spectra, and the pseudogap extracted from the spectra. We use an iterative treatment of the fermion self energy and hence the spectral function, beyond previous pseudogap approximation, based on a pairing fluctuation theory that incorporates both particle-particle and particle-hole T matrices, with self-consistent self energy feedback. Our results not only provide a microscopic explanation of the experimental data but also strengthen the support for both the pairing-induced pseudogap physics and the pairing fluctuation theory of Fermi superfluidity.

### [153] [Environmental Measurements in the Sedrun Access Shaft to the Gotthard Base Tunnel -- a Promising Site for a Long-Baseline Atom Interferometer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05558)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究在瑞士格劳宾登州塞德伦地区戈特哈德基线铁路隧道入口处进行了探索性环境测量活动，评估了地面运动活动和背景电磁场质量。

Abstract: Atom interferometer (AI) experiments offer interesting prospects for searches for the interactions of ultralight bosonic dark matter with Standard Model particles as well as detection of gravitational waves in a frequency band inaccessible to experiments that are operating or under construction. Ideal locations for the next generation of such experiments are provided by long vertical shafts, such as that providing access to the Gotthard base railway tunnel from the Sedrun locality in the Canton Grisons of Switzerland. We present the results of an exploratory environmental measurement campaign at this location to evaluate the ground motion activity and the background electromagnetic field quality. We find that the backgrounds due to both ground motion and electromagnetic fields, including those due to passing trains, are low enough for successful operation of a 800-m AI experiment.

### [154] [Long-range mid-infrared energy transfer mediated by hyperbolic phonon polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06184)
*Gonzalo Álvarez-Pérez,Simone De Liberato,Huatian Hu*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个理论框架，用于描述单层和扭曲双层双曲材料中的长程能量转移。研究表明，声子极化激元（phonon polaritons）能够在室温下增强能量转移范围，远超传统中红外平台，并具有极端方向性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决传统中红外平台中能量转移范围有限的问题，探索如何将通常严格限制在近场的偶极-偶极相互作用扩展到多个自由空间中红外波长范围之外。

Method: 研究提供了一个理论框架来描述二维双曲材料中的长程能量转移，使用α-MoO₃作为代表性材料进行分析，但该机制适用于整个电磁频谱的各向异性介质。

Result: 研究发现声子极化激元能够介导和增强室温下的能量转移，范围远超传统中红外平台，且具有极端方向性。这是因为偶极-偶极相互作用势能沿实空间双曲开口角的渐近线发散。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了经典和量子偶极相互作用，使其能够超越近场限制，达到多个自由空间中红外波长范围。该机制不仅限于中红外，而是适用于整个电磁频谱的各向异性介质。

Abstract: We provide a framework to theoretically describe long-range energy transfer in single and twisted two-dimensional hyperbolic slabs. We demonstrate that phonon polaritons (PhPs, quantum superpositions of photons and lattice vibrations in polar dielectrics) can mediate and enhance room-temperature energy transfer at ranges far exceeding those of conventional mid-infrared (MIR) platforms, and with extreme directionality. This is because the dipole-dipole interaction potential energy diverges along the asymptotes of the real-space hyperbolic opening angle. Our findings allow us to extend classical and quantum interactions between dipoles, typically strictly confined to the near-field, beyond several free-space MIR wavelengths. We use $α$-MoO$_3$ as a representative material, but this mechanism is not limited to the MIR: it is general to anisotropic media across the whole electromagnetic spectrum.

</details>
